### [1] [Reheating after Starobinsky Inflation in the Jordan Frame](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04497)
*Gláuber C. Dorsch,Luiz Carlos Miranda,Nelson Yokomizo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies gravitational reheating in the Starobinsky $R^2$ inflation model formulated in the Jordan frame, where no inflaton field exists and reheating occurs solely via gravitational particle production from Ricci scalar oscillations. The authors find that the effective background behaves as pressureless matter, particle production is self-consistently damped by backreaction, and they compute a reheating temperature of $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV. They also highlight differences between Jordan and Einstein frame predictions when quantum effects are included.
\n\n
本文研究了在Jordan frame中Starobinsky $R^2$ 暴胀模型中的引力再热过程，该框架下不存在显式的inflaton场，再热完全通过Ricci标量振荡引发的引力粒子产生实现。作者发现有效背景表现为无压物质，粒子产生的backreaction导致Ricci标量振荡指数衰减，从而自洽地终止粒子产生，并计算出再热温度 $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV。文章还指出，当考虑量子效应时，Jordan frame与Einstein frame在微观物理诠释和定量预言上可能存在差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand reheating in modified gravity models like Starobinsky inflation without invoking an inflaton field, focusing on purely gravitational particle production in the Jordan frame. Additionally, the paper aims to clarify how frame choice (Jordan vs. Einstein) affects reheating dynamics once quantum effects—such as particle production and backreaction—are included, despite classical equivalence.
\n\n
动机在于理解在不引入inflaton场的修改引力模型（如Starobinsky暴胀）中如何发生再热，特别关注Jordan frame中纯引力粒子产生机制。此外，文章旨在阐明尽管Jordan frame与Einstein frame在经典层面等价，但在包含量子效应（如粒子产生和backreaction）后，不同frame对再热动力学可能给出不同的描述。

Method: The authors analyze the post-inflationary evolution of the Ricci scalar $R$ in the Jordan frame of the Starobinsky model, treating the $R^2$ term as generating an effective scalar degree of freedom. They derive the effective equation of state during the oscillatory phase and solve the coupled system of background Friedmann equations and Boltzmann equations for gravitationally produced particles, including their backreaction on the spacetime geometry. This backreaction introduces a damping term in the Ricci scalar’s oscillation equation. They also compare results with the Einstein frame formulation.
\n\n
作者分析了Starobinsky模型在Jordan frame中暴胀结束后Ricci标量 $R$ 的演化，将 $R^2$ 项视为产生一个有效标量自由度。他们推导了振荡阶段的有效物态方程，并求解了背景Friedmann方程与引力产生粒子的Boltzmann方程的耦合系统，其中包含了粒子对时空几何的backreaction。该backreaction在Ricci标量振荡方程中引入了阻尼项。作者还与Einstein frame下的结果进行了比较。

Result: The effective fluid from the oscillating $R^2$ gravity mimics pressureless matter ($w \approx 0$). Gravitational particle production leads to exponential damping of Ricci scalar oscillations due to backreaction, self-consistently ending reheating. The computed reheating temperature is $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV. The Jordan and Einstein frames, while classically equivalent, yield different quantitative predictions for reheating when quantum particle production is considered.
\n\n
振荡的 $R^2$ 引力所产生的有效流体模拟无压物质（$w \approx 0$）。引力粒子产生通过backreaction导致Ricci标量振荡指数衰减，从而自洽地终结再热过程。计算得到的再热温度为 $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV。尽管Jordan frame与Einstein frame在经典层面等价，但在考虑量子粒子产生时，两者对再热的定量预言存在差异。

Conclusion: Gravitational reheating in the Jordan frame of the Starobinsky model is a self-consistent process driven by Ricci scalar oscillations, with backreaction playing a crucial role in terminating particle production. The frame dependence of reheating predictions underscores the importance of carefully accounting for quantum effects when comparing physical observables across conformally related frames in modified gravity.
\n\n
在Starobinsky模型的Jordan frame中，引力再热是由Ricci标量振荡驱动的自洽过程，其中backreaction在终止粒子产生中起关键作用。再热预言对frame的依赖性表明，在修改引力理论中比较共形相关frame之间的物理观测量时，必须谨慎处理量子效应。

Abstract: We investigate gravitational reheating in the Starobinsky model in the Jordan frame, where inflation is driven by an $R^2$ modification of gravity with no explicit inflaton field. In this description, reheating proceeds exclusively through gravitational particle production triggered by the oscillations of the Ricci scalar after the end of inflation. We analyze the post-inflationary background evolution and show that an effective fluid emerging from the modified gravitational dynamics behaves as pressureless matter during the oscillatory phase. Including the backreaction of the produced particles, we demonstrate that the Ricci scalar oscillations acquire an exponential damping, consistently terminating particle production. Solving the coupled background and Boltzmann equations, we obtain a reheating temperature $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV. We finally compare the Jordan and Einstein frame descriptions and argue that, although classically equivalent, they can lead to distinct microphysical interpretations and quantitative predictions for reheating once quantum effects are taken into account.

</details>


### [2] [Nonlinear Dynamics in General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04501)
*Vitor Cardoso,Jaime Redondo-Yuste,Ulrich Sperhake,Furkan Tuncer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper reveals new nonlinear phenomena in General Relativity—specifically higher harmonic generation, spectral broadening, and focusing—in the Einstein–Klein–Gordon system. It shows that monochromatic gravitational wave scattering in vacuum at quadratic order exhibits weak frequency dependence at large wavelengths, offering insights into the smoothness of black hole merger waveforms while warning against overly simplistic waveform interpretations.
\n\n
本文揭示了广义相对论中的新非线性现象——具体而言，在Einstein–Klein–Gordon系统中存在高次谐波生成（higher harmonic generation）、谱展宽（spectral broadening）和聚焦效应。文章表明，在真空中，单色引力波在二次阶的散射在长波长下对频率仅有微弱依赖性，这既有助于解释黑洞并合波形看似平滑的行为，也警示我们避免对波形进行过于简化的解读。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While black holes and gravitational waves are well-known consequences of the nonlinearity of Einstein’s equations, the authors argue that other subtle nonlinear effects remain underexplored. Understanding these could clarify features of observed gravitational waveforms from mergers and refine theoretical models beyond linearized gravity or post-Newtonian approximations.
\n\n
尽管黑洞和引力波是爱因斯坦方程非线性的著名结果，作者认为其他微妙的非线性效应仍未被充分探索。理解这些效应有助于澄清来自并合事件的观测波形特征，并改进超越线性化引力或后牛顿近似的理论模型。

Method: The authors analyze the Einstein–Klein–Gordon system perturbatively, working to quadratic order in the gravitational field. They study the scattering of monochromatic gravitational waves in vacuum, examining how nonlinear interactions generate higher harmonics, broaden the spectrum, and induce focusing. The analysis leverages weak-field expansions and asymptotic methods at large wavelengths ($\lambda \to \infty$).
\n\n
作者对Einstein–Klein–Gordon系统进行微扰分析，计算至引力场的二次阶。他们研究真空中单色引力波的散射，考察非线性相互作用如何产生高次谐波、展宽频谱并引发聚焦效应。该分析利用弱场展开和长波长（$\lambda \to \infty$）下的渐近方法。

Result: The study demonstrates that nonlinear interactions in General Relativity lead to higher harmonic generation and spectral broadening even in vacuum. At quadratic order, the scattering amplitude of monochromatic waves is only weakly dependent on frequency for large wavelengths. These effects provide a mechanism for the apparent smoothness in merger waveforms but imply that waveform structure encodes subtle nonlinear physics.
\n\n
研究表明，即使在真空中，广义相对论中的非线性相互作用也会导致高次谐波生成和谱展宽。在二次阶下，单色波的散射振幅在长波长下仅对频率有微弱依赖性。这些效应为并合波形的表观平滑性提供了机制，但也表明波形结构编码了微妙的非线性物理。

Conclusion: The paper establishes that beyond black hole formation and gravitational radiation, General Relativity harbors richer nonlinear dynamics—including harmonic generation and spectral broadening—that influence gravitational wave signatures. This cautions against interpreting merger waveforms through purely linear or quasi-linear models and highlights the need for higher-order nonlinear analyses in waveform modeling.
\n\n
本文确立了除黑洞形成和引力辐射之外，广义相对论还蕴含更丰富的非线性动力学——包括谐波生成和谱展宽——这些会影响引力波信号。这警示我们不要通过纯线性或准线性模型来解读并合波形，并强调在波形建模中需要更高阶的非线性分析。

Abstract: Black holes and gravitational waves are consequences of the nonlinear character of the Einstein equations. Yet, the remarkable properties of General Relativity point to the existence of other effects. Here we uncover new nonlinear facets of gravity. We establish higher harmonic generation, spectral broadening and focusing in the Einstein Klein-Gordon system. In vacuum, we show that scattering of monochromatic waves at quadratic order is weakly sensitive to frequency, at large wavelengths. These aspects can both explain the seemingly smooth behavior of mergers, but also caution us against too simplistic an interpretation of waveforms.

</details>


### [3] [Aspects of Relativity in Flat Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04574)
*C. J. Papachristou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This monograph provides a rigorous mathematical treatment of Special Relativity, emphasizing the structure and representations of the Lorentz group and their applications in relativistic mechanics and electrodynamics. An appendix has been added to the original published book manuscript.
\n\n
本专著对狭义相对论进行了严格的数学处理，重点强调Lorentz群的结构与表示及其在相对论力学和电动力学中的应用。原已出版的书稿新增了一个附录。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to present a mathematically precise foundation for Special Relativity by analyzing the Lorentz group—the symmetry group of Minkowski spacetime—and to clarify how its representation theory underpins physical laws in relativistic mechanics and classical electrodynamics.
\n\n
其动机在于通过分析Lorentz群（即Minkowski时空的对称群）来为狭义相对论提供一个数学上精确的基础，并阐明其表示理论如何支撑相对论力学和经典电动力学中的物理定律。

Method: The paper employs group-theoretic methods, particularly the representation theory of the Lorentz group $SO(1,3)$ and its covering group $SL(2,\\mathbb{C})$, to derive transformation properties of physical quantities such as four-vectors, tensors, and spinors. It also examines the covariance of Maxwell’s equations and the relativistic formulation of particle dynamics.
\n\n
本文采用群论方法，特别是Lorentz群 $SO(1,3)$ 及其覆盖群 $SL(2,\\mathbb{C})$ 的表示理论，推导四维矢量、张量和旋量等物理量的变换性质。同时考察了Maxwell方程的协变性以及粒子动力学的相对论表述。

Result: The monograph rigorously establishes how the Lorentz group governs the form of physical laws in Special Relativity, demonstrating that relativistic invariance constrains the structure of mechanical and electromagnetic theories. The appendix likely extends these results or provides supplementary mathematical tools.
\n\n
该专著严格地确立了Lorentz群如何支配狭义相对论中物理定律的形式，表明相对论不变性约束了力学和电磁理论的结构。附录可能扩展了这些结果或提供了补充的数学工具。

Conclusion: The work underscores the centrality of the Lorentz group in the mathematical formulation of Special Relativity and provides a foundational reference for understanding relativistic symmetries in both classical and quantum contexts.
\n\n
本工作强调了Lorentz群在狭义相对论数学表述中的核心地位，并为理解经典和量子语境下的相对论对称性提供了基础性参考。

Abstract: A monograph on the mathematical aspects of Special Relativity, focusing on the Lorentz group and the properties of relativistic transformations in mechanics and electrodynamics. Manuscript of published book, with an added appendix.

</details>


### [4] [Cosmological black holes in the inflationary epoch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04590)
*Ertola Urtubey Milos,Daniela Pérez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies primordial black holes (PBHs) during inflation that are cosmologically coupled via a generalized McVittie metric, where their mass scales with the scale factor. Within Starobinsky's $\mathcal{R}^2$ inflation model, the authors track PBH evolution through all cosmic epochs, incorporating Hawking evaporation, radiation accretion, and cosmological coupling. Consistency conditions—such as the black hole horizon remaining smaller than the particle horizon and avoidance of runaway accretion—constrain the initial mass window. Only PBHs born in a narrow mass range survive to today, with a maximum present-day mass of $M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$.
\n\n
本文研究了在暴胀时期存在的原初黑洞（PBH），这些黑洞通过广义McVittie度规与宇宙背景动力学耦合，其引力质量随宇宙标度因子缩放。在Starobinsky的$\mathcal{R}^2$暴胀模型框架下，作者追踪了PBH在暴胀、辐射、物质和暗能量时期的演化，综合考虑了宇宙学耦合、Hawking蒸发和辐射吸积效应。通过要求黑洞视界始终小于粒子视界，并避免辐射时期吸积失控，初始质量被严格限制。只有在狭窄初始质量窗口内形成的PBH能存活至今，其当前最大质量为$M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from recent proposals that black holes may be cosmologically coupled, with their masses scaling with the cosmic scale factor—a hypothesis motivated by observations of supermassive black holes and theoretical frameworks like the generalized McVittie solution. The paper aims to test this idea in the context of early-universe physics by examining whether such coupled black holes can survive from inflation to the present day, under the combined influence of Hawking radiation, accretion, and expansion dynamics within a well-motivated inflationary model (Starobinsky $\mathcal{R}^2$).
\n\n
该研究的动机源于近期关于黑洞可能具有宇宙学耦合的假设——即其质量随宇宙标度因子缩放，这一观点受到超大质量黑洞观测及广义McVittie解等理论框架的启发。本文旨在通过检验此类耦合黑洞能否在Starobinsky $\mathcal{R}^2$暴胀模型中，经受Hawking辐射、吸积和宇宙膨胀的共同作用，从暴胀时期存活至今，从而在早期宇宙物理背景下验证该假设。

Method: The authors employ a generalized McVittie geometry to model black holes whose gravitational mass $M(t)$ evolves proportionally to the scale factor $a(t)$, i.e., $M(t) \propto a(t)$. They adopt Starobinsky’s $\mathcal{R}^2$ inflation model to determine the background expansion history. The black hole mass evolution is governed by a differential equation combining three effects: (1) cosmological coupling ($dM/dt \propto H M$), (2) Hawking evaporation ($dM/dt \propto -1/M^2$), and (3) radiation accretion during the radiation-dominated era (using a Bondi-like or similar accretion rate). They impose two key physical constraints: (i) the black hole event horizon $r_s = 2GM/c^2$ must remain smaller than the particle horizon at all times, and (ii) accretion during the radiation era must not lead to unphysical runaway growth. These yield upper and lower bounds on the initial mass at formation during inflation.
\n\n
作者采用广义McVittie几何来描述引力质量$M(t)$随标度因子$a(t)$成比例演化的黑洞，即$M(t) \propto a(t)$。他们使用Starobinsky的$\mathcal{R}^2$暴胀模型确定背景宇宙的膨胀历史。黑洞质量演化由包含三种效应的微分方程控制：(1) 宇宙学耦合（$dM/dt \propto H M$），(2) Hawking蒸发（$dM/dt \propto -1/M^2$），(3) 辐射主导时期的辐射吸积（采用类Bondi吸积率）。他们施加两个关键物理约束：(i) 黑洞事件视界$r_s = 2GM/c^2$必须始终小于粒子视界；(ii) 辐射时期的吸积不能导致非物理的失控增长。这些条件对暴胀时期形成时的初始质量设定了上下限。

Result: The analysis shows that only black holes formed during inflation with an initial mass in a narrow range—bounded below by Hawking evaporation (to avoid complete evaporation before the end of inflation) and above by the requirement that the black hole horizon remains sub-horizon and accretion does not cause runaway growth—can survive to the present epoch. The surviving population peaks at a present-day mass of $M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$, placing them in the planetary-mass range. This result is specific to the Starobinsky $\mathcal{R}^2$ model and the assumed cosmological coupling ansatz.
\n\n
分析表明，只有在暴胀期间形成、且初始质量处于狭窄范围内的黑洞才能存活至今：下限由Hawking蒸发设定（避免在暴胀结束前完全蒸发），上限由黑洞视界必须保持亚视界尺度以及吸积不引发失控增长所决定。幸存黑洞群体的当前质量峰值为$M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$，属于行星质量范围。该结果依赖于Starobinsky $\mathcal{R}^2$模型及所假设的宇宙学耦合形式。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that cosmologically coupled primordial black holes in the context of Starobinsky inflation face stringent survival constraints. Despite the mass-increasing effect of cosmological coupling, the interplay of Hawking evaporation and regulated accretion limits viable initial conditions to a fine-tuned window. The resulting present-day mass is too small to account for dark matter or observed astrophysical black holes, but may have implications for microlensing surveys or exotic compact objects. The work highlights the sensitivity of PBH evolution to both early-universe physics and coupling assumptions.
\n\n
本文得出结论：在Starobinsky暴胀背景下，具有宇宙学耦合的原初黑洞面临严格的存活限制。尽管宇宙学耦合具有增质量效应，但Hawking蒸发与受控吸积的相互作用将可行的初始条件限制在一个精细调节的窗口内。所得当前质量过小，无法解释暗物质或已观测到的天体物理黑洞，但可能对微引力透镜巡天或奇异致密天体研究具有启示意义。该工作凸显了PBH演化对早期宇宙物理及耦合假设的高度敏感性。

Abstract: We investigate the evolution of black holes present during the inflationary epoch, assuming they are dynamically coupled to the cosmological background through a generalized McVittie geometry, such that their gravitational mass scales with the cosmic scale factor. Adopting Starobinsky's $\mathcal{R}^2$ inflation model, we analyse the combined effects of cosmological coupling, Hawking evaporation and radiation accretion during the subsequent cosmic eras: inflation, radiation, matter, and dark energy. Requiring the black hole event horizon to remain smaller than the particle horizon at all times yields an upper bound on the mass parameter. Radiation accretion during the radiation era further constrains the parameter space to prevent runaway growth. Hawking evaporation sets a lower bound on the initial mass to ensure survival through inflation. We find that only black holes formed within a narrow initial mass range during inflation can persist to the present day, reaching a maximum mass of $M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$.

</details>


### [5] [Junction Conditions for General Gravitational Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04645)
*José M. M. Senovilla*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper derives junction conditions for generalized gravity theories with Lagrangians depending on arbitrary functions of curvature scalar invariants (including differential invariants) using distributional methods. It provides a general expression for thin-shell energy-momentum and generalized Israel conditions, showing that the presence or absence of thin shells depends critically on the continuity of higher-order covariant derivatives of the Riemann tensor determined by the highest derivative order $m$ in the Lagrangian. Special behavior is found for $m=0$ quadratic theories (admitting gravitational double layers) and for General Relativity/$F(R)$ theories (allowing curvature shells like impulsive gravitational waves).
\n\n
本文利用分布理论推导了拉格朗日量依赖于曲率标量不变量（包括微分不变量）的任意函数的广义引力理论的连接条件。文章给出了薄壳能量-动量张量的一般表达式和广义Israel条件，表明薄壳的存在与否关键取决于拉格朗日中最高阶导数项 $m$ 所决定的Riemann张量高阶协变导数在匹配超曲面上的连续性。特别地，$m=0$ 的二次理论允许Riemann张量不连续，从而产生薄壳和引力双层结构；而General Relativity和$F(R)$理论则因允许第二基本形式的跃变而支持曲率壳（如脉冲引力波）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to systematically understand how spacetime matching works in generalized gravitational theories beyond General Relativity—particularly those involving higher-order curvature invariants or non-linear functions of curvature scalars—by rigorously applying distributional calculus to derive consistent junction conditions across hypersurfaces, which is essential for modeling thin shells, domain walls, or impulsive gravitational waves in such theories.
\n\n
动机在于系统理解广义引力理论（特别是包含高阶曲率不变量或曲率标量非线性函数的理论）中时空匹配的机制。通过严格应用分布理论推导跨超曲面的一致连接条件，这对于在这些理论中建模薄壳、畴壁或脉冲引力波至关重要。

Method: The authors employ the distributional formalism to handle discontinuities in geometric quantities across a timelike or null matching hypersurface. They consider gravitational actions with Lagrangian densities depending on arbitrary functions of curvature scalar invariants, including up to $m$-th order covariant derivatives of the Riemann tensor. By analyzing the variational principle in the presence of distributional sources, they derive the generalized Israel junction conditions and identify the precise continuity requirements on geometric tensors to avoid thin shells.
\n\n
作者采用分布理论处理匹配超曲面（类时或类光）上几何量的不连续性。他们考虑拉格朗日密度依赖于曲率标量不变量任意函数的引力作用量，其中包含Riemann张量最高至 $m$ 阶协变导数的项。通过分析存在分布源时的变分原理，推导出广义Israel连接条件，并明确指出为避免薄壳所需满足的几何张量连续性条件。

Result: Key results include: (i) thin shells arise if the $m$-th covariant derivative of the Riemann tensor is continuous at the hypersurface; (ii) shell-free matching requires continuity of the $(m+1)$-th derivative; (iii) $m=0$ theories quadratic in curvature invariants uniquely permit Riemann tensor discontinuities, leading to thin shells and gravitational double layers; (iv) General Relativity and $F(R)$ theories are exceptional in allowing curvature shells (e.g., impulsive gravitational waves) because they do not require continuity of the second fundamental form, unlike other higher-derivative theories.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(i) 若Riemann张量的 $m$ 阶协变导数在超曲面上连续，则会出现薄壳；(ii) 无壳匹配要求 $(m+1)$ 阶导数也连续；(iii) $m=0$ 且拉格朗日为曲率不变量二次型的理论是特殊的，唯一允许Riemann张量不连续，从而产生薄壳和引力双层结构；(iv) General Relativity和$F(R)$理论是例外，因其不要求第二基本形式连续，故可支持曲率壳（如脉冲引力波），而其他高阶导数理论则不允许。

Conclusion: The paper establishes a comprehensive framework for junction conditions in broad classes of modified gravity theories, revealing a hierarchy of continuity conditions tied to the derivative order in the Lagrangian. It highlights the unique status of General Relativity, $F(R)$ gravity, and quadratic $m=0$ theories in permitting distributional sources like thin shells or double layers, thereby clarifying which theories can support impulsive gravitational phenomena without violating field equations in a distributional sense.
\n\n
本文为一大类修正引力理论建立了完整的连接条件框架，揭示了连续性条件与拉格朗日中导数阶数之间的层级关系。研究突显了General Relativity、$F(R)$引力和二次型$m=0$理论在允许薄壳或双层等分布源方面的独特地位，从而阐明了哪些理论能在分布意义下支持脉冲引力现象而不违反场方程。

Abstract: The junction conditions for general theories of gravity based on actions that depend on arbitrary functions of the curvature scalar invariants (including differential invariants) are obtained using the distributional formalism. In case of the existence of thin shells, a general expression for the shell energy-momentum is presented. The generalized Israel conditions are also obtained. The conditions for a proper matching, without shells, are also derived. The main results are: (i) shells arise if the $m$th-covariant derivative of the Riemann tensor is continuous at the matching hypersurface, where $m$ is the maximum order appearing in the Lagrangian density; (ii) a proper junction without thin shells requires further that the $(m+1)$-th derivative be also continuous, (iii) theories with $m=0$ that are quadratic in the scalar curvature invariants are special and unique for they allow for discontinuities of the Riemann tensor resulting in the existence of {\em thin shells and gravitational double layers} and (iv) General Relativity and $F(R)$ theories are extraordinary theories that admit shells of curvature (i.e. impulsive gravitational waves) because other theories require the absence of jumps of the second fundamental form across the matching hypersurface. All results are derived for a minimal coupling with the matter, but the strategy would be analogous for more general couplings.

</details>


### [6] [Going into a tailspin near the abyss: analytic solutions for spinning particles on near equatorial, plunging orbits in Kerr spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04682)
*Gabriel Andres Piovano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper provides the first analytic solutions for nearly equatorial plunging trajectories of a spinning test-particle in Kerr spacetime at linear order in the particle's spin. It includes spin-induced orbital plane precession, gives a closed-form correction to the innermost bound circular orbit (IBCO) radius, and proposes a Keplerian-like parametrization for generic plunging orbits.
\n\n
本文首次给出了Kerr时空中近赤道面自旋测试粒子在粒子自旋一阶微扰下的径向 plunge 轨道的解析解。该解包含由粒子自旋进动引起的轨道平面微小进动，以闭合形式给出了最内束缚圆轨道（IBCO）半径的修正，并提出了一种适用于一般plunge轨道的类开普勒参数化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Analytic solutions for spinning-body dynamics in strong-field general relativity are essential for accurate gravitational waveform modeling, especially during the late inspiral and plunge phases near black holes. Existing treatments often neglect spin-induced orbital plane precession or lack closed-form expressions for key quantities like the IBCO radius. This work addresses these gaps for nearly equatorial plunging orbits in Kerr spacetime.
\n\n
强场广义相对论中自旋体动力学的解析解对于精确引力波形建模至关重要，尤其是在黑洞附近的晚期旋进和plunge阶段。现有处理通常忽略自旋诱导的轨道平面进动，或缺乏对IBCO半径等关键量的闭合表达式。本文针对Kerr时空中近赤道面plunge轨道填补了这些空白。

Method: The authors solve the Mathisson–Papapetrou–Dixon (MPD) equations perturbatively at first order in the small-body spin $S$, assuming $E < 1$ (plunging orbits). They account for the spin-curvature coupling and the resulting precession of the orbital plane. A novel parametrization inspired by Keplerian orbital elements is introduced to describe generic non-circular, non-equatorial (but nearly equatorial) plunging geodesics and their spin corrections.
\n\n
作者在小质量体自旋 $S$ 的一阶微扰下求解Mathisson–Papapetrou–Dixon（MPD）方程，假设能量 $E < 1$（对应plunge轨道）。他们考虑了自旋-曲率耦合及其导致的轨道平面进动。文中引入了一种受开普勒轨道根数启发的新参数化方法，用于描述一般的非圆、非赤道（但近赤道）plunge测地线及其自旋修正。

Result: The paper derives explicit analytic expressions for the plunging trajectories including spin-induced precession, computes the first-order-in-spin correction to the innermost bound circular orbit (IBCO) radius in closed form, and constructs a Keplerian-like parametrization that facilitates the description of generic plunging orbits with spin.
\n\n
本文推导了包含自旋诱导进动的plunge轨迹的显式解析表达式，以闭合形式计算了最内束缚圆轨道（IBCO）半径在自旋一阶微扰下的修正，并构建了一种类开普勒参数化方法，便于描述含自旋的一般plunge轨道。

Conclusion: These analytic solutions enhance the theoretical toolkit for modeling extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) and related gravitational waveforms using self-force methods and black hole perturbation theory, particularly during the transition from inspiral to plunge. The inclusion of spin-induced orbital precession and the new parametrization improve waveform accuracy and computational efficiency.
\n\n
这些解析解增强了利用自力（self-force）方法和黑洞微扰理论对极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）及相关引力波形建模的理论工具，特别是在从旋进到plunge的过渡阶段。自旋诱导轨道进动的纳入和新参数化方法提升了波形精度与计算效率。

Abstract: This work presents, the first time, analytic solutions for the nearly equatorial, plunging motion of a spinning test-particle in Kerr spacetime. The equations of motion are solved at first-order in the small-body spin for all classes of plunging orbits with energy $E < 1$. The solutions incorporate the small precession of the orbital plane caused by the precession of the particle's spin. Additionally, we present the correction to the radius of the innermost bound circular orbit in closed form, and introduce a novel, Keplerian-like parametrization for generic plunging orbits. Our solutions will be useful in the modelling of inspiral-merger-ringdown waveforms with self-force methods and black hole perturbation theory.

### [7] [Inflation in fractional Newtonian cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04712)
*S. M. M. Rasouli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper explores early universe cosmology using fractional Newtonian cosmology, demonstrating a non-singular pre-inflationary phase that naturally transitions into inflation. The model identifies a transition time governed by force balance, shows inflation as a stable attractor, links the number of $e$-folds to the fractional parameter $α$ via the near-coincidence of the fractional force zero and the end of inflation, and provides a graceful exit to a standard radiation-dominated era.
\n\n
本文在分数阶牛顿宇宙学（fractional Newtonian cosmology）框架下研究早期宇宙演化，展示了从无奇点的暴胀前阶段自然过渡到暴胀阶段。模型通过力平衡确定了过渡时间，证明暴胀是一个稳定的动力学吸引子，并通过分数阶力零点与暴胀结束时刻的微小偏移，建立了 $e$ 折叠数与分数阶参数 $α$ 之间的可观测一致关系，同时实现了向标准辐射主导时期的优雅退出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to address the initial singularity and fine-tuning issues in standard inflationary cosmology by employing fractional calculus within a Newtonian framework. The authors aim to construct a physically motivated fractional potential that yields a non-singular beginning, a natural onset of inflation, and a graceful exit consistent with standard post-inflationary cosmology.
\n\n
动机在于利用牛顿框架下的分数阶微积分（fractional calculus）解决标准暴胀宇宙学中的初始奇点和精细调节问题。作者旨在构建一个物理上合理的分数阶势（fractional potential），以实现无奇点的宇宙开端、暴胀的自然启动，以及与标准暴胀后宇宙学一致的优雅退出。

Method: The authors formulate a fractional Newtonian cosmology by introducing a fractional gravitational potential, leading to a modified Friedmann-like equation. They analyze the dynamical system defined by the balance between the fractional force and the standard Hubble friction term. Stability analysis around the transition point is performed to identify inflation as an attractor. The zero-crossing of the fractional force is computed and compared to the end of inflation to derive a relation between the number of $e$-folds $N$ and the fractional parameter $α$. The post-inflationary solution is obtained by solving the equations in the limit where the fractional force vanishes.
\n\n
作者通过引入一个分数阶引力势（fractional gravitational potential）来构建分数阶牛顿宇宙学，从而导出修正的类弗里德曼方程（Friedmann-like equation）。他们分析由分数阶力与标准哈勃摩擦项（Hubble friction term）之间平衡所定义的动力学系统，并在过渡点附近进行稳定性分析，以确认暴胀为吸引子。通过计算分数阶力的零点并与暴胀结束时刻比较，推导出 $e$ 折叠数 $N$ 与分数阶参数 $α$ 之间的关系。在分数阶力消失的极限下求解方程，得到暴胀后的解。

Result: The key results are: (1) a non-singular pre-inflationary solution exists; (2) a transition time $t_{\\text{trans}}$ is identified where the fractional force balances the Hubble drag, marking the onset of inflation; (3) the inflationary solution is a stable attractor of the dynamics; (4) the fractional force $F_{\\alpha}$ vanishes at a time $t_0$ very close to the end of inflation $t_{\\text{end}}$, with the small separation $\\Delta t = t_{\\text{end}} - t_0$ yielding the relation $N \\approx \\frac{1}{2(1-\\alpha)}$ for the number of $e$-folds; (5) a graceful exit leads to an exact radiation-dominated solution $a(t) \\propto t^{1/2}$ with an $α$-dependent amplitude.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 存在一个无奇点的暴胀前解；(2) 确定了一个过渡时间 $t_{\\text{trans}}$，此时分数阶力与哈勃阻尼（Hubble drag）平衡，标志着暴胀的开始；(3) 暴胀解是动力学的稳定吸引子；(4) 分数阶力 $F_{\\alpha}$ 在 $t_0$ 时刻为零，该时刻非常接近暴胀结束时刻 $t_{\\text{end}}$，其微小间隔 $\\Delta t = t_{\\text{end}} - t_0$ 导出 $e$ 折叠数关系 $N \\approx \\frac{1}{2(1-\\alpha)}$；(5) 优雅退出机制导向一个精确的辐射主导解 $a(t) \\propto t^{1/2}$，其振幅依赖于 $α$。

Conclusion: Fractional Newtonian cosmology provides a compelling alternative framework that resolves the initial singularity, naturally initiates a stable inflationary phase as a dynamical attractor, and ensures a graceful exit to standard radiation domination. The derived link between the observable number of $e$-folds and the fundamental fractional parameter $α$ offers a testable prediction, making the model phenomenologically viable and theoretically attractive.
\n\n
分数阶牛顿宇宙学提供了一个引人注目的替代框架，能够解决初始奇点问题，自然地将暴胀相作为动力学吸引子启动，并确保向标准辐射主导时期的优雅退出。所导出的可观测 $e$ 折叠数与基本分数阶参数 $α$ 之间的联系提供了可检验的预言，使该模型在现象学上可行且在理论上具有吸引力。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the evolution of the early universe within the framework of fractional Newtonian cosmology. By constructing a suitable fractional potential, we show that the cosmological evolution can naturally originate from a non-singular pre-inflationary regime. We find a natural transition time, separating the pre-inflationary and inflationary regimes, characterized by the balance of the corresponding forces. By analyzing the dynamics near the transition time, we show that the inflationary phase emerges as a stable dynamical attractor. We show that the fractional force vanishes and undergoes a sign change at a point very close to the end of inflation. We then determine the small separation between the force zero point and the end of inflation, and show that it leads to a meaningful relation between the number of $e$-folds and the fractional parameter $α$, ensuring consistency with observations and resolving the horizon problem. Moreover, our results demonstrate the existence of a graceful exit from inflation, followed by an exact radiation-dominated solution with the standard time dependence and an $α$-dependent normalization.

</details>


### [8] [Search for continuous gravitational waves from neutron stars in five globular clusters in the first part of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04792)
*Damon H. T. Cheung,Keith Riles,Rafel Amengual,Preet Baxi,Alicia Calafat,Anamaria Effler,Tabata Aira Ferreira,Evan Goetz,Tom Kimpson,David Keitel,Alan M. Knee,Joan-Rene Merou,Quynh Lan Nguyen,Joseph O'Leary,Ornella J. Piccinni,Alicia M. Sintes,Karl Wette*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper reports on a directed search for continuous gravitational waves from unknown neutron stars in five Milky Way globular clusters using LIGO data from the first eight months of the O4 observing run. No detection was made in the 20–475 Hz band for sources older than 300 years, and the study sets the most stringent upper limits to date, with a median 95% confidence level limit of $\sim 4.2 \times 10^{-26}$ near 282 Hz for NGC 6397.
\n\n
本文报告了利用LIGO在第四次观测运行（O4）前八个月的数据，对银河系五个球状星团中未知中子星的连续引力波进行的定向搜索。在20–475 Hz频段内，对于年龄大于300年的源未发现信号，并设定了迄今为止最严格的上限，在282 Hz附近对NGC 6397的95%置信度中位上限达到$\sim 4.2 \times 10^{-26}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to detect or constrain continuous gravitational wave emission from rapidly spinning, non-axisymmetric neutron stars residing in globular clusters—dense stellar environments where such objects may be abundant but remain electromagnetically undetected. These searches probe extreme physics inaccessible by other means and test general relativity in the strong-field regime.
\n\n
动机在于探测或限制来自球状星团中快速旋转、非轴对称中子星的连续引力波辐射——这些致密恒星环境中可能存在大量此类天体，但尚未被电磁手段探测到。这类搜索可探索其他手段无法触及的极端物理，并在强场条件下检验广义相对论。

Method: The authors employ the WEAVE semi-coherent search pipeline, which aggregates matched-filter detection statistics over numerous short time segments covering the observation period. This method balances computational cost and sensitivity by coherently analyzing data within segments and incoherently combining results across segments. The analysis uses LIGO data from the first eight months of the O4 run and targets five globular clusters, assuming source ages >300 years.
\n\n
作者采用WEAVE半相干搜索流程，该方法在覆盖整个观测时段的多个短时间段内聚合匹配滤波检测统计量。此方法通过在各时间段内进行相干分析、跨时间段非相干组合结果，在计算成本与灵敏度之间取得平衡。分析使用LIGO在O4运行前八个月的数据，针对五个球状星团，假设源年龄>300年。

Result: No statistically significant continuous gravitational wave signal was detected in the 20–475 Hz frequency band. Simulated signal injections demonstrate that the search achieves the highest sensitivity to date over most of the parameter space, with a median 95% confidence upper limit on strain amplitude as low as $\sim 4.2 \times 10^{-26}$ near 282 Hz for the cluster NGC 6397.
\n\n
在20–475 Hz频段内未发现具有统计显著性的连续引力波信号。通过注入模拟信号验证，该搜索在大部分参数空间中达到了迄今最高的灵敏度，对NGC 6397星团在282 Hz附近应变振幅的95%置信度中位上限低至$\sim 4.2 \times 10^{-26}$。

Conclusion: While no detection was made, this work sets the most constraining upper limits on continuous gravitational wave emission from unknown neutron stars in globular clusters to date. The results improve constraints on neutron star ellipticity and internal structure, and demonstrate the advancing capabilities of ground-based detectors in probing persistent gravitational wave sources.
\n\n
尽管未实现探测，但本工作设定了迄今为止对球状星团中未知中子星连续引力波辐射最严格的上限。结果改进了对中子星椭率（ellipticity）和内部结构的约束，并展示了地面探测器在搜寻持续引力波源方面不断提升的能力。

Abstract: We present the results of directed searches for continuous gravitational waves from unknown neutron stars in five Milky Way globular clusters. We carry out the searches in the LIGO data from the first eight months of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run using the WEAVE semi-coherent program, which sums matched-filter detection-statistic values over many time segments spanning the observation period. No gravitational wave signal is detected in the search band of 20-475 Hz for assumed source ages greater than 300 years. Injections of simulated continuous wave signals in the data indicate that we achieve the most sensitive results to date across most of the explored parameter space volume, obtaining median 95% confidence level upper limits as low as $\sim 4.2 \times 10^{-26}$ near 282 Hz for NGC 6397.

</details>


### [9] [Dyonic hairy black holes in $U(1)$ gauge-invariant scalar-vector-tensor theories: Cubic and quartic interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04884)
*Masaki Kitagawa,Naoki Tsukamoto,Ryotaro Kase*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We construct and classify static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically flat hairy black holes in $U(1)$ gauge-invariant scalar-vector-tensor (SVT) theories with both electric and magnetic charges. By including cubic and quartic interactions and imposing a consistency condition to preserve second-order equations of motion, we identify new solution branches activated solely by the magnetic charge. Scalar hair is classified as primary or secondary depending on symmetry, and distinct asymptotic behaviors are found for different couplings. Global regularity is confirmed via matched asymptotic and numerical solutions.
\n\n
我们在具有电荷和磁荷的 $U(1)$ 规范不变标量-矢量-张量（scalar-vector-tensor, SVT）理论中，构造并分类了静态、球对称、渐近平坦的“带毛”黑洞解。通过引入三次和四次相互作用项，并施加一致性条件以保持运动方程为二阶，我们识别出仅由磁荷激活的新解分支。根据对称性，标量毛被分为 primary hair 和 secondary hair，并发现不同耦合下标量场具有不同的渐近衰减行为。通过匹配解析展开与数值积分，验证了解的整体正则性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous studies of hairy black holes in scalar-vector-tensor (SVT) theories focused primarily on electrically charged configurations and quadratic-order interactions. However, the inclusion of magnetic charge introduces new derivative structures that can lead to higher-order equations of motion unless carefully controlled. Moreover, the role of higher-order (cubic and quartic) interaction terms in the presence of magnetic monopoles remains unexplored. This work aims to systematically extend the construction of hairy black hole solutions to include both electric and magnetic charges, clarify the conditions under which the theory remains second-order, and uncover how magnetic charge activates otherwise inert interaction sectors.
\n\n
以往对标量-矢量-张量（SVT）理论中“带毛”黑洞的研究主要集中于电荷构型和二次相互作用项。然而，磁荷的引入会产生新的导数结构，若不加以控制，会导致高阶运动方程。此外，在磁单极存在下，高阶（三次和四次）相互作用项的作用尚未被探索。本文旨在系统地将“带毛”黑洞解的构造扩展到同时包含电荷和磁荷的情形，明确理论保持二阶运动方程的条件，并揭示磁荷如何激活原本在纯电构型中不起作用的相互作用项。

Method: We consider $U(1)$ gauge-invariant SVT theories with general cubic and quartic derivative couplings between the scalar field $\\phi$, the vector field $A_\\mu$, and the metric $g_{\\mu\\nu}$. Assuming static, spherically symmetric, and asymptotically flat spacetime, we impose a purely magnetic ansatz ($Q = 0$, $P \\neq 0$) alongside electric configurations. To avoid Ostrogradsky instabilities, we derive a consistency condition on the quartic coupling function $\\tilde{f}_4(\\phi, X)$ (with $X = -\\frac{1}{2}\\nabla_\\mu\\phi\\nabla^\\mu\\phi$) that cancels dangerous higher-derivative terms induced by the magnetic field. We then solve the resulting second-order field equations analytically near the horizon and at infinity, and match these expansions with numerical integration to construct global solutions. The symmetry properties of the coupling functions—specifically whether they are shift-symmetric ($\\phi \\to \\phi + c$) or explicitly $\\phi$-dependent—determine the nature of the scalar hair.
\n\n
我们考虑具有标量场 $\\phi$、矢量场 $A_\\mu$ 和度规 $g_{\\mu\\nu}$ 之间一般三次和四次导数耦合的 $U(1)$ 规范不变 SVT 理论。假设时空是静态、球对称且渐近平坦的，我们同时考虑纯磁构型（$Q = 0$, $P \\neq 0$）和电构型。为避免 Ostrogradsky 不稳定性，我们对四次耦合函数 $\\tilde{f}_4(\\phi, X)$（其中 $X = -\\frac{1}{2}\\nabla_\\mu\\phi\\nabla^\\mu\\phi$）推导出一个一致性条件，以抵消由磁场诱导的危险高阶导数项。随后，我们在视界附近和无穷远处解析求解所得的二阶场方程，并通过数值积分匹配这些展开式以构建全局解。耦合函数的对称性质——特别是是否具有平移对称性（$\\phi \\to \\phi + c$）或显含 $\\phi$——决定了标量毛的类型。

Result: We find that the magnetic charge $P$ enables new interaction channels: specifically, the cubic coupling $\\tilde{f}_3$ contributes to the field equations only when $P \\neq 0$, and vanishes identically in purely electric cases. We identify solution branches that exist only for $P \\neq 0$ and disappear in the limit $P \\to 0$, demonstrating the essential role of magnetic charge. Scalar hair is classified into two types: (i) secondary hair, arising from shift-symmetric couplings and tied to a conserved Noether current, and (ii) primary hair, generated by explicit $\\phi$-dependence in the Lagrangian. The asymptotic decay of the scalar field differs between these types: e.g., $\\phi(r) \\sim 1/r$ for secondary hair versus $\\phi(r) \\sim 1/r^k$ ($k > 1$) for certain primary hair configurations. All solutions are globally regular, as confirmed by smooth matching of near-horizon and asymptotic expansions with numerical profiles.
\n\n
我们发现磁荷 $P$ 开启了新的相互作用通道：具体而言，三次耦合 $\\tilde{f}_3$ 仅在 $P \\neq 0$ 时对场方程有贡献，在纯电情形下恒为零。我们识别出仅在 $P \\neq 0$ 时存在的解分支，且在 $P \\to 0$ 极限下消失，表明磁荷的关键作用。标量毛分为两类：(i) secondary hair，源于平移对称耦合，与守恒的 Noether 流相关；(ii) primary hair，由拉格朗日量中显含 $\\phi$ 的项产生。这两类标量毛的渐近衰减行为不同：例如，secondary hair 满足 $\\phi(r) \\sim 1/r$，而某些 primary hair 构型满足 $\\phi(r) \\sim 1/r^k$（$k > 1$）。所有解均整体正则，这通过视界附近与无穷远展开式与数值解的光滑匹配得到验证。

Conclusion: Magnetic charge is not merely a passive parameter but actively reshapes the landscape of hairy black hole solutions in SVT theories. It activates otherwise dormant interaction terms (e.g., $\\tilde{f}_3$), enforces nontrivial consistency conditions on higher-order operators, and gives rise to solution branches with no electric counterpart. The distinction between primary and secondary hair, governed by internal symmetries, leads to observable differences in asymptotic scalar profiles. This work establishes a systematic framework for constructing healthy (second-order) hairy black holes with dyonic charges and highlights the indispensable role of magnetic monopoles in generalized gravity theories.
\n\n
磁荷不仅是被动参数，而是主动重塑了 SVT 理论中“带毛”黑洞解的结构。它激活了原本休眠的相互作用项（如 $\\tilde{f}_3$），对高阶算子施加非平凡的一致性条件，并产生没有电对应物的解分支。由内禀对称性决定的 primary hair 与 secondary hair 之分，导致标量场渐近轮廓的可观测差异。本工作为构造具有双荷（dyonic）的健康（二阶）“带毛”黑洞建立了一个系统框架，并突显了磁单极在广义引力理论中的不可或缺作用。

Abstract: We construct and classify asymptotically flat, static, spherically symmetric hairy black hole solutions in $U(1)$ gauge-invariant scalar-vector-tensor (SVT) theories carrying both electric and magnetic charges. Extending previous studies beyond the quadratic sector, we systematically incorporate cubic and quartic interaction terms in the presence of the magnetic charge. We derive a consistency condition for the quartic interaction that eliminates higher-order derivative terms induced by the magnetic charge, ensuring the theory remains second-order. We classify the obtained solutions based on their symmetry properties: shift-symmetric couplings yield secondary hair governed by the Noether current, whereas $φ$-dependent interactions generate primary hair. Crucially, our analysis reveals that the magnetic charge plays a key role in activating specific interaction sectors such as the cubic coupling $\tilde{f}_3$, which does not appear in the field equations in purely electric configurations. We identify solution branches that are intrinsic to the magnetic charge, as they cease to exist in the vanishing monopole limit ($P\to 0$). Furthermore, we demonstrate that the scalar hair exhibits distinct asymptotic decay rates depending on the interaction type, suggesting possible variations in observational signatures. Finally, we verify the global regularity of these solutions by connecting analytic expansions with numerical integration.

</details>


### [10] [A loop quantization of the marginally bound Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi dust model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04995)
*Luca Cafaro,Farshid Soltani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a loop quantization of the marginally bound Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi (LTB) model for spherically symmetric gravitational collapse of pressureless dust. By modeling the system as non-interacting shells with individual loop quantum dynamics, the authors demonstrate that quantum effects resolve the classical central singularity via a bounce at Planckian densities. They also compare this loop quantum gravity (LQG) approach with Wheeler-DeWitt quantization and find that interference patterns in wave packets near the bounce reduce the accuracy of the LQG effective theory close to the cloud center.
\n\n
本文提出了一种对边际束缚的Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi（LTB）模型的圈量子化方法，用于描述无压尘埃在球对称下的引力坍缩。通过将系统建模为具有独立圈量子动力学的非相互作用壳层，作者证明了量子效应通过在Planck密度处的反弹解决了经典中心奇点问题。他们还将此圈量子引力（LQG）方法与Wheeler-DeWitt量子化进行了比较，并发现波包在反弹附近产生的干涉图样会降低LQG有效理论在尘埃云中心附近的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The classical LTB model predicts a curvature singularity during gravitational collapse, signaling a breakdown of general relativity. Loop Quantum Gravity (LQG) offers a potential resolution through quantum geometry effects that may replace singularities with bounces. This work aims to construct a full quantum LTB model using loop quantization, investigate whether the singularity is resolved, and evaluate the reliability of the commonly used effective dynamics in capturing the full quantum behavior—particularly in inhomogeneous settings where shell interactions are absent but spatial gradients matter.
\n\n
经典的LTB模型在引力坍缩过程中预言了曲率奇点，表明广义相对论在此失效。圈量子引力（LQG）通过量子几何效应可能以反弹取代奇点，从而提供一种解决方案。本研究旨在利用圈量子化方法构建完整的量子LTB模型，探究奇点是否被解决，并评估常用的有效动力学在捕捉完整量子行为方面的可靠性——特别是在无壳层相互作用但存在空间梯度的非均匀情形中。

Method: The authors decompose the marginally bound LTB spacetime into a continuum of non-interacting spherical shells, each treated as an independent symmetry-reduced system. Each shell is quantized using loop quantum cosmology (LQC)-inspired techniques, employing holonomy corrections derived from the full LQG framework. The quantum Hamiltonian constraint for each shell is solved numerically to evolve Gaussian wave packets initially peaked on classical collapsing trajectories. The full quantum LTB solution is then assembled by stacking these single-shell evolutions. Additionally, the Wheeler-DeWitt equation for the same single-shell model is solved for comparison, and the loop quantum effective dynamics—based on a modified Friedmann equation with $\\rho_{\\text{crit}}$—is tested against the full quantum evolution.
\n\n
作者将边际束缚的LTB时空分解为一系列非相互作用的球形壳层，每个壳层被视为一个独立的对称性约化系统。每个壳层采用受圈量子宇宙学（LQC）启发的技术进行量子化，使用源自完整LQG框架的holonomy修正。通过数值求解每个壳层的量子Hamilton约束，演化初始时局域在经典坍缩轨迹上的高斯波包。完整的量子LTB解通过堆叠这些单壳层演化而构建。此外，还求解了相同单壳层模型的Wheeler-DeWitt方程以作比较，并将基于修正Friedmann方程（含$\\rho_{\\text{crit}}$）的圈量子有效动力学与完整量子演化进行对比测试。

Result: The single-shell loop quantum dynamics is non-singular: collapsing wave packets bounce at energy densities near the Planck scale ($\\rho \\sim 0.41 \\rho_{\\text{Pl}}$) and transition smoothly to expansion. However, during the bounce, wave packets develop significant interference fringes due to the superposition of pre- and post-bounce components. This interference is most pronounced near the center of the dust cloud (small shell radii), where the effective loop quantum theory—which assumes a single semiclassical trajectory—fails to accurately reproduce the full quantum evolution. In contrast, the Wheeler-DeWitt quantization does not yield a bounce and retains the singularity, highlighting a key difference between the two quantum approaches.
\n\n
单壳层圈量子动力学是非奇异的：坍缩波包在接近Planck尺度的能量密度（$\\rho \\sim 0.41 \\rho_{\\text{Pl}}$）处发生反弹，并平滑过渡到膨胀阶段。然而，在反弹过程中，由于反弹前后成分的叠加，波包产生显著的干涉条纹。这种干涉在尘埃云中心附近（小壳层半径处）最为明显，而圈量子有效理论——假设单一的半经典轨迹——在此区域无法准确复现完整量子演化。相比之下，Wheeler-DeWitt量子化未产生反弹，仍保留奇点，凸显了两种量子方法的关键差异。

Conclusion: Loop quantum gravity successfully resolves the central singularity in the LTB collapse model through a quantum bounce, confirming the robustness of singularity resolution in inhomogeneous settings within LQG. However, the emergence of quantum interference near the bounce implies that the standard effective dynamics, while useful in homogeneous cosmologies, may be insufficient for accurately describing the deep quantum regime in inhomogeneous models—especially near symmetry centers. This underscores the necessity of full quantum treatments when studying Planck-scale physics in gravitational collapse.
\n\n
圈量子引力通过量子反弹成功解决了LTB坍缩模型中的中心奇点，证实了LQG在非均匀背景下奇点消除的鲁棒性。然而，反弹附近出现的量子干涉表明，标准有效动力学虽在均匀宇宙学中有用，但在非均匀模型的深度量子区域（尤其在对称中心附近）可能不足以准确描述物理过程。这强调了在研究引力坍缩中的Planck尺度物理时，必须采用完整的量子处理方法。

Abstract: We present a loop quantization of the marginally bound Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi (LTB) model, describing the gravitational collapse of pressureless dust in spherical symmetry. The full quantum LTB model is constructed as a collection of non-interacting shells, each governed by an individual single-shell loop quantum dynamics. We show that the single-shell evolution is non-singular and that wave packets initially peaked on a collapsing trajectory undergo a bounce at Planckian energy densities and subsequently follow an expanding classical trajectory, resolving the classical central curvature singularity. We also compare the loop quantum theory with the Wheeler-DeWitt quantization of the same model and assess the accuracy of the loop quantum gravity effective theory in reproducing the full quantum dynamics. Specifically, we find that initially collapsing wave packets generically develop an interference pattern at the bounce, which suppresses the accuracy of the effective theory near the center of the dust cloud.

</details>


### [11] [Observational and Thermodynamic aspects of one-dimensional Dark Energy EoS parametrization models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05009)
*Anirban Chatterjee,Yungui Gong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the Gong-Zhang (GZ) dark energy equation-of-state parametrizations—GZ-Type I and GZ-Type II—using only late-time cosmological data (SNe Ia, BAO, and $H(z)$). It finds that both models are competitive with $Λ$CDM, with GZ-Type II preferred due to lower parameter degeneracy and stronger Bayesian evidence. Additionally, configuration entropy is introduced as a thermodynamic probe of structure formation, showing sensitivity to dynamical dark energy effects on late-time clustering while preserving early-universe consistency.
\n\n
本文利用仅限于晚期宇宙学探针（Ia型超新星、BAO和$H(z)$）研究了Gong-Zhang（GZ）暗能量状态方程参数化模型——GZ-Type I 和 GZ-Type II。结果表明，两种模型均与$Λ$CDM具有竞争力，其中GZ-Type II因更低的参数简并性和更强的贝叶斯证据而被优先支持。此外，文章引入构型熵（configuration entropy）作为结构形成的热力学探针，证明其对动力学暗能量在晚期引力聚团中的影响高度敏感，同时保持早期宇宙行为的标准性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test whether the Gong-Zhang dark energy parametrizations—designed to be physically transparent and avoid unphysical divergences—can serve as viable alternatives to the standard $Λ$CDM model using only late-time observational data. Additionally, the authors aim to go beyond background expansion by introducing a thermodynamically grounded diagnostic (configuration entropy) to assess how dynamical dark energy affects structure formation.
\n\n
动机在于检验Gong-Zhang暗能量参数化模型（设计上具有物理透明性且避免非物理解发散）是否能仅通过晚期观测数据成为标准$Λ$CDM模型的可行替代方案。此外，作者希望超越背景膨胀测试，引入一个基于热力学的诊断量（构型熵），以评估动力学暗能量如何影响结构形成。

Method: The authors constrain the GZ-Type I and GZ-Type II models using Bayesian inference applied to late-time datasets: Type Ia supernovae (Union3, Pantheon+SH0ES, DES-SN5YR), DESI baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), and cosmic chronometer $H(z)$ measurements. Model comparison is performed via information criteria (e.g., Jeffreys scale). To probe structure formation, they compute the configuration entropy production rate, defined from the matter density field, as a thermodynamic measure sensitive to gravitational clustering under dynamical dark energy.
\n\n
作者采用贝叶斯推断方法，利用晚期宇宙学数据集（Ia型超新星Union3、Pantheon+SH0ES、DES-SN5YR；DESI重子声学振荡BAO；以及宇宙计时器$H(z)$测量）对GZ-Type I和GZ-Type II模型进行约束。模型比较通过信息准则（如Jeffreys尺度）完成。为探测结构形成，他们从物质密度场出发计算构型熵产生率，将其作为对动力学暗能量下引力聚团敏感的热力学度量。

Result: Both GZ parametrizations are statistically competitive with $Λ$CDM, but GZ-Type II is consistently favored across datasets due to reduced parameter degeneracy and higher Bayesian evidence. The configuration entropy production rate shows clear sensitivity to the dynamics of dark energy at late times, distinguishing the GZ models from $Λ$CDM in their impact on structure growth, while maintaining agreement with standard early-universe physics.
\n\n
两种GZ参数化模型在统计上均与$Λ$CDM具有竞争力，但GZ-Type II在所有数据集中均被一致偏好，因其参数简并性更低且贝叶斯证据更强。构型熵产生率对晚期暗能量动力学表现出明显敏感性，能够区分GZ模型与$Λ$CDM在结构增长上的差异，同时保持与标准早期宇宙物理的一致性。

Conclusion: The Gong-Zhang framework provides a physically well-motivated and observationally viable extension of $Λ$CDM. The GZ-Type II model emerges as a particularly promising alternative, and the use of configuration entropy offers a novel, thermodynamically grounded tool to probe the influence of dynamical dark energy on cosmic structure formation beyond background expansion.
\n\n
Gong-Zhang框架为$Λ$CDM提供了一个物理动机清晰且观测上可行的扩展。其中GZ-Type II模型尤为突出，而构型熵的引入则提供了一种新颖且基于热力学的工具，用于探测动力学暗能量对宇宙结构形成的效应，超越了仅依赖背景膨胀的传统方法。

Abstract: We examine the observational viability and physical implications of the Gong-Zhang (GZ) dark--energy equation-of-state parametrizations using exclusively late-time cosmological probes. Two one-dimensional parametrization models, GZ-Type~I and GZ-Type~II, are constrained with Type~Ia supernovae (Union3, Pantheon+SH0ES, and DES-SN5YR), DESI baryon acoustic oscillations, and cosmic chronometer measurements of $H(z)$. Bayesian inference combined with information-criteria diagnostics shows that both parametrizations provide competitive alternatives to $Λ$CDM, while the GZ-Type~II model is consistently favored, exhibiting reduced parameter degeneracy and stronger Jeffreys-scale support. Beyond background expansion tests, we employ configuration entropy as a thermodynamically motivated probe of structure formation. We demonstrate that the entropy-production rate sensitively traces the impact of dynamical dark energy on late-time gravitational clustering while preserving standard early-time behavior. Our results establish the Gong-Zhang framework as a physically transparent and observationally consistent extension of $Λ$CDM, with configuration entropy providing a complementary diagnostic of late-time cosmic acceleration.

### [12] [Strong breaking of black-hole uniqueness from coexisting scalarization mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05064)
*Astrid Eichhorn,Pedro G. S. Fernandes,Lidia Marino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates a strong violation of black-hole uniqueness in a modified gravity theory with a cubic scalar-Gauss-Bonnet coupling, where multiple distinct black-hole branches coexist and exhibit both continuous and discontinuous phase transitions at high spin.
\n\n
本文展示了一种在具有立方标量-高斯-博内特（Gauss-Bonnet）耦合的修正引力理论中黑洞唯一性（black-hole uniqueness）的强烈破缺：在高自旋下，多个不同的黑洞解分支共存，并表现出连续与不连续的相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Black-hole uniqueness theorems in General Relativity assert that stationary vacuum black holes are uniquely described by the Kerr metric. However, in theories beyond General Relativity, this uniqueness may fail. The authors aim to explore whether such breaking can be "strong"—i.e., multiple distinct black-hole solutions coexist for the same physical parameters—particularly in scalar-tensor theories with higher-curvature couplings.
\n\n
广义相对论中的黑洞唯一性定理断言，稳态真空黑洞可唯一由Kerr度规描述。然而，在广义相对论之外的理论中，这种唯一性可能失效。作者旨在探索这种破缺是否可以是“强”的——即对于相同的物理参数，存在多个不同的黑洞解——特别是在具有高曲率耦合的标量-张量理论中。

Method: The authors consider a scalar-tensor theory featuring a cubic coupling between a scalar field $\\phi$ and the Gauss-Bonnet invariant $\\mathcal{G}$, i.e., an interaction term $\\sim \\phi^3 \\mathcal{G}$. They analyze the non-linear instability of the Kerr solution under this coupling, which triggers spontaneous scalarization. By solving the field equations numerically for rotating black holes, they map out the phase diagram in the parameter space of spin and coupling strength, identifying distinct branches of scalarized black-hole solutions.
\n\n
作者考虑一种标量-张量理论，其中标量场 $\\phi$ 与高斯-博内特不变量 $\\mathcal{G}$ 之间存在立方耦合，即相互作用项 $\\sim \\phi^3 \\mathcal{G}$。他们分析了在此耦合下Kerr解的非线性不稳定性，该不稳定性触发了自发标量化（spontaneous scalarization）。通过数值求解旋转黑洞的场方程，他们在自旋与耦合强度的参数空间中绘制出相图，识别出不同的标量化黑洞解分支。

Result: At large black-hole spin, two scalarization mechanisms—curvature-induced and spin-induced—compete when the coupling constant has a fixed sign. This competition leads to a rich phase structure with multiple coexisting black-hole branches. The transitions between these branches can be either continuous (second-order) or discontinuous (first-order), indicating a complex thermodynamic landscape beyond General Relativity.
\n\n
在大黑洞自旋下，当耦合常数符号固定时，曲率诱导（curvature-induced）与自旋诱导（spin-induced）两种标量化机制相互竞争。这种竞争导致了丰富的相结构，其中多个黑洞解分支共存。这些分支之间的转变可以是连续的（二阶）或不连续的（一阶），表明在广义相对论之外存在复杂的热力学景观。

Conclusion: The study provides a concrete example of strong black-hole uniqueness violation in a theoretically consistent modified gravity model. The coexistence of multiple black-hole solutions and the presence of both continuous and discontinuous phase transitions highlight the complexity of black-hole physics beyond General Relativity and have implications for gravitational-wave tests of fundamental gravity.
\n\n
本研究在一个理论上自洽的修正引力模型中给出了黑洞唯一性强破缺的具体范例。多个黑洞解的共存以及连续与不连续相变的存在，凸显了广义相对论之外黑洞物理的复杂性，并对引力波检验基础引力理论具有重要意义。

Abstract: Black-hole uniqueness, i.e., the statement that all stationary vacuum black holes in the universe are described by the Kerr solution, is expected to break in theories beyond General Relativity. This breaking can take a particularly strong form, if several branches of black-hole solutions beyond the Kerr solution coexist. We find an example of a theory that exhibits such strong breaking. In this theory, a cubic coupling of a scalar field to the Gauss-Bonnet invariant triggers black-hole scalarization through a non-linear instability of the Kerr solution. At large spin, curvature-induced and spin-induced scalarization mechanisms compete at fixed sign of the coupling. This results in a rich phase structure of black-hole solutions and continuous as well as discontinuous transitions between the different branches of black holes.
