### [13] [External magnetic field influence on massive binary black hole inspiral gravitational waves and its similarity with environmental effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05084)
*Xulong Yuan,Xiangdong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates how external magnetic fields around massive black holes—modeled by Bertotti-Robinson and Bonnor-Melvin spacetimes—imprint distinctive signatures in gravitational waveforms via the parametrized post-Einsteinian (ppE) framework. The leading-order magnetic corrections appear at $-2$ PN (Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson) and $-3$ PN (Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin), which are distinguishable from modified gravity but degenerate with certain matter distributions.
\n\n
本文研究了外部磁场（通过Bertotti-Robinson和Bonnor-Melvin时空建模）如何在引力波形中留下特征印记，采用parametrized post-Einsteinian (ppE)框架进行分析。磁场所致的主导阶修正分别出现在$-2$ PN（Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson）和$-3$ PN（Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin）阶，这些修正可与modified gravity效应区分，但与特定物质分布存在简并。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to disentangle environmental effects—such as external magnetic fields—from genuine deviations from General Relativity in gravitational wave (GW) observations. Massive black holes at galactic centers are expected to reside in magnetized environments, and their influence on inspiraling compact objects may mimic or obscure signatures of new physics. Clarifying the unique GW imprints of magnetic fields is essential for accurate interpretation of future LISA-like observations.
\n\n
动机源于需要在引力波（GW）观测中将环境效应（如外部磁场）与广义相对论的真实偏离区分开来。位于星系中心的大质量黑洞被认为处于磁化环境中，其对旋近致密天体的影响可能模仿或掩盖新物理的信号。明确磁场在GW中的独特印记对于准确解读未来LISA类观测至关重要。

Method: The authors employ the parametrized post-Einsteinian (ppE) formalism to compute frequency-domain gravitational waveforms for extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) into Kerr black holes immersed in external magnetic fields—specifically, the Bertotti-Robinson and Bonnor-Melvin solutions. They perform a post-Newtonian (PN) expansion of the orbital dynamics and waveform phase, isolating corrections due to the magnetic field and black hole spin. The resulting ppE parameters are then compared against known environmental (e.g., accretion disks) and modified gravity templates to assess degeneracies.
\n\n
作者采用parametrized post-Einsteinian (ppE)形式体系，计算极端质量比旋近（EMRIs）进入嵌入外部磁场中的Kerr黑洞（具体为Bertotti-Robinson和Bonnor-Melvin解）所产生的频域引力波形。他们对轨道动力学和波形相位进行post-Newtonian (PN)展开，分离出由磁场和黑洞自旋引起的修正项，并将所得ppE参数与已知的环境（如吸积盘）及modified gravity模板进行比较，以评估简并性。

Result: For a Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) black hole, the leading magnetic correction enters at $-2$ PN order, with a subleading spin-induced term at $-1.5$ PN. For a Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin (KBM) black hole, the leading magnetic correction is at $-3$ PN, while the spin contribution remains at $-1.5$ PN. These magnetic ppE corrections are not degenerate with typical modified gravity effects but mimic the gravitational influence of surrounding matter with power-law density profiles: $\\gamma = 1$ for KBR and $\\gamma = 0$ for KBM.
\n\n
对于Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR)黑洞，主导的磁修正出现在$-2$ PN阶，次主导的自旋诱导项在$-1.5$ PN阶。对于Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin (KBM)黑洞，主导磁修正出现在$-3$ PN阶，而自旋贡献仍为$-1.5$ PN阶。这些磁性ppE修正与典型的modified gravity效应不简并，但会模拟周围物质的引力影响——其密度呈幂律分布：KBR对应$\\gamma = 1$，KBM对应$\\gamma = 0$。

Conclusion: Future gravitational wave detectors like LISA will be sensitive to negative PN-order corrections, enabling the detection of environmental effects such as magnetic fields or matter distributions around massive black holes. However, distinguishing between magnetic fields and specific matter profiles ($\\gamma = 0$ or $1$) will require additional observational handles or multi-messenger data, as their ppE signatures are degenerate. Crucially, these magnetic imprints do not mimic modified gravity, preserving the robustness of tests of General Relativity in magnetized environments.
\n\n
未来的引力波探测器（如LISA）将对负PN阶修正敏感，从而能够探测大质量黑洞周围的环境效应，如磁场或物质分布。然而，由于磁场与特定物质分布（$\\gamma = 0$或$1$）的ppE信号存在简并，要区分二者需依赖额外的观测约束或多信使数据。关键的是，这些磁印记不会模仿modified gravity效应，从而在磁化环境中仍能稳健地检验广义相对论。

Abstract: Magnetic fields represent a critical component of astrophysical research, laying the foundation for interpreting high-energy astrophysical activity across galactic scales. In this work, we investigate the parametrized post-Einsteinian (ppE) waveform imprints induced by the external magnetic fields of Bertotti-Robinson and Bonnor-Melvin black holes, with the aim of distinguishing such magnetic effects from environmental influences--particularly for massive black holes posited to reside at galactic centers. We first compute the ppE frequency-domain waveform for a small black hole inspiraling into a massive Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) black hole, which corresponds to a Kerr black hole embedded in an external magnetic field. We find that the leading-order correction arising from the magnetic field is at the $-2$ post-Newtonian (PN) order relative to the quadrupole term, while the next-leading-order correction is at $-1.5$ PN, originating from the spin of the black hole. We further examine the effects of a spinning Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin (KBM) black hole, whose leading-order magnetic correction is at $-3$ PN (consistent with the preceding result), whereas its spin-induced correction is also at $-1.5$ PN. The leading-order ppE corrections for both KBR and KBM black holes do not appear degenerate with any modified theory of gravity effects; nonetheless, we demonstrate that they resemble the gravitational pull contributions from additional matter with power-law distributions of index $γ=1$ and $γ=0$, respectively. As a result, future gravitational wave (GW) observations detecting $-3$ or $-2$ PN order corrections will infer their origin as either magnetic field effects or matter environmental influences.

</details>


### [14] [Double-sphere enhanced optomechanical spectroscopy constrains symmetron dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05090)
*Jiawei Li,Ka-Di Zhu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper proposes an optomechanical experimental setup using two optically levitated nanospheres in a cavity to detect symmetron-mediated fifth forces. The induced coupling shifts the resonance spectrum, enabling constraints on symmetron parameters in the $μ\sim 10^{-2}$–$10^{-4}$ eV range, improving current laboratory bounds by several orders of magnitude.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于腔内两个光学悬浮纳米球的光机实验方案，用于探测对称子（symmetron）介导的第五力。该相互作用诱导的有效耦合会导致光机共振谱的可测分裂，从而在 $μ\sim 10^{-2}$–$10^{-4}$ eV 范围内对对称子参数施加限制，比现有实验室界限提升数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Screened scalar fields like the symmetron are theoretically well-motivated dark energy candidates that evade traditional detection due to screening mechanisms. Laboratory tests for such fifth forces are extremely challenging, necessitating novel high-precision approaches that can probe screened interactions at microscopic scales.
\n\n
对称子等屏蔽标量场是理论上合理的暗能量候选者，但由于屏蔽机制（screening mechanisms）的存在，传统探测手段难以发现它们。对此类第五力的实验室检验极具挑战性，亟需发展能够在微观尺度上探测屏蔽相互作用的新颖高精度方法。

Method: The authors employ an optomechanical system consisting of two optically levitated nanospheres within an optical cavity. The symmetron field mediates a Yukawa-like interaction between the spheres, generating an effective position-dependent coupling. This coupling modifies the normal modes of the system, leading to a resolvable splitting in the optomechanical resonance spectrum, which can be measured with high precision.
\n\n
作者采用一个由光学腔内两个光学悬浮纳米球组成的光机系统。对称子场在两球之间介导一种类 Yukawa 相互作用，产生有效的位置依赖耦合。该耦合改变系统的正则模，导致光机共振谱中出现可分辨的分裂，可通过高精度测量加以探测。

Result: The proposed setup forecasts sensitivity to symmetron parameters in the mass range $μ\sim 10^{-2}$–$10^{-4}$ eV, improving existing laboratory constraints by up to several orders of magnitude. The measurable resonance splitting provides a direct signature of the symmetron-mediated fifth force.
\n\n
所提出的方案预计可在质量范围 $μ\sim 10^{-2}$–$10^{-4}$ eV 内对对称子参数具有灵敏度，将现有实验室限制提升多达数个数量级。可测的共振分裂为对称子介导的第五力提供了直接信号。

Conclusion: Optomechanical spectroscopy with levitated nanoparticles offers a powerful new avenue for probing screened scalar fields like the symmetron. This approach significantly enhances laboratory sensitivity to fifth forces and demonstrates the potential of quantum optomechanical systems in fundamental physics tests.
\n\n
利用悬浮纳米粒子的光机光谱学为探测对称子等屏蔽标量场提供了一条强有力的新途径。该方法显著提升了实验室对第五力的灵敏度，展示了量子光机系统在基础物理检验中的潜力。

Abstract: Screened scalar fields such as the symmetron provide a viable description of dark energy yet their laboratory detection remains challenging. We propose an optomechanical scheme to constrain symmetron interactions using two optically levitated nanospheres inside a cavity. The symmetron-mediated interaction induces an effective coupling which leads to a measurable splitting in the optomechanical resonance spectrum. We forecast constraints in the regime $μ\sim 10^{-2}$eV-$10^{-4}$ eV, which shows that this approach can improve existing laboratory bounds by up to several orders of magnitude, demonstrating the sensitivity of optomechanical spectroscopy to screened fifth forces.

</details>


### [15] [New Improved Schwarzschild Black Hole and Its Thermodynamics and Topological Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05130)
*G. Alencar,T. M. Crispim,C. R. Muniz,M. Nilton*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We construct a renormalization-group (RG) improved Schwarzschild black hole using an exact running Newton coupling, yielding a regular de Sitter core at short distances and recovering classical Schwarzschild geometry at large distances. Quantum corrections induce a remnant and nontrivial thermodynamic phase structure, while topological analysis shows the global topological charge remains unchanged despite shifts in the critical point.
\n\n
我们利用精确的跑动牛顿耦合构建了一个重整化群（RG）改进的史瓦西黑洞，该解在短距离处呈现规则的类德西特核心，在长距离处恢复经典史瓦西几何。量子修正导致残余态和非平凡的热力学相结构，而拓扑分析表明，尽管临界点发生偏移，全局拓扑荷仍保持不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The classical Schwarzschild black hole contains a curvature singularity at $r=0$, which signals a breakdown of general relativity. Asymptotic Safety in quantum gravity suggests that gravitational couplings run with energy scale, potentially resolving such singularities. The motivation is to implement this idea via a consistent RG-improvement scheme that interpolates between ultraviolet (UV) fixed-point behavior and infrared (IR) classical gravity, thereby constructing a nonsingular black hole geometry with well-defined thermodynamics and topology.
\n\n
经典史瓦西黑洞在 $r=0$ 处存在曲率奇点，表明广义相对论在此失效。量子引力中的渐近安全（Asymptotic Safety）理论指出引力耦合随能标跑动，可能消除此类奇点。本文动机在于通过一个自洽的重整化群改进方案，将紫外（UV）不动点行为与红外（IR）经典引力平滑连接，从而构建一个无奇点的黑洞几何，并具有明确定义的热力学与拓扑性质。

Method: The authors employ the exact running Newton coupling $G(k)$ derived from the functional renormalization group within the Asymptotic Safety scenario. A proper-distance-based interpolating function $k(r)$ is used to identify the RG scale $k$ with the spacetime coordinate $r$, ensuring smooth transition between UV and IR regimes. This yields a coordinate-dependent effective coupling $G(r) = G(k(r))$, which is substituted into the Schwarzschild metric ansatz to obtain the improved line element $ds^2 = -f(r)dt^2 + f(r)^{-1}dr^2 + r^2 d\Omega^2$, where $f(r) = 1 - 2G(r)M/r$. Thermodynamic quantities (temperature, entropy, heat capacity) are computed from $f(r)$, and the phase space topology is analyzed via the Euler characteristic or similar topological invariants.
\n\n
作者采用来自泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）在渐近安全框架下导出的精确跑动牛顿耦合 $G(k)$。通过基于固有距离的插值函数 $k(r)$ 将重整化群标度 $k$ 与时空坐标 $r$ 关联，确保紫外与红外区域之间的平滑过渡。由此得到坐标依赖的有效耦合 $G(r) = G(k(r))$，并将其代入史瓦西度规假设，获得改进的线元 $ds^2 = -f(r)dt^2 + f(r)^{-1}dr^2 + r^2 d\Omega^2$，其中 $f(r) = 1 - 2G(r)M/r$。热力学量（温度、熵、热容）由 $f(r)$ 计算得出，并通过欧拉示性数或其他拓扑不变量对相空间进行拓扑分析。

Result: The improved metric function $f(r)$ asymptotes to the classical Schwarzschild form as $r \to \infty$, while near $r \to 0$ it approaches $f(r) \approx 1 - (\Lambda_{\text{eff}}/3) r^2$, indicating a regular de Sitter core with effective cosmological constant $\Lambda_{\text{eff}}$. The black hole temperature vanishes at a finite radius, implying the existence of a stable remnant. The heat capacity exhibits sign changes, revealing a nontrivial phase structure with possible first- or second-order transitions. Topological classification shows the thermodynamic phase space retains the same global topological number as the classical Schwarzschild solution, though the critical point is shifted by asymptotically safe quantum corrections.
\n\n
改进的度规函数 $f(r)$ 在 $r \to \infty$ 时趋近于经典史瓦西形式，而在 $r \to 0$ 附近表现为 $f(r) \approx 1 - (\Lambda_{\text{eff}}/3) r^2$，表明存在一个具有有效宇宙学常数 $\Lambda_{\text{eff}}$ 的规则类德西特核心。黑洞温度在有限半径处趋于零，暗示存在稳定残余态。热容出现符号变化，揭示了包含可能一级或二级相变的非平凡相结构。拓扑分类表明，尽管渐近安全量子修正使临界点发生偏移，热力学相空间仍保持与经典史瓦西解相同的全局拓扑数。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that incorporating Asymptotic Safety via RG-improvement yields a nonsingular black hole geometry with physically meaningful thermodynamics. The resolution of the central singularity into a de Sitter core, the emergence of a remnant, and the preservation of global topology underscore the robustness of the Asymptotic Safety paradigm in addressing fundamental issues in black hole physics.
\n\n
本工作表明，通过重整化群改进引入渐近安全机制可得到一个无奇点的黑洞几何，其热力学具有物理意义。中心奇点被规则化为德西特核心、残余态的出现以及全局拓扑的保持，凸显了渐近安全范式在解决黑洞物理基本问题方面的稳健性。

Abstract: We construct a renormalization-group improved Schwarzschild-like black hole geometry using the exact new scheme running for the Newton coupling. The scale identification is implemented via a standard interpolating proper-distance function that smoothly connects the ultraviolet and infrared regimes. We present the resulting coordinate-dependent coupling and the improved metric function, analyzing its asymptotic expansions. The large-distance limit is shown to recover the classical Schwarzschild solution, while the short-distance behavior exhibits a regular de Sitter-like core, demonstrating the regularization of the central singularity. We also analyze the thermodynamic properties of the solution, showing that quantum corrections significantly modify the small-radius behavior, leading to a remnant configuration and a nontrivial phase structure. Finally, we perform a topological classification of the thermodynamic phase space and demonstrate that asymptotically safe effects shift the critical point while preserving the global topological number of the Schwarzschild solution.

</details>


### [16] [Accretion Disk Perturbations and Their Effects on Kerr Black Hole Superradiance and Gravitational Atom Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05182)
*Ruiheng Li,Zhong-hao Luo,Zehong Wang,Fa Peng Huang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates how accretion disk gravity perturbs the energy levels and couplings of bosonic states in Kerr black hole superradiance, showing that disk-induced tidal fields can suppress, quench, or enhance superradiant growth via state mixing and level shifts, thereby critically affecting gravitational-wave signatures of ultralight bosons.
\n\n
本文研究了吸积盘引力如何扰动Kerr黑洞超辐射中玻色子态的能级和耦合，表明盘诱导的潮汐场可通过态混合与能级移动来抑制、淬灭或增强超辐射增长，从而显著影响超轻玻色子的引力波信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Realistic astrophysical environments around spinning black holes include accretion disks whose gravitational fields can perturb the hydrogen-like energy levels of boson clouds formed via superradiance. Ignoring these environmental effects may lead to inaccurate predictions for superradiant instability rates and gravitational-wave signals, limiting the reliability of using BH superradiance as a probe of ultralight bosons and dark matter.
\n\n
在现实天体物理环境中，旋转黑洞周围存在吸积盘，其引力场会扰动通过超辐射形成的玻色子云的类氢能级。忽略这些环境效应可能导致对超辐射不稳定性增长率和引力波信号的预测不准确，从而限制了利用黑洞超辐射探测超轻玻色子和暗物质的可靠性。

Method: The authors model the accretion disk as a weak external gravitational perturbation expanded in multipoles. They focus on the $n=2$ subspace $\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$ of the bosonic cloud and derive an effective three-level Hamiltonian in the weak-coupling regime. Symmetry considerations (axisymmetry, equatorial reflection) determine selection rules for couplings induced by disk multipoles: quadrupolar ($\ell_d=2$) tidal fields dominate, with $m_d=0$ causing diagonal energy shifts, $m_d=\pm2$ enabling $\Delta m = \pm 2$ mixing between $\ket{211}$ and $\ket{21-1}$, and breaking of equatorial symmetry allowing $\Delta m = \pm 1$ transitions involving $\ket{210}$. Two illustrative scenarios are analyzed: a transient $m=2$ spiral density wave and a quasi-static warp.
\n\n
作者将吸积盘建模为弱外部引力扰动，并以多极展开形式处理。他们聚焦于玻色子云的$n=2$子空间$\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$，并在弱耦合极限下推导出一个有效三能级哈密顿量。通过对称性分析（轴对称性、赤道反射对称性）确定由盘多极矩诱导的耦合选择定则：四极（$\ell_d=2$）潮汐场占主导地位，其中$m_d=0$项引起对角能级移动，$m_d=\pm2$项导致$\ket{211}$与$\ket{21-1}$之间的$\Delta m = \pm 2$混合，而赤道对称性破缺则允许涉及$\ket{210}$的$\Delta m = \pm 1$跃迁。文中分析了两种典型情形：瞬态$m=2$螺旋密度波和准静态翘曲。

Result: The leading-order disk perturbation is the quadrupolar tidal field. A transient equatorial $m=2$ spiral wave couples $\ket{211}$ and $\ket{21-1}$, forming a two-level system that can suppress or quench superradiance by transferring population to a decaying mode. A quasi-static warp breaks more symmetries, inducing full three-level mixing and creating narrow ``growth gaps'' near accidental near-degeneracies where superradiant growth is temporarily halted; conversely, static reshuffling of mode weights can also enhance growth if amplitude concentrates in the unstable mode.
\n\n
主导阶的盘扰动是四极潮汐场。瞬态赤道$m=2$螺旋波耦合$\ket{211}$与$\ket{21-1}$，形成二能级系统，可通过将粒子数转移至衰减模式来抑制或淬灭超辐射。准静态翘曲破坏更多对称性，引发完整的三能级混合，并在偶然近简并点附近产生狭窄的“增长间隙”，暂时中止超辐射增长；反之，若模式权重的静态重分布使振幅集中于不稳定模式，则可增强增长。

Conclusion: Accretion disk gravity is not a negligible environmental effect but a key factor that can qualitatively alter the dynamics of black hole superradiance through symmetry-breaking perturbations. Accurate modeling of such disk-induced couplings and level shifts is essential for reliable predictions of boson cloud evolution and gravitational-wave detectability of ultralight particles in realistic astrophysical systems.
\n\n
吸积盘引力并非可忽略的环境效应，而是通过对称性破缺扰动定性改变黑洞超辐射动力学的关键因素。要可靠预测玻色子云演化及超轻粒子在真实天体物理系统中的引力波可探测性，必须精确建模此类盘诱导的耦合与能级移动。

Abstract: Kerr black hole (BH) superradiance can form gravitational atoms and produce characteristic gravitational-wave signals, providing a probe of ultralight bosons and dark matter. In realistic systems, accretion-disk gravity can shift energy levels and mix states, modifying the effective superradiant growth. We model the disk as a weak external perturbation via a multipole expansion and derive an effective three-level Hamiltonian for the $n=2$ subspace $\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$ in the weak-coupling regime. The leading disk effect is the quadrupolar ($\ell_d=2$) tidal field, whose symmetries fix the selection rules: axisymmetry gives only diagonal shifts, equatorial nonaxisymmetry activates $Δm=\pm2$ mixing ($\ket{211}\leftrightarrow\ket{21-1}$), and breaking equatorial reflection opens $Δm=\pm1$ couplings involving $\ket{210}$. As illustrations, a transient equatorial $m=2$ spiral wave drives the resulting two-level system and can suppress or quench superradiance by populating a decaying mode, while a quasi-static warp produces full three-level mixing and can generate narrow ``growth gaps'' near accidental near-degeneracies, with the same static reshuffling also allowing enhancement when weight shifts toward the growing mode. These findings demonstrate that accretion disk perturbations are a crucial environmental factor in determining the dynamics of BH superradiance and the evolution of boson clouds, thereby providing a more reliable theoretical basis for assessing the detectability of ultralight bosons in realistic astrophysical settings.

</details>


### [17] [Can Light Cross a Singularity? Exact Solutions from Analogue Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05285)
*Juan Manuel Paez,Franco Fiorini,Santiago M. Hernández*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates electromagnetic fields in a spacetime with a strong curvature naked singularity using an analogue gravity model, finding exact regular solutions to both electrostatic and electrodynamic equations, some of which allow bounded power flux through the singularity.
\n\n
该论文利用类比引力模型研究了具有强曲率裸奇点的时空中的电磁场，找到了静电和电动力学方程的精确正则解，其中某些解允许有限的功率通量穿过奇点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the unresolved physical behavior of classical fields near naked singularities—spacetime regions where general relativity predicts infinite curvature without an event horizon. Understanding whether physical fields like electromagnetism can remain regular or transmit energy across such singularities tests the limits of classical field theory and may inform quantum gravity or cosmic censorship conjectures.
\n\n
动机源于经典场在裸奇点附近物理行为的未解之谜——广义相对论预言的无事件视界的无限曲率时空区域。理解电磁场等物理场是否能在这种奇点附近保持正则性或传输能量，可检验经典场论的极限，并可能为量子引力或宇宙监督猜想提供启示。

Method: The authors employ an analogue gravity framework, mapping the electromagnetic field equations onto a tractable effective spacetime geometry that hosts a strong curvature naked singularity. They solve the full Maxwell equations (both electrostatic and time-dependent) in this background, imposing regularity conditions at the singularity and analyzing the resulting power flux via the Poynting vector $\\mathbf{S} = \\frac{1}{\\mu_0} \\mathbf{E} \\times \\mathbf{B}$.
\n\n
作者采用类比引力（analogue gravity）框架，将电磁场方程映射到一个具有强曲率裸奇点的可处理的有效时空几何中。他们在该背景下求解完整的麦克斯韦方程组（包括静电和含时情形），在奇点处施加正则性条件，并通过坡印廷矢量 $\\mathbf{S} = \\frac{1}{\\mu_0} \\mathbf{E} \\times \\mathbf{B}$ 分析所得的功率通量。

Result: Exact analytical solutions to the Maxwell equations are obtained that remain finite and smooth at the naked singularity. Notably, certain dynamical solutions exhibit a regular and bounded Poynting vector, implying that electromagnetic energy can propagate through the singularity without divergence.
\n\n
获得了在裸奇点处保持有限且光滑的麦克斯韦方程组的精确解析解。值得注意的是，某些动力学解展现出正则且有界的坡印廷矢量，表明电磁能量可在无发散的情况下穿过奇点传播。

Conclusion: The results challenge the conventional view that naked singularities necessarily disrupt physical field propagation, demonstrating that electromagnetic fields can remain well-behaved and transmit energy across such extreme geometries within classical theory. This suggests that not all naked singularities are pathological from a field-theoretic perspective.
\n\n
结果挑战了裸奇点必然破坏物理场传播的传统观点，表明在经典理论框架内，电磁场可在这种极端几何中保持良好行为并传输能量。这说明从场论角度看，并非所有裸奇点都是病态的。

Abstract: Using a simple spacetime hosting a strong curvature naked singularity, we employ an analogue gravity model to study electromagnetic fields in this background. We find exact solutions to the full set of electrostatic and electrodynamic equations that remain regular even in the presence of the singularity. Moreover, certain solutions sustain a regular and bounded power flux across the singularity, suggesting that electromagnetic energy may be transmitted through it.

</details>

# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [18] [Quantum field theories with many fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04481)
*Ludo Fraser-Taliente*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This thesis explores large-$N$ melonic quantum field theories (QFTs)—including SYK-like models, tensor models, and vector models—using the large-$N$ limit to access strongly-coupled regimes. It introduces $\tilde{F}$-extremization as a solution method for infrared conformal fixed points, demonstrates its application in a quartic Yukawa tensor model across continuous dimensions, and reveals universal features such as fixed-point multiplicity, stability, and operator spectra consistent between large-$N$ and $\\epsilon$-expansion approaches.
\n\n
本论文研究大$N$梅洛尼克量子场论（QFT）——包括SYK类模型、张量模型和矢量模型——利用大$N$极限探索强耦合物理。文中提出$\tilde{F}$-极值化方法求解红外共形不动点，并在连续维度下的四次Yukawa张量模型中加以应用，揭示了此类理论的普适特征：不动点的多重性、稳定性以及算符谱，且大$N$展开与$\epsilon$-展开结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand strongly-coupled quantum field theories, which are generally non-perturbative and analytically intractable. The large-$N$ limit offers a controlled approximation where simplifications occur due to dominance of melonic diagrams, enabling exact solutions. Melonic QFTs—including Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK)-like models, tensor models, and certain vector models—exhibit solvable infrared conformal fixed points, making them ideal laboratories for studying non-perturbative phenomena such as emergent conformality, operator spectra, and renormalization group flows.
\n\n
动机在于理解强耦合量子场论，这类理论通常是非微扰且难以解析处理的。大$N$极限提供了一种可控近似，其中梅洛尼克图（melonic diagrams）主导，从而实现精确求解。梅洛尼克QFT——包括Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）类模型、张量模型和某些矢量模型——展现出可解的红外共形不动点，使其成为研究非微扰现象（如涌现共形性、算符谱和重整化群流）的理想平台。

Method: The paper employs the large-$N$ expansion in melonic QFTs, focusing on the simplification of Feynman diagrams to melonic dominance. It introduces $\tilde{F}$-extremization: a variational principle where the infrared CFT is determined by extremizing $\tilde{F}$ (the universal part of the free energy on a sphere) subject to constraints from interactions. This method bypasses traditional beta-function computations. The approach is illustrated using two solvable toy models (a 0D theory and a generalized free field flow) and then applied to a quartic Yukawa tensor model in continuous spacetime dimension $d$, solved via large-$N$ techniques and matched with dimensional ($\\epsilon = d_{\\text{crit}} - d$) expansion results.
\n\n
本文采用梅洛尼克QFT中的大$N$展开，聚焦于费曼图简化为梅洛尼克主导的情形。文中提出$\tilde{F}$-极值化方法：一种变分原理，其中红外CFT通过在相互作用约束下对$\tilde{F}$（球面上自由能的普适部分）进行极值化来确定。该方法绕过了传统的β函数计算。作者首先用两个可解玩具模型（零维理论和广义自由场流）阐明此方法，随后将其应用于连续时空维度$d$下的四次Yukawa张量模型，通过大$N$技术求解，并与维度展开（$\epsilon = d_{\text{crit}} - d$）结果进行匹配。

Result: The key results include: (1) formulation of $\tilde{F}$-extremization as a general solution method for large-$N$ melonic CFTs; (2) explicit solution of the quartic Yukawa tensor model in continuous $d$, revealing multiple interacting infrared fixed points; (3) analysis of their stability under RG flow; (4) computation of the operator spectrum (scaling dimensions and OPE data); and (5) quantitative agreement between large-$N$ and dimensional expansion predictions, confirming universality of melonic CFT features.
\n\n
主要结果包括：(1) 提出$\tilde{F}$-极值化作为大$N$梅洛尼克CFT的一般求解方法；(2) 在连续维度$d$下显式求解四次Yukawa张量模型，揭示多个相互作用的红外不动点；(3) 分析这些不动点在重整化群流下的稳定性；(4) 计算算符谱（标度维度和OPE数据）；(5) 大$N$展开与维度展开的预测在定量上一致，证实了梅洛尼克CFT特征的普适性。

Conclusion: Melonic large-$N$ QFTs constitute a solvable class of strongly-coupled theories whose infrared physics is governed by extremization of $\tilde{F}$ under simple interaction constraints. Their fixed-point structure, stability, and spectral data exhibit universal behavior accessible through both large-$N$ and $\\epsilon$-expansion methods. This framework provides a powerful analytic handle on non-perturbative dynamics and opens avenues for exploring connections to holography, quantum chaos, and critical phenomena beyond conventional Wilson-Fisher paradigms.
\n\n
梅洛尼克大$N$ QFT构成一类可解的强耦合理论，其红外物理由在简单相互作用约束下对$\tilde{F}$的极值化所支配。其不动点结构、稳定性及谱数据展现出普适行为，可通过大$N$展开和$\epsilon$-展开两种方法获得。该框架为非微扰动力学提供了强有力的解析工具，并为探索与全息对偶、量子混沌及超越传统Wilson-Fisher范式的临界现象之间的联系开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The large-$N$ quantum field theories provide a window into the regime of strongly-coupled physics. Our principal object of study in this thesis is the large-$N$ family of melonic QFTs, which contain the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev-like models, tensor models, and vector models. We begin with a review of this limit of a large number of degrees of freedom (large-$N$) as an approach to the solution of QFTs. Two toy models are used to clarify this approach: a zero-dimensional field theory and the flow of a generalized free field theory. Both models are solvable, and so we can explicitly demonstrate: using the former, the simplifications at large $N$; using the latter, the tools used to study scale-dependence of physics -- the renormalization group. We develop $\tilde{F}$-extremization, a simple method of solution for an arbitrary large-$N$ melonic QFT in its strongly-coupled limit. The infrared conformal field theories show remarkable simplicity, in that they are entirely solved by the requirement that they have as many degrees of freedom as possible, up to a simple constraint arising from the interaction between the fields. We measure the number of degrees of freedom of the conformal infrared theory via $\tilde{F}$, the universal part of the free energy. We then present the example of the quartic Yukawa model in continuous dimension. This model is considered as a tensor field theory, and solved for its conformal limit; we then illustrate its multiplicity of fixed points and their stability, as well as its operator spectrum, matching the data between the large-$N$ and dimensional expansions. These features reflect general characteristics of melonic conformal field theories: their existence, stability, and spectral characteristics. We conclude with future directions of exploration for the melonic theories.

</details>


### [19] [Higher-Spin and Higher-Point Constraints on Stringy Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04485)
*Ivano Basile,Grant N. Remmen,Georgina Staudt*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper uses multiparticle factorization and soft kinematics to constrain possible deformations of tree-level open string and superstring amplitudes. It shows that the Regge intercept is uniquely fixed by seven-point factorization, matching bosonic string theory, and proves that certain satellite deformations of four-point superstring amplitudes are ruled out by unitarity due to the infinite higher-spin tower.
\n\n
本文利用多粒子因子化和软运动学来约束树图级开弦和超弦振幅的可能形变。研究表明，通过七点因子化可以唯一确定Regge截距，与玻色弦理论一致，并证明由于无限高自旋塔的存在，某些四点超弦振幅的卫星形变被幺正性排除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to test the rigidity of string theory amplitudes against deformations that preserve basic physical principles like unitarity and factorization. Specifically, the authors aim to understand whether the structure of string amplitudes—particularly the Regge behavior and the spectrum of higher-spin states—is uniquely determined by consistency conditions, reinforcing the idea that string theory is highly constrained compared to effective field theories with finite particle content.
\n\n
动机在于检验弦理论振幅在保持幺正性和因子化等基本物理原理的前提下对形变的刚性。作者特别希望理解弦振幅的结构（尤其是Regge行为和高自旋态谱）是否由一致性条件唯一确定，从而强化“相比具有有限粒子内容的有效场论，弦理论受到更强约束”这一观点。

Method: The authors apply multiparticle factorization constraints to Koba-Nielsen-type amplitudes under minimal degeneracy assumptions up to the second excited level, using seven-point amplitudes to fix the Regge intercept $\\alpha(0)$. For superstrings, they consider massless external states and arbitrary spectral degeneracy, employing soft kinematics in the large-level limit to derive multipositivity bounds. These bounds are then applied to satellite deformations in the Gross family of amplitudes to test compatibility with unitarity.
\n\n
作者在最小简并度假设下（直至第二激发能级），对Koba-Nielsen型振幅应用多粒子因子化约束，利用七点振幅固定Regge截距$\\alpha(0)$。对于超弦，他们考虑无质量外态和任意谱简并度，在大能级极限下采用软运动学推导出多重正定性（multipositivity）界，并将这些界应用于Gross振幅族中的卫星形变，以检验其是否满足幺正性。

Result: The Regge intercept for all Koba-Nielsen-type amplitudes is uniquely fixed to $\\alpha(0)=1$, matching the bosonic string, via seven-point factorization. Novel constraints on worldsheet integrand deformations are derived. In the superstring case, multipositivity bounds at leading and subleading orders in the large-level expansion rule out the simplest factorizable satellite deformation of four-point amplitudes, demonstrating that such deformations violate unitarity when the full infinite tower of higher-spin states is included.
\n\n
通过七点因子化，所有Koba-Nielsen型振幅的Regge截距被唯一确定为$\\alpha(0)=1$，与玻色弦一致。同时推导出对世界面积分元形变的新约束。在超弦情形中，大能级展开的领头阶和次领头阶多重正定性界排除了四点振幅中最简单的可因子化卫星形变，表明当包含完整的无限高自旋塔时，此类形变违反幺正性。

Conclusion: The results confirm that string amplitudes are exceptionally rigid: their structure, including the Regge trajectory and the infinite higher-spin spectrum, cannot be deformed without violating fundamental consistency conditions like unitarity and factorization. This supports the folklore that string theory’s infinite tower of higher-spin states imposes far stronger constraints than any finite-species effective theory.
\n\n
结果证实弦振幅具有极强的刚性：其结构（包括Regge轨迹和无限高自旋谱）无法在不破坏幺正性和因子化等基本一致性条件的情况下进行形变。这支持了“弦理论的无限高自旋塔所施加的约束远强于任何有限物种有效理论”的传统观点。

Abstract: We employ multiparticle factorization to constrain deformations of tree-level open string amplitudes. Assuming minimal degeneracy among intermediate states of the same spin up through the second excited level, we find that the Regge intercept among all amplitudes of the Koba-Nielsen type can be uniquely fixed using seven-point factorization, precisely matching the bosonic string. Moreover, we produce novel constraints on deformations of the worldsheet integrand. We then turn to deformations of superstrings, with massless external states and arbitrary spectral degeneracy, using soft kinematics. Accounting for the infinite tower of higher-spin resonances, we obtain novel multipositivity bounds to leading and subleading order in the large-level limit. We apply these bounds to the simplest factorizable satellite deformation in the family of amplitudes found by Gross, showing that any deformation of four-point string amplitudes of this type is forbidden by unitarity. Our results reinforce the folklore that the higher-spin tower of string excitations is dramatically more rigid than any finite number of species.

### [20] [Nonabelian Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture and Monopole Confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04494)
*Matthew Reece,Tom Rudelius*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates violations of the Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture (LWGC) in heterotic string compactifications, confirming that such violations are accompanied by fractionally charged confined monopoles and are constrained by the structure of the gauge group's center.
\n\n
本文研究了杂化弦紧致化中Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture (LWGC) 的破坏情形，证实此类破坏总是伴随着分数电荷的禁闭磁单极子，并且受到规范群中心结构的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from recent counterexamples to the LWGC, which challenges the universality of this quantum gravity conjecture. A hypothesis was proposed that LWGC violation is always associated with fractionally charged confined monopoles. The authors aim to test this hypothesis in explicit string theory constructions—specifically, toroidal orbifold compactifications of the heterotic string—which are known to violate LWGC in both abelian and nonabelian sectors.
\n\n
动机源于近期发现的LWGC反例，这对该量子引力猜想的普适性提出了挑战。此前有假设认为，LWGC的破坏必然伴随分数电荷的禁闭磁单极子。作者旨在通过具体的弦论构造——即杂化弦的环面轨形紧致化（已知在abelian和nonabelian规范扇区均破坏LWGC）——来检验这一假设。

Method: The authors analyze toroidal orbifold compactifications of the heterotic string, focusing on the structure of the gauge group $G$ and its center $Z(G)$. They identify a discrete subgroup $K \subseteq Z(G)$ such that the quotient group $G/K$ admits a consistent charge lattice where superextremal particles populate every electric site, while confined monopoles occupy every magnetic site. This involves examining the electric and magnetic charge lattices $\\Gamma$ and their relation to the center of the gauge group, leveraging properties of orbifold projections and heterotic string spectra.
\n\n
作者分析杂化弦的环面轨形紧致化，聚焦于规范群 $G$ 及其中心 $Z(G)$ 的结构。他们识别出一个离散子群 $K \subseteq Z(G)$，使得商群 $G/K$ 具有一个自洽的电荷格点：超极端粒子占据所有电荷格点，而禁闭磁单极子占据所有磁荷格点。该方法涉及考察电荷格点 $\\Gamma$ 与磁荷格点及其与规范群中心的关系，并利用轨形投影和杂化弦谱的性质。

Result: In all examined cases of LWGC violation in heterotic orbifolds, there exists a subgroup $K \subseteq Z(G)$ such that the LWGC holds for the quotient gauge group $G/K$, with superextremal particles at every electric lattice site and confined monopoles at every dual magnetic lattice site. This confirms the hypothesis linking LWGC violation to fractionally charged confined monopoles and reveals that LWGC violation cannot occur if $Z(G)$ is trivial. Moreover, the extent of violation is bounded by the maximal order of elements in $Z(G)$.
\n\n
在所有考察的杂化轨形LWGC破坏情形中，均存在子群 $K \subseteq Z(G)$，使得商规范群 $G/K$ 满足LWGC：超极端粒子出现在每个电荷格点，禁闭磁单极子出现在对偶磁荷格点。这证实了LWGC破坏与分数电荷禁闭磁单极子之间的关联，并揭示若 $Z(G)$ 平凡则LWGC破坏不可能发生。此外，破坏程度受 $Z(G)$ 中元素最大阶数的限制。

Conclusion: The study establishes a refined understanding of LWGC violation: it is not arbitrary but tightly controlled by the global structure of the gauge group, specifically its center. The presence of fractionally charged confined monopoles is a necessary feature of such violations, and theories with trivial gauge centers automatically satisfy the LWGC. This provides a structural criterion for when the LWGC can fail in quantum gravity.
\n\n
本研究建立了对LWGC破坏的更精细理解：其并非任意，而是由规范群的整体结构（特别是其中心）严格控制。分数电荷禁闭磁单极子的存在是此类破坏的必要特征，而具有平凡规范中心的理论自动满足LWGC。这为量子引力中LWGC何时可能失效提供了结构性判据。

Abstract: Within the known landscape of quantum gravity, most theories satisfy the Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture (LWGC), which requires a superextremal particle at every site in the electric charge lattice $Γ$. However, counterexamples to the LWGC exist, and it was recently hypothesized that such counterexamples necessarily feature fractionally charged confined monopoles. In this work, we verify this hypothesis in toroidal orbifold compactifications of the heterotic string, which notably feature LWGC violation in both the abelian and nonabelian gauge sectors. In all the cases we consider, there exists a discrete subgroup of the center of the gauge group $K \subseteq Z(G)$ such that superextremal particles exist at every site in the charge lattice of the quotient group $G/K$, while (confined) monopoles exist at all sites in the magnetic charge lattice of $G/K$. This suggests that LWGC violation cannot occur for gauge groups with trivial centers, and more generally the degree of LWGC violation in a nonabelian gauge theory is bounded in terms of the maximal order of the center.

</details>


### [21] [From BPS geodesics to mode-driven dynamics in the scattering of multiple BPS vortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04495)
*Alberto Alonso-Izquierdo,Maximilian Bachmaier,Andrzej Wereszczynski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates how exciting a massive bound mode in the Abelian-Higgs model at critical coupling modifies geodesic motion in vortex scattering. While symmetric BPS geodesics remain formally unchanged, generic collisions (e.g., 1–2 or 2–2 vortices) deviate significantly from BPS predictions due to mode-generated forces, increasing chaos in final-state formation.
\n\n
本文研究了在临界耦合的Abelian-Higgs模型中，激发一个重束缚模如何改变涡旋散射中的测地线运动。尽管对称的BPS测地线在形式上保持不变，但一般的碰撞（例如1–2或2–2涡旋）由于模产生的力而显著偏离BPS预测，从而增强了末态形成的混沌行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand the dynamics of vortex scattering beyond the moduli space approximation (MSA), particularly when internal massive modes are excited. At critical coupling, the BPS sector provides exact static solutions, but time-dependent processes like collisions may involve non-BPS effects from mode excitations that alter trajectories and induce chaos.
\n\n
动机是理解超越模空间近似（moduli space approximation, MSA）的涡旋散射动力学，特别是在激发内禀重模的情况下。在临界耦合下，BPS扇区提供精确的静态解，但碰撞等含时过程可能涉及来自模激发的非BPS效应，从而改变轨迹并诱发混沌。

Method: The authors analyze geodesic motion on the moduli space of the 3- and 4-vortex sectors in the Abelian-Higgs model at critical coupling, incorporating corrections due to the excitation of a massive bound mode. They compute the mode-generated force, defined as $F_i = -\\partial_i \\omega$, where $\\omega$ is the frequency of the bound mode varying along the geodesic, and study its impact on vortex trajectories in specific scattering setups (e.g., head-on 1–2 and 2–2 collisions).
\n\n
作者分析了临界耦合下Abelian-Higgs模型中3涡旋和4涡旋扇区的模空间上的测地线运动，并引入重束缚模激发带来的修正。他们计算了模产生的力，定义为 $F_i = -\\partial_i \\omega$，其中 $\\omega$ 是沿测地线变化的束缚模频率，并研究其对特定散射构型（如正碰的1–2和2–2涡旋）中涡旋轨迹的影响。

Result: The study finds that BPS geodesics with enhanced symmetry (e.g., rotational or reflection symmetry) are invariant under mode excitation, though the actual direction of motion depends on the mode-generated force. In contrast, generic asymmetric collisions exhibit strong deviations from BPS geodesics, leading to more complex and chaotic final states.
\n\n
研究发现，具有增强对称性（如旋转或反射对称性）的BPS测地线在模激发下保持不变，尽管实际运动方向依赖于模产生的力。相比之下，一般的非对称碰撞表现出对BPS测地线的强烈偏离，导致更复杂且混沌的末态。

Conclusion: Excitation of massive internal modes introduces non-geodesic corrections to vortex dynamics even at critical coupling, challenging the strict validity of the moduli space approximation for time-dependent processes. The resulting mode-generated forces can significantly alter scattering outcomes and enhance chaos, especially in multi-vortex systems without high symmetry.
\n\n
重内禀模的激发即使在临界耦合下也会引入对涡旋动力学的非测地修正，这对模空间近似在含时过程中的严格有效性提出了挑战。由此产生的模产生的力可显著改变散射结果并增强混沌，尤其在缺乏高对称性的多涡旋系统中。

Abstract: We analyze how the geodesic motion in the 3- and 4-vortex sectors of the Abelian-Higgs model at critical coupling is deformed by the excitation of a massive bound mode. We find that the geodesics corresponding to BPS solutions with enhanced symmetry remain unchanged, although the direction of the actual motion depends on the mode-generated force, i.e., a force arising from the change of the mode frequency along the geodesic. In a generic case, for example in head-on collisions between the axially symmetric 1- and 2-vortex or between two 2-vortices, the vortex trajectories can differ strongly from the BPS geodesic. This enhances the chaotic behavior in the formation of the final state.

### [22] [On curvature corrections for field theory cosmic strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05243)
*Josu C. Aurrekoetxea,Jose J. Blanco-Pillado,Alberto García Martín-Caro,J. M. Queiruga*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper derives and validates a low-energy effective action for cosmic strings in the Abelian-Higgs model, showing that curvature corrections vanish for pure Goldstone (translational) modes and arise only through couplings between massive worldsheet excitations and the worldsheet Ricci scalar. Lattice simulations with Adaptive Mesh Refinement confirm the effective theory’s predictions and reveal a parametric instability transferring energy from massive modes to Goldstone modes.
\n\n
本文推导并验证了Abelian-Higgs模型中宇宙弦的低能有效作用量，表明当仅保留Goldstone（平移）模时曲率修正项消失，而曲率效应仅通过世界面上的重质量激发与世界面Ricci标量的耦合引入。采用自适应网格细化（Adaptive Mesh Refinement）的格点模拟证实了有效理论的预测，并揭示了一种参数不稳定性，可将能量从重质量模转移至Goldstone模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to rigorously derive the effective worldsheet theory of cosmic strings directly from the solitonic field theory (Abelian-Higgs model) and clarify the structure of curvature corrections—particularly whether they appear at leading order when only massless Goldstone modes are considered. Additionally, the authors aim to incorporate massive fluctuations of the soliton profile into the effective description and test theoretical predictions against first-principles numerical simulations.
\n\n
动机在于从孤子场论（Abelian-Higgs模型）出发严格推导宇宙弦的世界面有效理论，并澄清曲率修正项的结构——特别是当仅考虑无质量Goldstone模时，曲率修正是否在最低阶出现。此外，作者旨在将孤子剖面的重质量涨落纳入有效描述，并通过第一性原理数值模拟检验理论预测。

Method: The authors start from the full Abelian-Higgs field theory and perform a systematic expansion around the static string solution to derive the low-energy effective action. They separate massless translational (Goldstone) modes from massive profile fluctuations. Using this decomposition, they compute how curvature of the string worldsheet couples to these modes. The resulting effective theory is then tested via high-resolution lattice simulations of the full nonlinear field equations in flat spacetime, employing Adaptive Mesh Refinement (AMR) to resolve both the string core and large-scale dynamics. The simulations track energy transfer between sectors and compare trajectories with effective action predictions.
\n\n
作者从完整的Abelian-Higgs场论出发，围绕静态弦解进行系统展开以推导低能有效作用量。他们将无质量的平移（Goldstone）模与重质量的剖面涨落分离，并利用此分解计算弦世界面曲率如何与这些模耦合。随后，通过在平直时空中的高分辨率格点模拟对全非线性场方程进行数值求解来检验所得有效理论，采用自适应网格细化（Adaptive Mesh Refinement, AMR）技术同时解析弦芯和大尺度动力学。模拟追踪不同自由度间的能量转移，并将轨迹与有效作用量的预测进行对比。

Result: The analysis shows that the effective action for pure Goldstone modes contains no nontrivial curvature corrections at leading order—i.e., the Nambu-Goto action is exact to this order. Curvature effects enter only when massive modes are included, via a coupling of the form $\\int d^2\\sigma \\sqrt{-g} \\, \\phi^2 R^{(2)}$, where $\\phi$ represents massive fluctuations and $R^{(2)}$ is the worldsheet Ricci scalar. Numerical simulations confirm the validity of the effective theory within its regime of applicability and demonstrate a parametric resonance instability: excited strings decay by transferring energy from massive modes to the massless Goldstone sector.
\n\n
分析表明，纯Goldstone模的有效作用量在最低阶不含非平凡的曲率修正项——即Nambu-Goto作用量在此阶是精确的。只有当包含重质量模时，曲率效应才通过形如 $\\int d^2\\sigma \\sqrt{-g} \\, \\phi^2 R^{(2)}$ 的耦合项引入，其中 $\\phi$ 表示重质量涨落，$R^{(2)}$ 为世界面Ricci标量。数值模拟在有效理论适用范围内证实了其正确性，并展示了一种参数共振不稳定性：受激弦通过将能量从重质量模转移至无质量Goldstone模而衰变。

Conclusion: The work establishes a consistent and predictive effective field theory for cosmic strings that bridges solitonic field theory and worldsheet dynamics. It resolves a long-standing question about the absence of intrinsic curvature corrections for translational modes and demonstrates that massive excitations are essential for curvature couplings. The agreement with first-principles simulations validates the effective theory framework and reveals new dynamical phenomena like parametric instabilities, which may have implications for cosmic string network evolution in cosmology.
\n\n
本工作建立了连接孤子场论与世界面动力学的一致且具有预测能力的宇宙弦有效场论。它解决了关于平移模不存在内禀曲率修正这一长期问题，并表明重质量激发对曲率耦合至关重要。与第一性原理模拟的良好吻合验证了有效理论框架，并揭示了参数不稳定性等新动力学现象，这对宇宙学中宇宙弦网络的演化可能具有重要意义。

Abstract: We present a combined analytical and numerical study of the effective action of field theory cosmic strings in the Abelian-Higgs model in flat space. Starting directly from the underlying solitonic field theory description, we provide a systematic derivation of the low energy effective action and present evidence for the absence of nontrivial curvature correction terms when only the translational Goldstone modes are retained. Using this framework, we extend the effective theory to include higher energy fluctuations of the soliton profile, which map to massive degrees of freedom propagating on the worldsheet. We show that the leading curvature contribution enters only through the coupling between these massive modes and the worldsheet Ricci scalar. We validate the resulting effective theory via lattice simulations of the full field theory equations of motion in flat space, implemented with Adaptive Mesh Refinement to capture the string dynamics across different scales. The numerical simulations confirm the dynamics obtained using the effective action in its validity range. Furthermore, they also demonstrate the existence of the predicted parametric instability of excited strings that drives the transfer of energy from massive excitations to the Goldstone sector.

</details>


### [23] [Spin Chains from large-$N$ QCD at strong coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04506)
*David Berenstein,Hiroki Kawai*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates the strong coupling limit of large $N$ QCD on a square lattice by mapping it to constrained 1D spin chains. While certain subsectors are integrable, the full model is shown to be non-integrable due to zigzag symmetry constraints from confining strings. Nevertheless, integrable subsectors enable an estimate of the roughening transition via extrapolation. The analysis extends to higher dimensions, where similar integrable subsectors exist in the absence of zigzag constraints.
\n\n
本文研究了大$N$ QCD在强耦合极限下通过映射到受约束的一维自旋链模型。尽管某些子 sector 是可积的，但由于禁闭弦的zigzag对称性约束，完整模型被证明是非可积的（至少在Bethe ansatz框架下）。然而，利用可积子 sector 的一阶解析结果外推，可以合理估计粗糙化相变点。该分析还推广到高维情形，在无zigzag约束的子 sector 中同样发现了可积性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the non-perturbative dynamics of large $N$ QCD in the strong coupling regime remains a central challenge. Mapping the Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian to lower-dimensional effective models like spin chains offers a tractable approach to explore confinement and phase transitions. A key motivation is to assess whether integrability—a powerful tool for solving quantum systems—can be leveraged in this context, and to clarify the role of physical constraints (e.g., from string zigzag symmetry) in breaking integrability.
\n\n
理解大$N$ QCD在强耦合区域的非微扰动力学仍是核心挑战。将Kogut-Susskind哈密顿量映射为低维有效模型（如自旋链）为研究禁闭和相变提供了可行途径。关键动机在于评估可积性（一种求解量子系统的强大工具）是否可用于此场景，并阐明物理约束（如来自弦zigzag对称性的约束）在破坏可积性中的作用。

Method: The authors reformulate the Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian of large $N$ QCD on a square lattice as a set of constrained one-dimensional spin chain models. They analyze integrability using Bethe ansatz techniques and identify subsectors that decouple from the zigzag symmetry constraints. By examining the algebraic structure and scattering properties of excitations, they test for Yang-Baxter consistency. The roughening transition point is estimated by extrapolating first-order perturbative results obtained within integrable subsectors. The method is generalized to higher spatial dimensions by considering analogous lattice constructions.
\n\n
作者将正方格点上的大$N$ QCD的Kogut-Susskind哈密顿量重新表述为一组受约束的一维自旋链模型。他们使用Bethe ansatz技术分析可积性，并识别出与zigzag对称性约束解耦的子 sector。通过检验激发态的代数结构和散射性质，测试Yang-Baxter一致性。粗糙化相变点通过外推在可积子 sector 中获得的一阶微扰结果来估计。该方法通过考虑类比的格点构造推广到更高空间维度。

Result: The study finds that while specific subsectors of the spin chain—those free from zigzag constraints—are integrable and solvable via Bethe ansatz, the full spin chain including all physical constraints is not integrable. The breakdown of integrability is directly attributed to the zigzag symmetry of confining strings. Despite this, analytical results from integrable subsectors yield a reasonable estimate for the roughening transition point through extrapolation. In higher dimensions, similarly constrained subsectors remain integrable when zigzag effects are absent.
\n\n
研究发现，虽然自旋链中某些子 sector（不受zigzag约束的）可通过Bethe ansatz求解且具有可积性，但包含所有物理约束的完整自旋链是非可积的。可积性的破坏直接归因于禁闭弦的zigzag对称性。尽管如此，通过外推可积子 sector 的解析结果，仍能合理估计粗糙化相变点。在高维情形中，当不存在zigzag效应时，类似的受限子 sector 仍保持可积性。

Conclusion: Integrability in the strong coupling limit of large $N$ QCD is limited to constrained subsectors of the effective spin chain description. The full theory is non-integrable due to physical constraints from string zigzag symmetry, highlighting the fragility of integrability in realistic gauge theories. Nevertheless, controlled use of integrable sectors provides valuable non-perturbative insights, such as estimating the roughening transition. This approach may inform future studies of confinement and phase structure in lattice gauge theories beyond integrability.
\n\n
在大$N$ QCD强耦合极限下，可积性仅限于有效自旋链描述中的受限子 sector。完整理论由于弦zigzag对称性引入的物理约束而不可积，这凸显了可积性在现实规范理论中的脆弱性。然而，对可积 sector 的受控使用仍能提供有价值的非微扰洞见，例如估计粗糙化相变点。该方法可能为未来研究超出可积性范畴的格点规范理论中的禁闭与相结构提供指导。

Abstract: We study the strong coupling expansion of large $N$ QCD in various dimensions, reformulating the Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian on a square lattice in terms of (constrained) one dimensional spin chain models. We study the integrability properties of the spin chain obtained this way: there is large class of integrable subsectors, but we show that the full spin chain is not integrable, at least when viewed from a description based on Bethe ansatz. We demonstrate that the spin chains no longer possess integrability due to the constraints arising from the zigzag symmetry of the confining strings. The spin chain description properly estimates the roughening transition point by extrapolating the first-order analytical results based on integrability of some subsectors. The generalization to higher dimensions are also considered, where we also find the small subsectors without the zigzag constraints to be integrable.

</details>


### [24] [Regge trajectories from the adjoint sector of Matrix Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04522)
*Igor R. Klebanov,Henry W. Lin,Pavel Meshcheriakov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates the adjoint sector of SU$(N)$ symmetric quantum mechanics of a Hermitian matrix in the large $N$ limit, revealing Regge trajectories with $Δ^2 \sim n/α'$ at criticality—interpreted as short folded open strings in dual 2D string theory—and a transition to long strings away from criticality.
\n\n
本文研究了大 $N$ 极限下具有 SU$(N)$ 对称性的 Hermitian 矩阵量子力学的伴随表示（adjoint）扇区，在临界点处揭示出满足 $Δ^2 \sim n/α'$ 的 Regge 轨迹——在对偶的二维弦论中被解释为“短”折叠开弦的激发态；稍偏离临界点时，高激发态转变为延伸至 Liouville 方向的“长弦”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While the singlet sector of this matrix quantum mechanics is exactly solvable via free fermions and well understood—including its connection to 2D string theory—the behavior of non-singlet sectors, particularly the adjoint sector near criticality (when the Fermi level approaches a potential maximum), remains less explored. The authors aim to uncover new physical phenomena in this regime and establish their holographic interpretation in 2D string theory.
\n\n
尽管该矩阵量子力学的单态（singlet）扇区可通过自由费米子精确求解，并已充分理解（包括其与二维弦论的联系），但非单态扇区（尤其是伴随表示扇区）在临界区域（即费米能级趋近势能极大值时）的行为仍较少被探索。作者旨在揭示此区域中的新物理现象，并建立其在二维弦论中的全息诠释。

Method: The authors solve the Marchesini-Onofri equation—which governs the dynamics of the adjoint sector in the large $N$ limit—using both numerical methods and analytical semiclassical approximations. They analyze the spectrum near criticality where the Fermi surface touches a local maximum of the confining potential, and compare the resulting energy levels with expectations from 2D string theory, particularly focusing on Regge behavior and string interpretations.
\n\n
作者通过数值方法和解析的半经典近似求解控制大 $N$ 极限下伴随表示扇区动力学的 Marchesini-Onofri 方程。他们分析了费米面接触禁闭势局部极大值时的临界区域谱，并将所得能级与二维弦论中的预期（特别是 Regge 行为和弦的物理解释）进行比较。

Result: At criticality, the energy eigenvalues in the adjoint sector follow Regge trajectories with $Δ^2 \sim n/α'$, where $n$ is the excitation number and $α'$ is the string tension parameter. These states are interpreted as oscillatory modes of a short folded open string in the dual 2D string theory. This Regge behavior is universal up to sub-leading corrections and independent of the specific form of the potential used to approach criticality. Slightly away from criticality, highly excited states become long strings extending into the Liouville direction.
\n\n
在临界点处，伴随表示扇区的能级遵循 Regge 轨迹 $Δ^2 \sim n/α'$，其中 $n$ 为激发量子数，$α'$ 为弦张力参数。这些态被解释为对偶二维弦论中“短”折叠开弦的振荡模式。该 Regge 行为在次领头阶修正下具有普适性，且不依赖于趋近临界点所采用的具体势函数形式。稍偏离临界点时，高激发态转变为延伸至 Liouville 方向的“长弦”。

Conclusion: The adjoint sector of large $N$ matrix quantum mechanics exhibits rich stringy physics near criticality, with a clear holographic realization in 2D string theory: short folded open strings at criticality and long strings away from it. The universality of the Regge behavior suggests a robust connection between matrix models and string theory beyond the singlet sector.
\n\n
大 $N$ 矩阵量子力学的伴随表示扇区在临界点附近展现出丰富的弦论物理，在二维弦论中具有清晰的全息实现：临界点处为短折叠开弦，偏离临界点则为长弦。Regge 行为的普适性表明，矩阵模型与弦论之间的联系在单态扇区之外依然稳健。

Abstract: We reexamine the large $N$ limit of SU$(N)$ symmetric quantum mechanics of a Hermitian matrix whose singlet sector is well known to be exactly solvable via free fermions. When the Fermi level approaches a maximum of the potential, there is critical behavior corresponding to string theory in two dimensions. We uncover new phenomena in the adjoint sector by solving the Marchesini-Onofri equation both numerically and analytically using semiclassical approximations: at criticality, the spectrum is governed by Regge trajectories with energy eigenvalues growing according to $Δ^2 \sim n/ α'$. In the dual 2D string theory, we interpret these states as oscillatory excitations of a ``short'' folded open string. Up to sub-leading corrections, this Regge behavior is essentially universal and is insensitive to the particular potential we choose to approach criticality. Slightly away from criticality, the highly excited states transition into ``long strings'' that extend far into the Liouville direction.

</details>


### [25] [A smooth road to bumpy horizons: shaping black holes with non-linear sigma models, from supergravity to higher dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04611)
*Fabrizio Canfora,Nicolás Grandi,Carla Henríquez-Báez,Julio Oliva*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper constructs new exact solutions in General Relativity coupled to non-linear sigma models, including bumpy black holes, stars, anisotropic cosmologies, and branes in $d \geq 4$, plus time-dependent 2+1D solutions, using first-order BPS relations for coset scalars.
\n\n
本文在广义相对论与非线性sigma模型耦合体系中构造了新的精确解，包括 $d \geq 4$ 维中的“bumpy”黑洞、恒星、各向异性宇宙学解以及黑弦和黑 $p$-膜，并利用coset标量场的一阶Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS) 关系给出了 $2+1$ 维的时间依赖解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend the known solution space of Einstein gravity coupled to non-linear sigma models—particularly those with homogeneous target spaces like $SU(2)/U(1)$—by leveraging recently discovered first-order BPS equations that simplify solving the full second-order field equations. This allows exploration of exotic geometries such as horizon deformations ("bumps") and anisotropic spacetimes relevant for both classical gravity and supergravity embeddings.
\n\n
动机在于扩展爱因斯坦引力与非线性sigma模型（尤其是具有齐次目标空间如 $SU(2)/U(1)$ 的模型）耦合体系的已知解空间。通过利用最近发现的一阶BPS方程，可简化求解完整的二阶场方程，从而探索诸如视界形变（“bumps”）和各向异性时空等奇异几何结构，这些解对经典引力和超引力嵌入均有意义。

Method: The authors employ a first-order Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS) ansatz for the scalar fields valued in a coset $G/H$, reducing the second-order Einstein-scalar equations to a set of integrable first-order differential equations. This method generalizes the construction in arXiv:2601.22914 and applies to a broad class of non-linear sigma models, enabling analytic solutions for neutral/charged/magnetized black holes, bumpy stars, anisotropic cosmologies, black strings, and $p$-branes in $d \geq 4$, as well as time-dependent solutions in $2+1$ dimensions.
\n\n
作者对取值于coset空间 $G/H$ 的标量场采用一阶Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield (BPS) 假设，将二阶爱因斯坦-标量场方程约化为一组可积的一阶微分方程。该方法推广了arXiv:2601.22914中的构造，适用于一大类非线性sigma模型，从而在 $d \geq 4$ 维中解析地求得中性/带电/磁化黑洞、“bumpy”恒星、各向异性宇宙学解、黑弦和 $p$-膜，以及 $2+1$ 维的时间依赖解。

Result: New families of exact solutions are obtained: (i) static and stationary black holes with deformed (“bumpy”) horizons; (ii) self-gravitating bumpy stars; (iii) anisotropic cosmological spacetimes; (iv) extended objects like black strings and black $p$-branes; and (v) time-dependent solutions in $2+1$ dimensions. Some solutions admit embedding into supergravity, enhancing their physical relevance.
\n\n
获得了多类新的精确解：(i) 具有形变（“bumpy”）视界的静态与稳态黑洞；(ii) 自引力“bumpy”恒星；(iii) 各向异性宇宙学时空；(iv) 黑弦和黑 $p$-膜等延展物体；(v) $2+1$ 维的时间依赖解。部分解可嵌入超引力理论，增强了其物理相关性。

Conclusion: The use of first-order BPS relations for coset-valued scalars provides a powerful framework for generating rich classes of exact solutions in gravity-sigma model systems, significantly expanding the landscape of known geometries beyond spherical symmetry and offering new arenas for studying strong-field gravity, holography, and supergravity.
\n\n
对取值于coset空间的标量场使用一阶BPS关系，为引力-sigma模型系统中生成丰富的精确解提供了一个强大框架，显著拓展了超越球对称性的已知几何景观，为研究强场引力、全息对偶和超引力开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We construct new families of solutions for General Relativity coupled to a general class of non-linear sigma models, some of which can be embedded in supergravity. The solutions include neutral, charged and magnetized black holes with bumpy horizons, bumpy stars, and anisotropic cosmologies in $d\geq 4$ dimensions, as well as black strings and black $p$-branes. We also present a family of time-dependent solutions in $2+1$-dimensions. The construction relies on a set of first-order Bogomol'nyi-Prasad-Sommerfield relations for the coset scalars, that were recently exploited for the construction of bumpy black holes on the non-linear sigma model with homogenous target $SU(2)/U(1)$ in 2601.22914 [hep-th].

TL;DR: The paper establishes a novel correspondence between $q$-series enumerating quarter-BPS black hole state degeneracies and $\hat{Z}$ invariants of 3D Chern-Simons theory on orientation-reversed manifolds, using resurgent continuation of transseries.
\n\n
该论文利用 transseries 的 resurgent continuation 方法，建立了枚举四分之一 BPS 黑洞态简并度的 $q$-级数与一类三维定向反转流形上 Chern-Simons 理论的 $\hat{Z}$ 不变量之间的新对应关系。

  <summary>Details</summary>

作者采用应用于 transseries 展开的 resurgent continuation 方法，将不同物理背景下的渐近级数进行解析延拓连接——具体而言，即四分之一 BPS 态简并度的 $q$-级数与定义在定向反转三维流形上的 Chern-Simons 理论中的 $\hat{Z}$ 不变量。

Conclusion: This work reveals a profound link between supersymmetric black hole physics and topological invariants via resurgence theory, opening new avenues for understanding quantum gravity through the lens of 3D topological field theories and non-perturbative completions of asymptotic series.

该工作通过 resurgence 理论揭示了超对称黑洞物理与拓扑不变量之间的深刻联系，为借助三维拓扑场论和渐近级数的非微扰完备化来理解量子引力开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The method of resurgent continuation of transseries reveals a new correspondence between the $q$-series for enumerating degeneracies of quarter-BPS states in supersymmetric black holes and $\hat{Z}$ invariants of Chern-Simons theory on a class of 3 dimensional orientation-reversed manifolds.
