### [27] [Holographic QCD and quarkonium melting: Finite temperature, density, and external field effects in self-consistent dynamical models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04725)
*Bruno Toniato*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This MSc dissertation develops a self-consistent dynamical holographic QCD model within the Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton framework to study heavy and exotic meson spectra and melting under finite temperature, density, and magnetic fields. It reveals sequential quarkonia melting, chemical potential–induced acceleration of dissociation, and a transition from inverse magnetic catalysis to magnetic catalysis due to spatial anisotropy.
\n\n
本篇硕士论文在Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton框架内构建了一个自洽的动力学全息QCD模型，用于研究有限温度、密度和磁场下重味及奇异介子的质量谱与熔解行为。研究揭示了夸克偶素的逐级熔解、化学势诱导的解离加速，以及由于空间各向异性导致的从逆磁催化到磁催化的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The AdS/CFT correspondence offers a non-perturbative approach to strongly coupled QCD phenomena, which are inaccessible via conventional perturbative methods. Understanding the behavior of heavy and exotic mesons—particularly their spectral properties and dissociation patterns—under extreme conditions (finite temperature $T$, baryon chemical potential $\mu_B$, and external magnetic fields $B$) is crucial for mapping the QCD phase diagram and interpreting heavy-ion collision data. Existing bottom-up holographic models often lack full backreaction or self-consistency; this work aims to address these limitations by constructing a fully dynamical background from coupled Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton equations.
\n\n
AdS/CFT对偶为研究强耦合QCD现象提供了一种非微扰方法，而这些现象无法通过传统微扰手段处理。理解重味及奇异介子在极端条件（有限温度$T$、重子化学势$\mu_B$和外加磁场$B$）下的谱性质与解离模式，对于描绘QCD相图和解释重离子碰撞实验数据至关重要。现有的自下而上全息模型通常缺乏完整的背反应或自洽性；本工作旨在通过从耦合的Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton方程出发构建完全动力学背景，以克服这些局限。

Method: The author constructs a self-consistent holographic background by solving the coupled Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton field equations in asymptotically AdS$_5$ spacetime. The dilaton field $\phi(z)$ and Maxwell field $A_t(z)$ encode the non-conformality and finite density, respectively, with the metric determined dynamically rather than imposed \textit{a priori}. Meson spectra are obtained by solving the linearized fluctuation equations for vector modes in this background. Spectral functions $\rho(\omega, T, \mu_B, B)$ are computed via the retarded Green’s function using the gauge-gravity dictionary. For magnetic field effects, the model is extended to include a nonlinear Einstein-Born-Infeld action coupled to the dilaton, introducing spatial anisotropy between directions parallel and perpendicular to $B$.
\n\n
作者通过求解渐近AdS$_5$时空中的耦合Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton场方程，构建了一个自洽的全息背景。其中，dilaton场$\phi(z)$和Maxwell场$A_t(z)$分别编码非共形性和有限密度效应，度规由动力学决定而非预先设定。介子谱通过在此背景下求解矢量模的线性化涨落方程获得。利用规范-引力对偶，通过推迟Green函数计算谱函数$\rho(\omega, T, \mu_B, B)$。为研究磁场效应，模型被推广至包含与dilaton耦合的非线性Einstein-Born-Infeld作用量，从而在平行与垂直于$B$的方向上引入空间各向异性。

Result: At finite temperature, the model exhibits a first-order confinement-deconfinement phase transition, accompanied by sequential melting of charmonia and bottomonia states as temperature increases. At finite density, increasing $\mu_B$ lowers the dissociation temperature of mesons, with spectral peaks broadening smoothly across the crossover region. Under strong magnetic fields, the system transitions from inverse magnetic catalysis (suppression of chiral condensate with $B$ at low $T$) to magnetic catalysis (enhancement of bound states) at higher temperatures, a phenomenon attributed to the anisotropic deformation of the holographic geometry induced by the Born-Infeld term.
\n\n
在有限温度下，模型展现出一级禁闭-退禁闭相变，并伴随随温度升高而发生的粲偶素和底偶素态的逐级熔解。在有限密度下，增大$\mu_B$会降低介子的解离温度，且谱峰在穿越相变区域时平滑展宽。在强磁场下，系统从逆磁催化（低温下$B$抑制手征凝聚）转变为磁催化（高温下束缚态增强），这一现象归因于Born-Infeld项所诱导的全息几何的空间各向异性形变。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that a fully backreacted, self-consistent Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton holographic model can successfully capture key non-perturbative features of QCD, including sequential quarkonia suppression, density-driven meson dissociation, and the interplay between magnetic fields and spatial anisotropy. The shift from inverse to direct magnetic catalysis underscores the importance of nonlinear electrodynamics and geometric backreaction in modeling QCD matter under extreme conditions. Such frameworks provide valuable insights for future studies of the QCD phase diagram and heavy-flavor observables in heavy-ion collisions.
\n\n
本工作表明，一个完全包含背反应的自洽Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton全息模型能够成功捕捉QCD的关键非微扰特征，包括夸克偶素的逐级压低、密度驱动的介子解离，以及磁场与空间各向异性之间的相互作用。从逆磁催化到正磁催化的转变凸显了非线性电动力学和几何背反应在极端条件下建模QCD物质的重要性。此类框架为未来研究QCD相图及重离子碰撞中的重味观测量提供了重要启示。

Abstract: This MSc dissertation is based on the papers arXiv:2502.12694 and arXiv:2408.14813. The AdS/CFT correspondence provides a powerful framework for modeling strongly coupled gauge theories and, as a consequence, investigating non-perturbative phenomena in QCD. In this work, following an overview of the ideas that encapsulate the AdS/CFT correspondence, we present a self-consistent dynamical holographic QCD model within the Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton framework, derived from the coupled field equations, to study the mass spectra and melting behavior of heavy and exotic mesons at finite temperature and density. Finite temperature analyses reveal a confinement-deconfinement transition and sequential quarkonia melting. At finite density, an increase in chemical potential accelerates meson melting, with spectral functions evolving smoothly across the phase transition line. Finally, using a nonlinear Einstein-Born-Infeld-dilaton model, magnetic field effects demonstrate a shift from inverse magnetic catalysis to magnetic catalysis, highlighting the impact of spatial anisotropy on quarkonium stability.

</details>


### [28] [$N^{3/2}$ Scaling from $3d$ $\mathcal{N}=2$ Dualities: an Alternative Approach to Chiral Quivers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04849)
*Antonio Amariti,Giulia Lanzetti*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We resolve a long-standing problem regarding the $N^{3/2}$ scaling of the free energy for 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ chiral quiver gauge theories dual to M2-branes at toric SE$_7$ singularities by showing their three-sphere partition functions are equivalent—via hyperbolic hypergeometric integral identities—to those of non-chiral quivers with chiral flavors, for which the scaling is known. This establishes a large $N$ duality generalizing Giveon-Kutasov duality to chiral settings.
\n\n
我们通过将三维球面配分函数表示为双曲超几何积分，并利用精确的积分恒等式，解决了关于对偶于M2膜在toric SE$_7$奇点处的3维$\mathcal{N}=2$手征箭图规范理论自由能$N^{3/2}$标度的长期未决问题。我们证明其配分函数等价于已知具有手征味的非手征箭图的情形，从而建立了推广Giveon-Kutasov对偶到手征情形的大$N$对偶，确认了所研究手征箭图的$N^{3/2}$标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The moduli space of certain 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ chiral quiver gauge theories—constructed via un-higgsing from non-chiral quivers and conjectured to describe M2-branes at toric Sasaki-Einstein seven-manifold (SE$_7$) singularities—was shown to match geometric expectations from M-theory. However, verifying the expected $N^{3/2}$ scaling of the free energy on the three-sphere, a key test of the AdS$_4$/CFT$_3$ correspondence, remained unresolved for over ten years. This motivated the search for new analytical techniques to compute or relate the partition function in the large $N$ limit.
\n\n
某些通过从未手征箭图出发经由un-higgsing构造的3维$\mathcal{N}=2$手征箭图规范理论，被猜想描述M2膜在toric Sasaki-Einstein七维流形（SE$_7$）奇点处的物理，其模空间已与M理论的几何预期一致。然而，在三维球面上自由能应呈现的$N^{3/2}$标度——作为AdS$_4$/CFT$_3$对偶的关键检验——在过去十余年中仍未得到验证。这促使人们寻找新的解析方法，以在大$N$极限下计算或关联其配分函数。

Method: The authors reformulate the three-sphere ($S^3$) partition function of the chiral quiver theories as a hyperbolic hypergeometric integral. They then apply exact integral identities—mathematical results from special function theory—to demonstrate that this integral reduces precisely to the partition function of a related non-chiral quiver theory with chiral flavor fields. This reduction relies on properties of the hyperbolic gamma function and generalizations of Seiberg-like dualities, specifically a chiral extension of Giveon-Kutasov duality.
\n\n
作者将手征箭图理论的三维球面（$S^3$）配分函数重新表述为双曲超几何积分，并应用特殊函数理论中的精确积分恒等式，证明该积分可精确约化为一个带有手征味场的相关非手征箭图理论的配分函数。这一约化依赖于双曲Gamma函数的性质以及Seiberg型对偶的推广，特别是Giveon-Kutasov对偶在手征情形下的推广。

Result: The free energy $F = -\log |Z_{S^3}|$ of the chiral quiver theories is shown to equal that of non-chiral quivers with chiral flavors, for which the large $N$ behavior is known to scale as $N^{3/2}$. Consequently, the $N^{3/2}$ scaling is rigorously established for the entire family of chiral quivers under consideration. Moreover, the equality of partition functions implies an exact large $N$ duality between these two classes of theories.
\n\n
手征箭图理论的自由能$F = -\log |Z_{S^3}|$被证明等于已知大$N$行为呈$N^{3/2}$标度的带手征味的非手征箭图理论的自由能。因此，所研究的整族手征箭图的$N^{3/2}$标度被严格确立。此外，配分函数的相等性意味着这两类理论之间存在精确的大$N$对偶。

Conclusion: This work resolves a decade-old open problem by establishing the $N^{3/2}$ scaling of the free energy for 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ chiral quiver gauge theories dual to M2-branes at toric SE$_7$ singularities. The key insight is a mathematical identity between hyperbolic hypergeometric integrals that physically realizes a generalized Giveon-Kutasov duality. This not only confirms the holographic expectation from M-theory but also extends the scope of known dualities to include chiral matter content, enriching the landscape of 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ dualities.
\n\n
本工作通过建立对偶于toric SE$_7$奇点处M2膜的3维$\mathcal{N}=2$手征箭图规范理论自由能的$N^{3/2}$标度，解决了长达十年的开放问题。关键在于双曲超几何积分之间的数学恒等式，它在物理上实现了Giveon-Kutasov对偶的推广。这不仅验证了M理论的全息预期，还将已知对偶性的适用范围扩展至包含手征物质的情形，丰富了3维$\mathcal{N}=2$对偶性的理论图景。

Abstract: We investigate families of 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ chiral quiver gauge theories conjectured to be dual to M2-branes probing toric SE$_7$ singularities. Geometrically, these families correspond to toric diagrams without internal points. At the field theory level, the models are constructed via an un-higgsing procedure applied to non-chiral quivers. While the moduli space of these theories was shown to match M-theory expectations, determining the $N^{3/2}$ scaling of the free energy remained an open problem for over a decade, with positive results emerging only very recently. In this work, we address this challenge by reformulating the three-sphere partition function as a hyperbolic hypergeometric integral. Using exact integral identities, we show that the free energy reduces precisely to that of non-chiral quivers with chiral flavors, for which the $N^{3/2}$ scaling is already established. Physically, this mathematical identity corresponds to the equivalence of three-sphere partition functions under a generalization of Giveon-Kutasov duality to chiral quivers. Our results thus provide a large $N$ duality between the chiral quivers and non-chiral quivers with chiral flavors, confirming the $N^{3/2}$ scaling for the chiral quivers under study.

</details>


### [29] [Parameter compression in the flux landscape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04941)
*Aman Chauhan,Michele Cicoli,Sven Krippendorf,Anshuman Maharana,Pellegrino Piantadosi,Andreas Schachner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper performs a data-driven analysis of the ensemble of no-scale type IIB flux vacua from \cite{Chauhan:2025rdj}, using dimensionality-reduction and topological methods to reveal that the effective dimensionality of the 12-dimensional flux space is much lower. A physics-informed autoencoder compresses flux and moduli data into a latent space that isolates regions with small $|W_0|$, while persistent homology uncovers robust topological structures, laying groundwork for foundation models in string phenomenology.
\n\n
本文对文献\\cite{Chauhan:2025rdj}中构建的无尺度（no-scale）IIB型通量真空系综进行了数据驱动分析，结合降维与拓扑方法，揭示出原本12维的通量空间具有显著更低的有效维度。作者使用物理信息自编码器（physics-informed autoencoder）将通量与模空间数据压缩至低维潜空间，成功分离出具有小$|W_0|$值的区域；同时利用持久同调（persistent homology）识别出模空间与通量子空间中稳健的拓扑结构，为弦唯象学中的基础模型（foundation models）发展奠定必要基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The vast landscape of type IIB flux vacua poses a major challenge for systematic exploration and phenomenological selection. Traditional linear analyses fail to capture non-trivial correlations among fluxes and moduli, especially those relevant for achieving small values of the flux superpotential $|W_0|$, which are crucial for KKLT-type de Sitter constructions. The authors aim to uncover hidden low-dimensional structures and topological features in this high-dimensional vacuum ensemble to enable more efficient and physically meaningful navigation of the landscape.
\n\n
IIB型通量真空景观的庞大规模对系统性探索和唯象筛选构成了重大挑战。传统的线性分析无法捕捉通量与模之间非平凡的相关性，尤其是那些对实现小通量超势$|W_0|$至关重要的关联——这在KKLT型de Sitter构造中尤为关键。作者旨在揭示该高维真空系综中隐藏的低维结构与拓扑特征，以实现对弦景观更高效、更具物理意义的导航。

Method: The authors employ a hybrid methodology combining machine learning and topological data analysis. They first apply linear (e.g., PCA) and non-linear dimensionality reduction techniques to the 12-dimensional flux data. A key innovation is a physics-informed autoencoder trained on paired flux-moduli data, whose loss function incorporates physical priors to prioritize features like small $|W_0|$. Concurrently, they use persistent homology—a tool from topological data analysis—to compute topological invariants (e.g., Betti numbers) across scales, revealing stable connected components, loops, or voids in the vacuum distribution within both flux and moduli spaces.
\n\n
作者采用结合机器学习与拓扑数据分析的混合方法。首先对12维通量数据应用线性（如PCA）与非线性降维技术。核心创新在于一个物理信息自编码器，其在通量-模配对数据上训练，损失函数嵌入了物理先验（如优先关注小$|W_0|$区域）。同时，他们使用持久同调（persistent homology）——一种拓扑数据分析工具——计算跨尺度的拓扑不变量（如Betti数），以揭示通量空间与模空间中真空分布内稳定的连通分支、环或空洞等拓扑结构。

Result: The analysis reveals that the intrinsic dimensionality of the flux space is significantly lower than 12, indicating strong constraints among flux choices. The physics-informed autoencoder successfully organizes vacua in its latent space such that regions with small $|W_0|$ are isolated and exhibit non-linear correlations invisible to PCA. Persistent homology identifies long-lived topological features (e.g., non-trivial $H_0$ and $H_1$) in both flux and moduli subspaces, suggesting an underlying geometric organization of the vacuum ensemble beyond simple clustering.
\n\n
分析表明，通量空间的内在维度远低于12维，说明通量选择之间存在强约束。物理信息自编码器成功在其潜空间中组织真空，使得小$|W_0|$区域被有效分离，并展现出PCA无法捕捉的非线性关联。持久同调在通量与模子空间中均识别出长寿命的拓扑特征（如非平凡的$H_0$与$H_1$），表明真空系综具有超越简单聚类的深层几何组织结构。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that advanced data science techniques—particularly physics-informed representation learning and topological data analysis—can extract meaningful structure from the complex landscape of string vacua. The identification of a low-dimensional latent organization and robust topological signatures provides a foundation for building predictive foundation models in string phenomenology, enabling targeted searches for vacua with desired physical properties such as small $|W_0|$.
\n\n
本工作表明，先进的数据科学技术——特别是物理信息表征学习与拓扑数据分析——能够从复杂的弦真空景观中提取有意义的结构。低维潜空间组织与稳健拓扑信号的识别，为构建弦唯象学中的预测性基础模型（foundation models）奠定了基础，使得可针对性地搜索具有特定物理性质（如小$|W_0|$）的真空成为可能。

Abstract: We present a data-driven investigation of the exhaustive ensemble of no-scale type IIB flux vacua constructed in \cite{Chauhan:2025rdj}. Using a combination of linear and non-linear dimensionality-reduction techniques, we analyse both flux and moduli spaces and demonstrate that the effective dimensionality of the underlying 12-dimensional flux space is substantially reduced. A central component of our study is a physics-informed autoencoder, which provides a non-linear compression of the flux and moduli data into a low-dimensional latent space. The learned latent representation organises vacua according to desired features and, in particular, isolates distinguished regions associated with small values of the flux superpotential $|W_0|$, revealing non-trivial correlations that are not captured by linear methods. In parallel, we apply tools from topological data analysis, specifically persistent homology, to probe the global structure of the vacuum distribution. This allows us to identify robust, long-lived topological features in both moduli and flux subspaces. This work is a necessary step for developing foundation models in string phenomenology.

</details>


### [30] [Gravitational instantons from closed superstring field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04953)
*Ivo Sachs,Xianghang Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates the exact marginality of deformations resolving a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold in closed superstring theory by computing equations of motion up to third order in the deformation parameter (orbifold resolution size), including $α'$ corrections. It finds no obstructions at third order and recovers the Eguchi-Hanson gravitational instanton in the field theory limit up to second order.
\n\n
本文通过在闭合超弦理论中计算至形变参数（轨道空间分辨率大小）三阶的运动方程（包括 $α'$ 修正），研究了 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 轨道空间分解形变的精确边缘性。结果发现三阶修正对所有形变模均无障碍，并在场论极限下通过适当选择模空间参数，重现了二阶精度的 Eguchi-Hanson 引力瞬子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding whether orbifold resolution deformations remain exactly marginal in string theory is crucial for moduli stabilization, non-renormalization theorems, and connecting string compactifications to smooth geometries. The presence of $α'$ corrections may obstruct marginality, so testing this to higher orders is essential.
\n\n
理解轨道空间分解形变在弦论中是否保持精确边缘性，对于模稳定化、非重整化定理以及将弦紧致化与光滑几何联系起来至关重要。$α'$ 修正可能会阻碍边缘性，因此有必要在更高阶进行检验。

Method: The authors solve the closed superstring equations of motion perturbatively in the deformation parameter corresponding to the resolution of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold singularity, expanding up to third order while incorporating $α'$ corrections. They analyze the solvability (i.e., absence of obstructions) of these equations and compare the resulting spacetime geometry in the low-energy field theory limit with known gravitational instantons.
\n\n
作者在对应于 $\mathbb{Z}_2$ 轨道空间奇点分解的形变参数中，对闭合超弦运动方程进行微扰求解，展开至三阶并包含 $α'$ 修正。他们分析这些方程的可解性（即无障碍条件），并将低能场论极限下得到的时空几何与已知的引力瞬子进行比较。

Result: The third-order correction to the deformation is unobstructed for all values of the deformation moduli, indicating exact marginality persists at this order. Moreover, by choosing appropriate moduli, the solution reproduces the Eguchi-Hanson gravitational instanton up to second order in the field theory limit.
\n\n
对所有形变模而言，三阶修正均无障碍，表明在此阶数下精确边缘性依然成立。此外，通过适当选择模参数，该解在场论极限下可重现二阶精度的 Eguchi-Hanson 引力瞬子。

Conclusion: The resolution deformation of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold remains exactly marginal at least up to third order in perturbation theory when $α'$ corrections are included. This supports the consistency of using such deformations to connect singular orbifolds to smooth Calabi–Yau geometries in string compactifications.
\n\n
当包含 $α'$ 修正时，$\mathbb{Z}_2$ 轨道空间的分解形变至少在微扰论三阶仍保持精确边缘性。这支持了在弦紧致化中使用此类形变将奇异轨道空间与光滑 Calabi–Yau 几何相连接的一致性。

Abstract: We test exact marginality of the deformation describing the resolution of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold by analyzing the closed superstring equations of motion to third order in the size, including $α'$ corrections. We find that the third order correction is unobstructed for all deformation moduli. We are also able to reproduce the Eguchi-Hanson gravitational instanton up to the second order in the field theory limit with a suitable choice of moduli.

</details>


### [31] [Simulating Lattice Gauge Theories with Virtual Rishons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05151)
*David Rogerson,João Barata,Robert M. Konik,Raju Venugopalan,Ananda Roy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper introduces a novel virtual rishon framework that enforces gauge symmetry in lattice gauge theories using a quantum-link formulation, enabling simulations in $d+1$ spacetime dimensions with both classical tensor networks and near-term quantum hardware. The method is validated in U(1) gauge theories: for $d=1$, it reproduces features of the multi-flavor Schwinger model linked to Wess-Zumino-Witten CFT; for $d=2$, it accurately computes the confining string tension.
\n\n
本文提出了一种新颖的虚拟rishon框架，通过量子链（quantum-link）形式在格点规范理论中强制实现规范对称性，使得在$d+1$维时空下可同时使用经典张量网络和近期量子硬件进行模拟。该方法在U(1)规范理论中得到验证：对于$d=1$，重现了多味Schwinger模型与Wess-Zumino-Witten共形场论相关的特征；对于$d=2$，准确计算出了禁闭弦张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Simulating real-time dynamics of lattice gauge theories remains a major challenge due to the sign problem in Monte Carlo methods and the difficulty of preserving gauge invariance in tensor network or quantum circuit approaches. Existing formulations often struggle to maintain exact gauge symmetry while encoding both gauge and matter fields as dynamical qubit degrees of freedom, especially in higher dimensions. This work aims to overcome these limitations by introducing a framework that intrinsically respects gauge symmetry through a quantum-link construction based on virtual rishons.
\n\n
格点规范理论的实时动力学模拟由于蒙特卡洛方法中的符号问题以及在张量网络或量子电路方法中保持规范不变性的困难而极具挑战性。现有方案在将规范场与物质场同时编码为动态qubit自由度时，往往难以精确维持规范对称性，尤其在高维情形下更为困难。本文旨在通过基于虚拟rishon的量子链构造，引入一个内禀地保持规范对称性的框架，以克服这些限制。

Method: The authors develop a quantum-link model where gauge fields are represented via virtual rishon degrees of freedom residing on links, ensuring exact U(1) gauge invariance at every step. Both gauge and matter fields are mapped to qubits, allowing implementation on classical tensor networks and quantum processors. The framework supports arbitrary boundary conditions and topological angles. For $d=1$, they simulate the multi-flavor Schwinger model ($1\\leq N_f\\leq3$) and extract conformal data matching Wess-Zumino-Witten CFT predictions. For $d=2$, they compute the static quark potential and extract the confining string tension.
\n\n
作者发展了一种量子链模型，其中规范场通过位于链上的虚拟rishon自由度表示，从而在每一步都确保精确的U(1)规范不变性。规范场与物质场均被映射为qubit，使其可在经典张量网络和量子处理器上实现。该框架支持任意边界条件和拓扑角。对于$d=1$，他们模拟了多味Schwinger模型（$1\\leq N_f\\leq3$），并提取出与Wess-Zumino-Witten CFT预言一致的共形数据；对于$d=2$，他们计算了静态夸克势并提取出禁闭弦张力。

Result: In (1+1)D, the framework successfully captures the central charge and scaling dimensions of the $N_f$-flavor Schwinger model, consistent with the SU($N_f$)$_1$ Wess-Zumino-Witten CFT. In (2+1)D, the extracted confining string tension agrees quantitatively with continuum expectations from effective field theory and previous numerical studies. The method demonstrates robustness across different boundary conditions and nonzero topological theta angles, confirming its ability to handle nontrivial vacuum structure.
\n\n
在(1+1)维中，该框架成功捕捉到$N_f$味Schwinger模型的中心荷与标度维数，与SU($N_f$)$_1$ Wess-Zumino-Witten CFT一致。在(2+1)维中，所提取的禁闭弦张力与来自有效场论及先前数值研究的连续极限预期定量吻合。该方法在不同边界条件和非零拓扑theta角下均表现出鲁棒性，证实其能处理非平凡真空结构。

Conclusion: The virtual rishon framework provides a scalable, gauge-invariant formulation of lattice gauge theories suitable for both classical tensor network simulations and near-term quantum computation. By embedding gauge symmetry directly into the representation of link variables, it avoids common pitfalls of gauge violation and enables accurate studies of real-time dynamics, confinement, and topological effects in $d+1$ dimensions.
\n\n
虚拟rishon框架提供了一种可扩展且规范不变的格点规范理论表述，适用于经典张量网络模拟和近期量子计算。通过将规范对称性直接嵌入到链变量的表示中，该方法避免了规范破坏的常见问题，使得在$d+1$维中对实时动力学、禁闭现象和拓扑效应的精确研究成为可能。

Abstract: Classical tensor network and hybrid quantum-classical algorithms are promising candidates for the investigation of real-time properties of lattice gauge theories. We develop here a novel framework which enforces gauge symmetry via a quantum-link virtual rishon representation applied at intermediate steps. Crucially, the gauge and matter degrees of freedom are dynamical variables encoded in terms of qubits, enabling analysis of gauge theories in $d+1$ spacetime dimensions. We benchmark this framework in a U(1) gauge theory with and without matter fields. For $d = 1$, the multi-flavor Schwinger model with $1\leq N_f\leq3$ flavors is analyzed for arbitrary boundary conditions and nonzero topological angle, capturing signatures of the underlying Wess-Zumino-Witten conformal field theory. For $d = 2$, we extract the confining string tension in close agreement with continuum expectations. These results establish the virtual rishon framework as a scalable and robust approach for the simulation of lattice gauge theories using both classical tensor networks as well as near-term quantum hardware.

</details>


### [32] [Introduction to holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05186)
*Nele Callebaut*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: These course notes provide a pedagogical introduction to holography, focusing on the AdS/CFT correspondence as a concrete realization of the holographic principle in quantum gravity. The notes begin with foundational symmetries (Poincaré and conformal), develop the physics of Anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime, and culminate in the formulation of AdS/CFT, including finite-temperature extensions involving black hole thermodynamics and the role of entanglement in emergent gravity.
\n\n
这些课程讲义对全息原理（holography）进行了教学性介绍，重点聚焦于AdS/CFT对应作为量子引力中全息原理的具体实现。讲义从基础对称性（Poincaré 对称性和共形对称性）出发，发展 Anti-de Sitter（AdS）时空的物理，并最终构建 AdS/CFT 对应关系，包括涉及黑洞热力学的有限温度推广，以及纠缠在引力涌现中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to offer Master-level students a clear, step-by-step pedagogical pathway into the concept of holography—particularly the AdS/CFT correspondence—as a non-perturbative framework for quantum gravity. By emphasizing symmetry structures and building from familiar quantum field theory concepts, the course aims to demystify how a gravitational bulk theory can be encoded in a non-gravitational boundary theory.
\n\n
其动机是为硕士生提供一条清晰、循序渐进的教学路径，以理解全息原理——特别是 AdS/CFT 对应——作为量子引力的非微扰框架。通过强调对称性结构并从熟悉的量子场论概念出发，该课程旨在阐明引力体理论如何被编码在一个无引力的边界理论中。

Method: The method is didactic and structural: it begins with a review of Poincaré symmetry in QFT, progresses to conformal symmetry in CFTs, introduces the geometry and dynamics of Anti-de Sitter space, and then synthesizes these elements to formulate the AdS/CFT dictionary. The approach integrates theoretical foundations (symmetry algebras, spacetime geometry) with physical insights (black hole thermodynamics, entanglement entropy) to build intuition for holographic duality.
\n\n
方法是教学性与结构性的：首先回顾量子场论中的 Poincaré 对称性，进而过渡到共形场论（CFT）中的共形对称性，引入 Anti-de Sitter 时空的几何与动力学，最后综合这些要素构建 AdS/CFT 对应字典。该方法结合了理论基础（对称代数、时空几何）与物理洞见（黑洞热力学、纠缠熵），以建立对全息对偶的直观理解。

Result: The course successfully constructs a coherent narrative leading from basic QFT symmetries to the full AdS/CFT correspondence, including its finite-temperature generalization via black holes in AdS and the modern perspective that spacetime geometry and gravity may emerge from quantum entanglement in the boundary CFT.
\n\n
该课程成功构建了一条连贯的叙述路径，从基本的量子场论对称性出发，通向完整的 AdS/CFT 对应，包括通过 AdS 中的黑洞实现的有限温度推广，以及现代观点——即时空几何和引力可能从边界 CFT 中的量子纠缠中涌现。

Conclusion: Holography, exemplified by AdS/CFT, provides a profound link between quantum field theory and quantum gravity, where symmetry principles and entanglement structure serve as the bridge between a gravitational bulk and a non-gravitational boundary. These notes lay the groundwork for understanding how gravity can be emergent rather than fundamental.
\n\n
以 AdS/CFT 为代表的全息原理在量子场论与量子引力之间建立了深刻联系，其中对称性原理和纠缠结构构成了引力体与无引力边界之间的桥梁。这些讲义为理解引力如何是涌现的而非基本的奠定了基础。

Abstract: These are course notes for the 'Introduction to holography' Master level course at University of Cologne. The goal of the course is to give a pedogogical introduction to holography. Holography is a popular approach to quantum gravity, in which a theory of gravity can be described by a lower-dimensional boundary theory that itself has no gravity. The most concrete known example of a holographic model is the AdS/CFT correspondence, where the gravitational theory has a negative cosmological constant (the universe is asymptotically Anti-de Sitter) and the boundary theory is a conformal field theory. Symmetry plays a very important role in this duality. We therefore start the course with a review of Poincaré symmetry in quantum field theory, before moving on in the second chapter to conformal symmetry in conformally invariant quantum field theories or CFT's. Then we move to the basics of AdS physics in chapters 3 and 4, which will already reveal hints to the existence of a duality with CFT. After gathering the basic ingredients (CFT and AdS), in the second half of the course we are ready to formulate the AdS/CFT correspondence (chapter 5), including finite temperature AdS/CFT (chapter 6), which involves black holes and their thermodynamics in the gravitational theory (chapter 7). We end the course with an introduction to entanglement in AdS/CFT and the origin of statements that 'gravity emerges from entanglement' in holography.

</details>


### [33] [Discrete \texorpdfstring{$θ$}{theta} Projection: A Gauge-Protected Solution to the Strong CP Problem Without Axions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05195)
*Sameer Ahmad Mir,Bobby Eka Gunara,Mir Faizal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper proposes "Discrete theta Projection," a novel axionless mechanism to solve the strong CP problem by gauging a discrete $Z_N$ subgroup of the $\theta$-angle shift symmetry. This orbifolds the QCD path integral, restricting topological sectors and dynamically selecting the vacuum closest to CP conservation, enforcing $|\bar{\theta}| \leq \pi/N$. The setup is radiatively and gravitationally stable due to higher-form/two-group symmetries with integer-quantized couplings, predicts suppressed neutron EDM ($\propto 1/N$), no axion signals, and distinctive lattice signatures.
\n\n
本文提出了一种名为“离散θ投影”（Discrete theta Projection）的新机制，通过规范θ角平移对称性的离散子群$Z_N$来无轴子地解决强CP问题。该机制通过对QCD路径积分进行轨形化（orbifold），限制拓扑扇区，并动态选择最接近CP守恒点的真空，从而强制满足$|\bar{\theta}| \leq \pi/N$。该构造借助高形式/二群（higher-form/two-group）对称性及整数量子化耦合，具有辐射和引力稳定性，预言中子电偶极矩被压低（$\propto 1/N$）、无轴子信号，并具有独特的格点可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The strong CP problem arises because experimental bounds on the neutron electric dipole moment require the physical QCD vacuum angle $\bar{\theta}$ to be unnaturally small ($\lesssim 10^{-10}$). Traditional Peccei-Quinn axion solutions introduce an approximate global $U(1)$ symmetry that is expected to be broken by quantum gravity effects and are tightly constrained by astrophysical and cosmological observations. This motivates the search for alternative, axionless mechanisms that are robust against gravitational corrections and do not rely on global symmetries.
\n\n
强CP问题源于中子电偶极矩的实验限制要求QCD物理真空角$\bar{\theta}$异常小（$\lesssim 10^{-10}$）。传统的Peccei-Quinn轴子方案引入一个近似的整体$U(1)$对称性，但该对称性预期会被量子引力效应破坏，且受到天体物理与宇宙学观测的严格限制。这促使人们寻找不依赖整体对称性、对引力修正鲁棒的无轴子替代机制。

Method: The authors gauge a finite cyclic subgroup $Z_N$ of the continuous $2\pi$ shift symmetry of the QCD $\theta$-angle. This couples QCD to a compact, local, gapped topological sector, effectively orbifolding the path integral so that configurations with $\theta$ differing by $2\pi/N$ are identified. Only instanton sectors with topological charge in $Z_N$ contribute. The vacuum energy becomes the lower envelope of orbifold images, dynamically minimizing $|\bar{\theta}|$. The construction is formalized using higher-form and two-group global symmetries, with integer-quantized couplings fixed by anomaly inflow from a 5D bulk, ensuring consistency with gauge-gravity constraints and forbidding continuous renormalization of $\theta$.
\n\n
作者规范了QCD θ角连续$2\pi$平移对称性的一个有限循环子群$Z_N$。这将QCD耦合到一个紧致、局域且能隙化的拓扑扇区，有效对路径积分进行轨形化，使得相差$2\pi/N$的θ构型被等同。仅允许拓扑荷属于$Z_N$的瞬子扇区贡献。真空能成为轨形像的下包络线，从而动态最小化$|\bar{\theta}|$。该构造通过高形式（higher-form）与二群（two-group）全局对称性形式化，其整数量子化耦合由五维体中的反常流入（anomaly inflow）固定，确保满足规范-引力一致性条件，并禁止θ的连续重整化。

Result: The theory dynamically enforces $|\bar{\theta}| \leq \pi/N$ without fine-tuning. It predicts a neutron EDM suppressed by $1/N$, absence of axion phenomenology (no axion particles, domain walls, or isocurvature perturbations), and distinctive nonperturbative lattice signatures: piecewise-analytic $\theta$-dependence of the vacuum energy with cusps at $\theta = (2k+1)\pi/N$, and global curvature scaling as $1/N^2$. The framework is UV-completable via constructions like discrete clockwork chains that generate large effective $N$ while preserving integrality and anomaly consistency.
\n\n
该理论无需精细调节即可动态强制$|\bar{\theta}| \leq \pi/N$。它预言中子电偶极矩被$1/N$压低，不存在轴子现象学（无轴子粒子、畴壁或等曲率扰动），并具有独特的非微扰格点信号：真空能对θ的依赖呈分段解析形式，在$\theta = (2k+1)\pi/N$处出现尖点，且整体曲率按$1/N^2$标度。该框架可通过离散钟表链（discrete clockwork chains）等紫外完备构造实现，生成大的有效$N$，同时保持耦合整数性和反常一致性。

Conclusion: Discrete theta Projection provides a theoretically robust, axionless solution to the strong CP problem that avoids the pitfalls of global symmetries by using gauged discrete shifts protected by higher-form/two-group structures. It is consistent with quantum gravity, radiatively stable, and makes concrete predictions testable via neutron EDM experiments and lattice QCD simulations.
\n\n
离散θ投影（Discrete theta Projection）通过利用受高形式/二群结构保护的规范离散平移，提供了一种理论上稳健、无轴子的强CP问题解决方案，避免了整体对称性的缺陷。该方案与量子引力相容、具有辐射稳定性，并可通过中子电偶极矩实验和格点QCD模拟进行具体检验。

Abstract: We address the strong CP problem: why the physical QCD angle theta-bar must be extraordinarily small given the stringent bounds on the neutron electric dipole moment. Peccei-Quinn axion models can relax theta-bar dynamically, but rely on an approximate global symmetry expected to be violated by quantum gravity and face severe astrophysical and cosmological constraints. We propose Discrete theta Projection, an axionless, gauge-protected resolution obtained by gauging a finite cyclic subgroup $Z_N $of the $2π$ shift symmetry of theta. Coupling QCD to a compact, local and gapped topological sector orbifolds the path integral, identifying theta values that differ by $2π/N$ and admitting only instanton sectors whose topological charge lies in $Z_N$. In the large four-volume limit the vacuum energy becomes the lower envelope of the orbifold images, so the theory dynamically selects the branch closest to the CP-symmetric point, enforcing $|\barθ| \le π/N$ without assuming any prior smallness. Because the discrete shift is gauged, continuous renormalization of theta is forbidden; the construction can be formulated via higher-form/two-group structure with integer-quantized couplings fixed by anomaly inflow, ensuring radiative and gravitational stability and satisfying mixed gauge-gravity consistency conditions. The framework predicts a neutron EDM suppressed by $1/N$, no axion signatures, no domain-wall/isocurvature issues, and lattice diagnostics: piecewise-analytic theta dependence with cusps at odd fractions of the reduced period and a global curvature scaling as $1/N^2$. We provide the EFT construction, a nonperturbative proof of vacuum projection, a full anomaly analysis, and UV embeddings (including discrete clockwork chains) that generate large effective N while preserving integrality and consistency throughout.

### [34] [3d-3d correspondence and abelian flat connection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05236)
*Hee-Joong Chung*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates that the homological block of a knot complement in $S^3$ for $G_{\mathbb{C}} = SL(2,\mathbb{C})$ can be realized as the half-index of a 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric theory, using an inverted Habiro series representation. 本文证明了对于 $G_{\\mathbb{C}} = SL(2,\\mathbb{C})$，$S^3$ 中纽结补空间的同调块（homological block）可通过倒置的 Habiro 级数表示为一个三维 $\\mathcal{N}=2$ 超对称理论的半指标（half-index）。此外，通过在半指标积分中选取特定极点，可还原出着色 Jones 多项式（colored Jones polynomial）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the desire to connect topological invariants of 3-manifolds—specifically homological blocks arising in complex Chern–Simons theory—with physical quantities in 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric gauge theories, thereby deepening the bridge between quantum topology and supersymmetric field theory. The authors aim to realize the homological block as a half-index, which encodes boundary conditions and BPS spectra, and to relate it to well-known knot polynomials like the colored Jones polynomial.
\n\n
该工作的动机源于将三维流形的拓扑不变量（特别是复 Chern–Simons 理论中出现的同调块）与三维 $\\mathcal{N}=2$ 超对称规范理论中的物理量联系起来，从而深化量子拓扑与超对称场论之间的桥梁。作者旨在将同调块实现为半指标（其编码边界条件与 BPS 谱），并将其与如着色 Jones 多项式等已知纽结多项式关联起来。

Method: The authors express the homological block of a knot complement as an inverted Habiro series—a formal power series related to quantum invariants—and identify this series with the half-index of a 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ theory. Conclusion: The results suggest a general correspondence between homological blocks of knot complements and half-indices of 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ theories, extendable beyond the examples studied. Abstract: We realize a homological block of a knot complement in $S^3$ for $G_{\mathbb{C}}=SL(2,\mathbb{C})$ as a half-index of a 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ theory via an expression of the homological block as an inverted Habiro series by working out some examples, which we expect to extend to general knots. ### [35] [Canonical Quantisation of Bound and Unbound WQFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05237)
*Riccardo Gonzo,Gustav Mogull*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper develops a canonical quantization approach to Worldline Quantum Field Theory (WQFT) that avoids the Schwinger-Keldysh path integral, enabling unified treatment of both scattering and bound states in the classical two-body problem. By quantizing Hamilton's equations for two charged particles interacting via a scalar field—either in flat space (post-Lorentzian expansion) or around a background (self-force expansion)—the authors compute matrix elements of the operator $\hat{N}(t,t_0) = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}(t,t_0)$. This yields gauge-invariant results for 1SF scattering up to 3PL order and corresponding bound-orbit observables, establishing a unified operator framework for conservative and radiative dynamics applicable to both gravity and electromagnetism.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于正则量子化的Worldline Quantum Field Theory (WQFT)方法，摒弃了Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分，从而统一处理经典二体问题中的散射态与束缚态。作者对通过标量场相互作用的两个带电粒子的哈密顿方程进行量子化——在平直空间中采用post-Lorentzian (PL)展开，在非零背景附近采用self-force (SF)展开——并计算算符$\hat{N}(t,t_0) = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}(t,t_0)$的矩阵元。由此获得了1SF散射动力学在3PL阶次内的规范不变矩阵元，以及对应的束缚轨道矩阵元，构建了一个统一的算符框架来描述双星系统的保守性与辐射性动力学，并可自然推广至引力和电磁相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional WQFT formulations rely on the Schwinger-Keldysh in-in path integral, which is well-suited for real-time evolution but can obscure the connection to canonical structures and operator-based observables. Moreover, existing approaches often treat scattering and bound orbits separately, lacking a unified framework for both conservative and radiative dynamics. The authors aim to develop a canonical quantization method that directly accesses the Magnus series and the operator $\hat{N}(t,t_0)$, thereby providing a coherent, gauge-invariant description applicable across different regimes (scattering vs. bound) and physical theories (electromagnetism and gravity).
\n\n
传统的WQFT形式依赖于Schwinger-Keldysh in-in路径积分，虽适用于实时演化，但可能掩盖了与正则结构及基于算符的可观测量之间的联系。此外，现有方法通常将散射与束缚轨道分开处理，缺乏一个统一框架来同时描述保守性和辐射性动力学。作者旨在发展一种正则量子化方法，直接获取Magnus级数和算符$\hat{N}(t,t_0)$，从而提供一个在不同物理情形（散射vs.束缚）和理论（电磁学与引力）下均适用的、规范不变的统一描述。

Method: The authors employ canonical quantization of Hamilton’s equations for a system of two point particles coupled to a scalar field. They consider two perturbative regimes: (i) post-Lorentzian (PL) expansion in flat spacetime for scattering processes, and (ii) self-force (SF) expansion around a non-trivial background for bound orbits. Instead of using the Schwinger-Keldysh formalism, they construct the time-evolution operator $\hat{U}(t,t_0)$ and define $\hat{N}(t,t_0) = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}(t,t_0)$, whose matrix elements are computed via the Magnus expansion. This operator-based approach allows them to compute finite-time (bound) and infinite-time (scattering) transition amplitudes while maintaining manifest gauge invariance.
\n\n
作者对两个点粒子与标量场耦合系统的哈密顿方程进行正则量子化。他们考虑两种微扰机制：(i) 在平直时空中的post-Lorentzian (PL)展开，用于散射过程；(ii) 在非平凡背景附近的self-force (SF)展开，用于束缚轨道。他们摒弃Schwinger-Keldysh形式，转而构造时间演化算符$\hat{U}(t,t_0)$，并定义$\hat{N}(t,t_0) = -i\hbar \log \hat{U}(t,t_0)$，其矩阵元通过Magnus展开计算。这种基于算符的方法可在保持显式规范不变性的同时，计算有限时间（束缚）和无限时间（散射）的跃迁振幅。

Result: The paper computes a complete set of gauge-invariant $\hat{N}$-matrix elements for 1SF scattering dynamics up to third post-Lorentzian (3PL) order, as well as analogous matrix elements for bound orbits. These matrix elements encode physical observables such as scattering angles, binding energy shifts, and radiative losses. The results demonstrate that the $\hat{N}$ operator unifies the description of conservative (time-symmetric) and radiative (dissipative) effects within a single quantum-mechanical framework, and the formalism naturally extends to both electromagnetic and gravitational interactions.
\n\n
本文计算了1SF散射动力学在三阶post-Lorentzian (3PL)精度下的完整规范不变$\hat{N}$矩阵元集合，以及对应的束缚轨道矩阵元。这些矩阵元编码了散射角、结合能修正和辐射损耗等物理可观测量。结果表明，$\hat{N}$算符在一个统一的量子力学框架内同时描述了保守性（时间对称）和辐射性（耗散）效应，且该形式可自然推广至电磁与引力相互作用。

Conclusion: The canonical quantization approach to WQFT presented here provides a powerful, unified operator framework for classical binary dynamics, bridging scattering and bound-state problems while maintaining gauge invariance and incorporating both conservative and radiative effects. By avoiding the Schwinger-Keldysh path integral and leveraging the Magnus expansion of $\hat{N}(t,t_0)$, the method offers a transparent connection to Hamiltonian mechanics and facilitates systematic high-order calculations. Its applicability to both scalar-mediated interactions and, by extension, gravity and electromagnetism, suggests broad utility in precision studies of binary systems in effective field theory and gravitational wave physics.
\n\n
本文提出的WQFT正则量子化方法为经典双星动力学提供了一个强大而统一的算符框架，能够无缝衔接散射与束缚态问题，在保持规范不变性的同时纳入保守性与辐射性效应。通过避免使用Schwinger-Keldysh路径积分并利用$\hat{N}(t,t_0)$的Magnus展开，该方法清晰地连接了哈密顿力学，并便于系统性高阶计算。其对标量媒介相互作用的有效性，以及向引力和电磁学的自然推广，预示其在有效场论和引力波物理中对双星系统的高精度研究具有广泛应用前景。

Abstract: Using canonical quantisation, and eschewing the Schwinger-Keldysh path integral, we derive a version of the Worldline Quantum Field Theory (WQFT) formalism suitable for both scattering and bound configurations of the classical two-body problem. Focusing on a pair of charged particles interacting via a scalar field, we quantise Hamilton's equations both in flat space and around a non-zero background, perturbing in post-Lorentzian (PL) and self-force (SF) expansions respectively. Our quantisation procedure provides access to the Magnus series, and is perfectly suited for computing matrix elements of $\hat{N}(t,t_0)=- i \hbar \log\hat{U}(t,t_0)$, both with and without external scalar states, for finite time intervals (bound orbits) and infinite time intervals (scattering). Doing so, we provide a complete set of gauge-invariant matrix elements describing the 1SF scattering dynamics up to 3PL order, and corresponding matrix elements for bound orbits. We also demonstrate how $\hat{N}$-matrix elements encode physical observables, providing a unified operator-based framework for conservative and radiative dynamics of binary systems. The new WQFT formalism generalises naturally to both gravity and electromagnetism.

</details>


### [36] [Gauge-string duality, monomial bases and graph determinants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05259)
*Garreth Kemp,Sanjaye Ramgoolam*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper introduces degeneracy graphs to study sequences of subalgebras in finite-dimensional commutative associative semisimple algebras $\mathcal{A}$, constructed by incrementally adjoining generators. These graphs encode projectors at each layer and enable a monomial basis construction for $\mathcal{A}$. The authors prove consistency with projector counting, explicitly construct projectors for 1- and 2-layer cases, and provide computational evidence (including a conjectured determinant formula) for the invertibility of the change-of-basis matrix between monomials and projectors. Applications include constructing matrix units in non-commutative semisimple algebras, relevant to AdS/CFT and quantum information theory.
\n\n
本文引入退化图（degeneracy graphs）来研究有限维交换结合半单代数 $\mathcal{A}$ 中通过逐层添加生成元所构造的子代数序列。这些图编码了每一层的投影算子（projectors），并由此导出 $\mathcal{A}$ 的单项式基（monomial basis）。作者证明了该构造与投影算子计数一致，显式构造了一层和两层情形下的投影算子，并通过计算证据（包括一个猜想的行列式公式）支持单项式基与投影算子基之间变换矩阵的可逆性。该方法在非交换半单代数中矩阵单位（matrix units）的构造中有应用，与 AdS/CFT 对应和量子信息理论相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivated by questions at the interface of AdS/CFT correspondence and quantum information theory, the paper seeks algebraic tools to analyze structures involving sequences of subalgebras generated by incrementally adding elements. Understanding projectors in such nested subalgebras is crucial for constructing orthogonal bases of gauge-invariant operators and for applications in quantum information, where projector decompositions underpin measurement and state discrimination protocols.
\n\n
受 AdS/CFT 对应与量子信息理论交叉问题的驱动，本文旨在发展代数工具以分析通过逐层添加元素所生成的子代数序列结构。理解此类嵌套子代数中的投影算子对构造规范不变算子的正交基至关重要，并且在量子信息理论中具有应用价值，因为投影算子分解是测量与态区分协议的基础。

Method: The authors define degeneracy graphs—layered tree graphs whose nodes represent projectors in successive subalgebras obtained by adjoining one generator at a time. Each node is labeled by formal variables representing eigenvalues of the newly adjoined generator. Using combinatorial properties of these graphs, they construct a linear basis of $\mathcal{A}$ from monomials in the generators. They verify consistency with the dimension of the projector space, explicitly build projectors for 1- and 2-layer cases, and compute the determinant of the change-of-basis matrix between monomials and projectors. In the 1-layer case, this determinant is a Vandermonde determinant; for general layers, they conjecture a closed-form non-vanishing formula supported by extensive numerical evidence.
\n\n
作者定义了退化图——一种分层树图，其节点表示通过逐次添加一个生成元所得到的连续子代数中的投影算子。每个节点用形式变量标记，这些变量对应于新添加生成元的本征值。利用这些图的组合性质，他们从生成元的单项式构造出 $\mathcal{A}$ 的线性基。他们验证了该构造与投影算子空间维度的一致性，显式构建了一层和两层情形下的投影算子，并计算了单项式基与投影算子基之间变换矩阵的行列式。在一层情形下，该行列式为范德蒙德（Vandermonde）行列式；对于一般层数，他们基于大量数值证据提出一个非零行列式的闭式猜想公式。

Result: The paper establishes a systematic method to construct a monomial basis for $\mathcal{A}$ using degeneracy graphs, proves its compatibility with the expected number of projectors, and provides explicit projector formulas for 1- and 2-layer cases. It shows that the change-of-basis matrix is invertible: exactly via Vandermonde determinant in the 1-layer case, and conjecturally via a general non-vanishing determinant formula supported by computation. Examples include centers of symmetric group algebras and algebras generated by Jucys–Murphy elements.
\n\n
本文建立了一种利用退化图系统构造 $\mathcal{A}$ 单项式基的方法，证明了其与预期投影算子数量的兼容性，并给出了一层和两层情形下投影算子的显式公式。文章证明了基变换矩阵的可逆性：在一层情形下通过范德蒙德行列式严格成立，在一般情形下则通过计算支持一个非零行列式的猜想公式。示例包括对称群代数的中心以及由 Jucys–Murphy 元素生成的极大交换子代数。

Conclusion: The degeneracy graph framework provides a powerful combinatorial-algebraic tool for constructing bases and projectors in commutative semisimple algebras built from incremental generators. This approach bridges representation theory, algebraic combinatorics, and quantum information, offering algorithmic pathways to matrix units in non-commutative semisimple algebras—key for constructing orthogonal multi-trace gauge-invariant operators in AdS/CFT and for quantum state engineering.
\n\n
退化图框架为在由增量生成元构建的交换半单代数中构造基与投影算子提供了一种强有力的组合-代数工具。该方法连接了表示论、代数组合学与量子信息理论，为非交换半单代数中矩阵单位的算法化构造提供了路径——这对 AdS/CFT 中正交多迹规范不变算子的构造以及量子态工程具有重要意义。

Abstract: Questions at the intersection of the AdS/CFT correspondence and quantum information theory motivate the study of projectors in sequences of subalgebras of finite-dimensional commutative associative semisimple algebras $\mathcal{A}$, obtained by incrementally adjoining one generator at each step to produce a non-linear generating set for $\mathcal{A}$. We define degeneracy graphs, which are finite layered tree graphs whose nodes represent projectors in the successive subalgebras. Using combinatorial properties of the degeneracy graph, we give a simple formula for constructing a linear basis of $\mathcal{A}$ in terms of monomials in the generators.The nodes can be labelled by formal variables corresponding to the eigenvalues of the generators added at each layer. We prove that the construction is compatible with the required counting of projectors in $\mathcal{A}$, and give explicit constructions of the projectors in terms of the monomials, in the cases of one- and two-layer degeneracy graphs with arbitrary numbers of nodes. More generally, we provide extensive computational evidence for the invertibility of the matrix relating the proposed monomial basis to the projector basis, by evaluating its determinant. In the 1-layer case, this is a Vandermonde determinant. A simple formula for the non-vanishing determinant in the general layer case is conjectured and supported by the computational data. The construction is illustrated with examples including centres of symmetric group algebras and maximally commuting subalgebras generated by JucysMurphy elements. We outline applications of the monomial basis to algorithms for constructing matrix units in non-commutative semisimple algebras, with relevance to orthogonal bases of multi-matrix gauge-invariant operators and to quantum information theory.

</details>


### [37] [7D (non-)susy vacua & DWs from dynamical open strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05470)
*Valentina Bevilacqua,Giuseppe Dibitetto,Giuseppe Sudano*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates warped compactifications of massive type IIA supergravity on $S^3$ with spacetime-filling O6/D6 sources, extending the 7D half-maximal gauged supergravity description by incorporating open string degrees of freedom (scalars and fluxes). This is achieved by coupling extra vector multiplets to the gravity multiplet and modifying the embedding tensor. The resulting scalar potential yields new AdS$_7$ vacua, both supersymmetric and non-supersymmetric, and the authors construct domain wall solutions interpolating between these vacua.
\n\n
本文研究了具有时空填充O6/D6源的massive type IIA超引力在$S^3$上的warped紧化，通过引入开弦自由度（标量和通量）扩展了7维半极大规范超引力描述。该扩展通过将额外的vector multiplet与gravity multiplet耦合并修改embedding tensor实现。所得标量势展现出新的AdS$_7$真空解（包括超对称和非超对称情形），作者还构造了在不同真空之间插值的domain wall解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding how open string degrees of freedom—specifically scalars and fluxes associated with spacetime-filling O6/D6 sources—affect the effective 7D half-maximal gauged supergravity description of warped compactifications of massive type IIA supergravity. While such compactifications are known to admit a 7D supergravity dual, the inclusion of open string sectors introduces new dynamics that require extending the standard framework via additional vector multiplets and a generalized embedding tensor.
\n\n
动机源于理解开弦自由度（特别是与时空填充O6/D6源相关的标量和通量）如何影响massive type IIA超引力warped紧化的有效7维半极大规范超引力描述。尽管这类紧化已知具有7维超引力对偶，但开弦扇区的引入带来了新动力学，需通过额外的vector multiplet和广义embedding tensor来扩展标准框架。

Method: The authors extend the 7D half-maximal gauged supergravity by coupling the gravity multiplet to additional vector multiplets, which encode the open string degrees of freedom. They generalize the embedding tensor to include new components that capture the gauging induced by the D6/O6 sources and their associated fluxes. Using this extended framework, they derive the scalar potential and analyze its critical points to identify new AdS$_7$ vacua. They then solve the BPS and non-BPS equations for domain walls, obtaining both analytical and numerical interpolating solutions between pairs of vacua.
\n\n
作者通过将gravity multiplet与额外的vector multiplet耦合来扩展7维半极大规范超引力，这些vector multiplet编码了开弦自由度。他们推广了embedding tensor以包含由D6/O6源及其相关通量诱导的新规范分量。利用这一扩展框架，他们推导出标量势并分析其临界点以识别新的AdS$_7$真空。随后求解domain wall的BPS与非BPS方程，得到在不同真空对之间插值的解析和数值解。

Result: The extended 7D supergravity model yields novel AdS$_7$ vacuum solutions, including both supersymmetric and non-supersymmetric cases. The authors successfully construct domain wall solutions—both analytically (in certain limits) and numerically—that interpolate between these distinct vacua, demonstrating the rich structure of the scalar potential landscape arising from the inclusion of open string degrees of freedom.
\n\n
所构建的扩展7维超引力模型产生了新的AdS$_7$真空解，包括超对称和非超对称情形。作者成功构造了在这些不同真空之间插值的domain wall解——在特定极限下获得解析解，并通过数值方法得到更一般的解，展示了因引入开弦自由度而产生的标量势景观的丰富结构。

Conclusion: Incorporating open string degrees of freedom into warped compactifications of massive type IIA supergravity significantly enriches the low-energy 7D effective theory, leading to new AdS$_7$ vacua and interpolating domain wall solutions. This demonstrates that the standard half-maximal gauged supergravity framework must be extended with extra vector multiplets and a modified embedding tensor to fully capture the physics of spacetime-filling brane sources.
\n\n
将开弦自由度纳入massive type IIA超引力的warped紧化显著丰富了低能7维有效理论，导致新的AdS$_7$真空和插值domain wall解的出现。这表明，为完整描述时空填充brane源的物理，标准的半极大规范超引力框架必须通过额外的vector multiplet和修正的embedding tensor加以扩展。

Abstract: Warped compactifications of massive type IIA supergravity on a 3-sphere with spacetime-filling O6/D6 sources are known to admit a half-maximal gauged supergravity description in 7D. We study the effect of introducing open string degrees of freedom (scalars and fluxes) in such dimensional reductions, associated with the spacetime-filling sources. From the 7D supergravity point of view, this can be realized by coupling the gravity multiplet with extra vector multiplets and adding new components to the embedding tensor describing the gauging. The scalar potential of the underlying theory exhibits novel AdS7 vacuum solutions, with and without supersymmetry. Finally, we explore the net of domain wall solutions interpolating between the different pairs of vacua, and present analytical as well as numerical solutions.

</details>


### [38] [Scattering amplitudes in dimensionless quadratic gravity coupled to QED](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05476)
*I. F. Cunha,A. C. Lehum*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper computes tree-level $2\to2$ scattering amplitudes in agravity—a scale-invariant, renormalizable quadratic gravity theory—coupled to Abelian gauge fields and matter (charged fermions and scalars). It provides analytic expressions for unpolarized squared matrix elements across multiple channels, includes photon–graviton interference, confirms gauge independence, and reveals universal ultra-Planckian differential cross sections scaling as $d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/s$.
\n\n
本文计算了在agravity（一种尺度不变、可重整化的二次量子引力理论）与Abelian规范场及物质（带电费米子和标量）耦合下的树图阶$2\to2$散射振幅。文章给出了多个散射道的无极化平方矩阵元的解析表达式，包含了光子–引力子干涉项，验证了结果对引力规范固定参数的独立性，并揭示了微分截面在超普朗克能区具有普适标度律$d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/s$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding how higher-derivative gravity modifies standard QED processes at ultra-Planckian energies is crucial for probing the UV consistency of quantum gravity theories with matter. Agravity, being renormalizable and scale-invariant, offers a controlled framework to study such effects without introducing new mass scales. Previous studies often neglected photon–graviton interference or focused solely on graviton exchange; this work aims to provide a complete amplitude-level description that includes all relevant tree-level contributions and clarifies universal high-energy behavior.
\n\n
理解高阶导数引力如何在超普朗克能量下修正标准QED过程，对于探测量子引力理论与物质耦合时的紫外（UV）一致性至关重要。Agravity因其可重整性和尺度不变性，提供了一个不含新质量标度的可控框架来研究此类效应。以往研究常忽略光子–引力子干涉或仅关注纯引力子交换；本文旨在提供一个包含所有相关树图贡献的完整振幅级描述，并阐明普适的高能行为。

Method: The authors compute tree-level $2\to2$ scattering amplitudes in a theory combining agravity (with a $1/p^4$ graviton propagator from quadratic curvature terms) and Abelian gauge theory. They consider all combinations of external charged fermions, scalars, and photons, evaluating Feynman diagrams involving both graviton and photon exchange, as well as their interference. Unpolarized squared matrix elements are derived analytically using standard spinor and polarization sum techniques. The gravitational gauge-fixing dependence is explicitly checked and shown to cancel, ensuring physical results. High-energy asymptotics are extracted by analyzing the Mandelstam variable $s$ dependence.
\n\n
作者在结合agravity（其引力子传播子因曲率平方项而呈$1/p^4$形式）与Abelian规范理论的框架下，计算树图阶$2\to2$散射振幅。他们考虑所有由带电费米子、标量和光子组成的外态组合，计算包含引力子交换、光子交换及其干涉项的费曼图。利用标准旋量与极化求和技巧，解析推导出无极化平方矩阵元。显式检验了引力规范固定参数的依赖性并证明其抵消，确保结果物理。通过分析Mandelstam变量$s$的依赖关系提取高能渐近行为。

Result: The paper obtains compact analytic formulas for unpolarized squared matrix elements across seven scattering channels: $\gamma\gamma$, $ff$, $f\gamma$, $\phi f$, $\phi\gamma$, $\phi\phi$, and annihilation. All amplitudes exhibit forward/backward peaks due to the $1/p^4$ graviton propagator. Crucially, photon–graviton interference is systematically included and shown not to spoil gauge independence. The differential cross sections universally scale as $d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/s$ in the ultra-Planckian limit ($s \gg M_{\text{Pl}}^2$), reflecting the dimensionless nature of agravity couplings. This scaling holds across all matter content considered.
\n\n
本文获得了七个散射道（$\gamma\gamma$、$ff$、$f\gamma$、$\phi f$、$\phi\gamma$、$\phi\phi$及湮灭道）的无极化平方矩阵元的简洁解析公式。所有振幅因$1/p^4$引力子传播子而呈现前向/后向增强。关键的是，系统地包含了光子–引力子干涉项，并证明其不破坏规范独立性。在超普朗克极限（$s \gg M_{\text{Pl}}^2$）下，微分截面普适地满足$d\sigma/d\Omega \propto 1/s$，反映了agravity耦合的无量纲特性。该标度律对所有考虑的物质内容均成立。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that agravity induces universal modifications to QED-like scattering at ultra-Planckian energies, characterized by $1/s$ differential cross sections and robust interference effects. These analytic results serve as foundational building blocks for future investigations into infrared (IR) safety, unitarity bounds, and the consistency of matter coupling in higher-derivative quantum gravity. The explicit gauge independence confirms the reliability of the amplitude computations within the agravity framework.
\n\n
本研究表明，agravity在超普朗克能区对类QED散射引入了普适修正，其特征为$1/s$微分截面和稳健的干涉效应。这些解析结果为未来研究红外（IR）安全性、幺正性界以及高阶导数量子引力中物质耦合的一致性提供了基础构件。显式的规范独立性验证了在agravity框架内振幅计算的可靠性。

Abstract: We study ultra-Planckian $2\to2$ scattering in an Abelian gauge theory coupled to agravity, the scale-free and renormalizable realization of quadratic quantum gravity. Focusing on charged fermions and scalars interacting with the photon and the higher-derivative graviton, we present compact analytic expressions for the unpolarized squared matrix elements for a broad set of tree-level processes, including photon--photon, fermion--fermion, fermion--photon, scalar--fermion, scalar--photon, scalar--scalar, and annihilation channels. In contrast to purely graviton-mediated analyses, we retain systematically the photon--graviton interference contributions and verify explicitly the independence of the results on the gravitational gauge-fixing parameter. The amplitudes display characteristic forward/backward enhancements associated with small momentum transfer, amplified by the $1/p^{4}$ graviton propagator, while their high-energy scaling reflects the underlying dimensionless gravitational couplings. Moreover, for all channels analyzed the corresponding differential cross sections exhibit the universal ultra-Planckian scaling $dσ/dΩ\propto 1/s$, where $s$ is the Mandelstam invariant (the squared center-of-momentum energy). Our results furnish a unified amplitude-level description of how higher-derivative gravity reshapes familiar QED scattering at ultra-Planckian energies and provide analytic building blocks for further studies of IR definitions and UV consistency in agravity with matter.

</details>

### [39] [The dark fate of ultra-faint dwarfs: gravothermal collapse in action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04508)
*Moritz S. Fischer,Hai-Bo Yu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Ultra-faint dwarf (UFD) galaxies around the Milky Way show diverse dark matter (DM) density profiles that can be explained by self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) undergoing gravothermal evolution. High-resolution SIDM N-body simulations reveal that most UFDs are likely in the post-core-expansion collapse phase, with large cross-sections ($σ/m_χ \approx 80$ cm² g⁻¹ at $v \approx 20$ km s⁻¹) consistent with observations. Tidal stripping accelerates this evolution, especially for satellites with smaller pericentres.
\n\n
围绕银河系的超微弱矮星系（Ultra-faint dwarf, UFD）展现出多样的暗物质（DM）密度轮廓，这可以通过经历引力热演化（gravothermal evolution）的自相互作用暗物质（Self-Interacting Dark Matter, SIDM）模型加以解释。高分辨率SIDM N-body模拟表明，大多数UFD很可能处于核心膨胀后的坍缩阶段，且大截面（$σ/m_χ \approx 80$ cm² g⁻¹，在速度 $v \approx 20$ km s⁻¹ 时）与观测一致。潮汐剥离加速了这一演化过程，尤其对近心距较小的卫星星系更为显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UFD galaxies are the most DM-dominated systems known, making them ideal laboratories to test non-gravitational DM physics such as self-interactions. Observations of stellar kinematics in Milky Way UFDs suggest a diversity in their central DM densities that cannot be easily explained by standard cold dark matter (CDM) models. This motivates exploring whether SIDM-induced gravothermal evolution—featuring core formation followed by collapse—can reproduce the observed diversity and constrain the DM self-interaction cross-section.
\n\n
UFD星系是目前已知暗物质占比最高的系统，使其成为检验非引力暗物质物理（如自相互作用）的理想实验室。银河系UFD中恒星运动学的观测表明其中心暗物质密度存在多样性，这难以用标准冷暗物质（Cold Dark Matter, CDM）模型轻易解释。这促使研究者探索：由SIDM引发的引力热演化（包括核心形成及后续坍缩）是否能够重现观测到的多样性，并约束暗物质自相互作用截面。

Method: The authors perform idealized high-resolution SIDM N-body simulations tailored to a Milky Way-like host halo. They model satellite halos undergoing gravothermal evolution under self-interactions and tidal effects from the host. The simulated DM density profiles of subhalos are then compared directly with observational inferences from stellar kinematics of MW UFDs. The analysis focuses on mapping the evolutionary stage—core expansion versus gravothermal collapse—based on central density and structural parameters.
\n\n
作者开展了针对类银河系主晕的高分辨率理想化SIDM N-body模拟。他们建模了受宿主潮汐影响、同时经历自相互作用驱动的引力热演化的子晕。随后将模拟得到的子晕暗物质密度轮廓与银河系UFD恒星运动学推断的观测结果直接对比。分析重点在于根据中心密度和结构参数，判断子晕所处的演化阶段——是核心膨胀阶段还是引力热坍缩阶段。

Result: The simulations show that SIDM halos exhibit a wide range of central DM densities due to varying stages of gravothermal evolution. Most observed MW UFDs match simulated halos that have passed the maximum core expansion and entered the gravothermal collapse phase, where central density increases over time. Tidal stripping enhances this evolution, particularly for satellites with small pericentre distances. The data are consistent with a large SIDM cross-section of $σ/m_χ \approx 80$ cm² g⁻¹ at $v \approx 20$ km s⁻¹.
\n\n
模拟显示，由于引力热演化阶段不同，SIDM晕表现出广泛的中心暗物质密度分布。大多数观测到的银河系UFD与那些已过最大核心膨胀、进入引力热坍缩阶段（中心密度随时间增加）的模拟晕相匹配。潮汐剥离增强了这一演化，尤其对近心距较小的卫星星系更为显著。数据与在速度 $v \approx 20$ km s⁻¹ 下具有大截面 $σ/m_χ \approx 80$ cm² g⁻¹ 的SIDM模型一致。

Conclusion: SIDM with a velocity-dependent cross-section of $\sigma/m_\chi \sim 80$ cm² g⁻¹ at dwarf galaxy velocities can naturally explain the observed diversity in DM densities of Milky Way UFDs through gravothermal evolution. The majority of UFDs are likely in the collapse phase, and tidal interactions play a crucial role in accelerating this evolution. These findings support SIDM as a viable alternative to CDM on small scales and provide a pathway to constrain DM microphysics using UFD observations.
\n\n
在矮星系速度下具有速度依赖截面（$\sigma/m_\chi \sim 80$ cm² g⁻¹）的SIDM模型可通过引力热演化自然解释银河系UFD中观测到的暗物质密度多样性。大多数UFD很可能处于坍缩阶段，而潮汐相互作用在加速该演化过程中起关键作用。这些发现支持SIDM作为小尺度上冷暗物质（CDM）的可行替代理论，并为利用UFD观测约束暗物质微观物理提供了途径。

Abstract: Ultra-faint dwarf (UFD) galaxies are a promising probe for dark matter (DM) physics as they are the most DM-dominated systems known. The Milky Way (MW) hosts many UFDs for which the properties of their DM distribution have been inferred from measurements of their stellar kinematics. If DM has self-interactions beyond gravity, the UFD halos may undergo a gravothermal evolution, giving rise to a population of galaxies with more diverse DM density profiles. We investigate DM densities of MW UFDs in self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) models, with an aim of determining the stage of gravothermal evolution for their halos. Therefore, we employ idealised high-resolution SIDM N-body simulations targeted to a MW-like system and compare the properties of simulated satellites to those of the observed UFDs. We find that the gravothermal evolution of SIDM halos produces diverse DM distributions, aligning with observations of the MW UFDs. Most of the UFDs have high DM densities, indicating that their halos have passed the period of maximum core expansion and entered the collapse phase, i.e., their central density may increase with time. The depth to which they have evolved into the gravothermal collapse may vary strongly across the satellites. This allows SIDM to account for the diversity in their DM densities. Moreover, the acceleration of the gravothermal evolution by tidal stripping goes hand-in-hand with explaining the diversity of the UFDs, as the ones with smaller pericentre distances require having evolved further into the gravothermal catastrophe. Large SIDM cross-sections of $σ/ m_χ\approx$ 80 cm$^2$ g$^{-1}$ at a velocity of $v \approx$ 20 km s$^{-1}$ are plausible, as the halo densities of MW UFDs are consistent with the gravothermal evolution predicted in SIDM, with most of them being in the collapse phase.

</details>


### [40] [Beyond21: A Global Framework for Cosmic Dawn and Reionization Within and Beyond the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04542)
*Omer Zvi Katz*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Beyond21 is a fast, open-source Python package that self-consistently models Pop II/III star formation, radiation backgrounds, and their effects on the intergalactic medium to predict observables like the global 21-cm signal, UVLFs, ionization history, and CXB. It enables rapid parameter exploration and supports modular extensions, such as millicharged dark matter scenarios.
\n\n
Beyond21 是一个快速、开源的 Python 软件包，通过自洽地建模 Pop II/III 恒星形成、辐射背景及其对星系际介质（intergalactic medium）的影响，预测全局 21-cm 信号、UV 光度函数（UVLFs）、电离历史和宇宙 X 射线背景（CXB）等可观测量。它支持快速参数探索，并具有模块化架构，可方便地扩展新物理，例如 millicharged dark matter 场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: With improving observations of the Cosmic Dawn (CD) and Epoch of Reionization (EoR), there is a growing need for unified theoretical frameworks that can consistently interpret multi-wavelength data—such as the 21-cm signal, UV luminosity functions, and X-ray background—within a single physical model. Existing tools often lack speed, modularity, or self-consistency across these observables.
\n\n
随着对 Cosmic Dawn（CD）和 Epoch of Reionization（EoR）观测的不断改进，亟需统一的理论框架，在单一物理模型内自洽地解释多波段数据（如 21-cm 信号、UV 光度函数和 X 射线背景）。现有工具往往在速度、模块化或跨可观测量的自洽性方面存在不足。

Method: Beyond21 implements a coupled evolution framework that integrates flexible prescriptions for Population II and III star formation with radiative transfer and thermal/ionization balance in the intergalactic medium. It computes the global 21-cm signal via the spin temperature evolution, UVLFs from galaxy formation models, ionization history from photon budgeting, and CXB contributions from X-ray sources. The code is written in Python, optimized for speed (~0.1 s per run on one CPU core), and designed with a modular architecture to allow easy modification of astrophysical assumptions or inclusion of new physics (e.g., millicharged dark matter).
\n\n
Beyond21 实现了一个耦合演化框架，将 Population II 和 III 恒星形成的灵活处方与星系际介质中的辐射转移及热/电离平衡相结合。它通过自旋温度演化计算全局 21-cm 信号，从星系形成模型导出 UV 光度函数（UVLFs），通过光子预算计算电离历史，并从 X 射线源计算对宇宙 X 射线背景（CXB）的贡献。该代码用 Python 编写，经过速度优化（单 CPU 核心上每次运行约 0.1 秒），并采用模块化架构，便于修改天体物理假设或引入新物理（例如 millicharged dark matter）。

Result: The pipeline successfully reproduces key observables—including the global 21-cm signal, UVLFs at high redshift, reionization history, and CXB—within a single self-consistent model. It achieves high computational efficiency, enabling extensive parameter space exploration. As a demonstration, the authors incorporate a millicharged dark matter component, showing how it modifies baryon cooling and thus the 21-cm signal through elastic scattering.
\n\n
该流程在一个自洽模型中成功复现了关键可观测量，包括全局 21-cm 信号、高红移 UV 光度函数（UVLFs）、再电离历史和宇宙 X 射线背景（CXB）。其计算效率高，支持大范围参数空间探索。作为示例，作者引入了 millicharged dark matter 成分，展示了其通过弹性散射改变重子冷却过程，从而影响 21-cm 信号。

Conclusion: Beyond21 provides a fast, flexible, and self-consistent platform for interpreting multi-messenger observations of the early universe. Its open-source and modular design makes it suitable for testing a wide range of astrophysical and particle physics scenarios, including non-standard dark matter models, against upcoming CD and EoR data.
\n\n
Beyond21 为解释早期宇宙的多信使观测提供了一个快速、灵活且自洽的平台。其开源和模块化设计使其适用于检验广泛的天体物理和粒子物理场景（包括非标准 dark matter 模型），并与即将到来的 Cosmic Dawn（CD）和 Epoch of Reionization（EoR）数据进行对比。

Abstract: Observations of the Cosmic Dawn (CD) and Epoch of Reionization (EoR) are steadily improving, opening new opportunities to study early galaxies through complementary probes. To enable consistent interpretation of these observations, we present Beyond21, a fully open-source Python package that implements flexible prescriptions for Pop II and Pop III star formation and computes the resulting radiation backgrounds and their impact on the intergalactic medium. From this coupled evolution, Beyond21 predicts the global 21-cm signal, UV luminosity functions (UVLFs), the ionization history, and the contribution to the observed cosmic X-ray background (CXB) within a single, self-consistent pipeline. A full global evolution run executes in $\sim0.1 \ {\rm s}$ on a single CPU core, enabling broad, high-resolution parameter exploration. The modular architecture facilitates straightforward modification of astrophysical prescriptions and the incorporation of new physics. As an illustrative example, we implement a scenario in which a small fraction of dark matter is millicharged, leading to baryon cooling through elastic interactions.

</details>


### [41] [Probing Dark Energy on the Moon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04841)
*Alfredo Gurrola,Robert J. Scherrer,Oem Trivedi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: A lunar laser interferometer can probe horizon-scale metric fluctuations to directly constrain the kinetic sector of the Effective Field Theory (EFT) of dark energy—specifically the operator coefficient $M_2^4$ and sound speed $c_s^2$—offering a new observational window beyond background expansion.
\n\n
月球激光干涉仪可通过探测视界尺度度规涨落，直接约束暗能量有效场论（EFT）的动能项，特别是算符系数 $M_2^4$ 和声速 $c_s^2$，从而提供超越背景膨胀历史的新观测窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Current cosmological observations primarily constrain the background expansion history of dark energy but poorly constrain the kinetic operators in the EFT of cosmic acceleration, which encode microphysical properties of scalar perturbations. A new observational probe is needed to test the internal consistency and viability of modified gravity and dark energy models.
\n\n
当前宇宙学观测主要约束暗能量的背景膨胀历史，但对宇宙加速有效场论（EFT）中描述标量扰动微观物理性质的动能算符约束很弱。需要新的观测手段来检验修改引力和暗能量模型的内部自洽性与可行性。

Method: The authors propose using a lunar laser interferometer to measure horizon-scale metric fluctuations. These fluctuations are sensitive to the kinetic sector of the EFT of dark energy, particularly through the time-dependent coefficient $M_2^4(t)$ and the associated dark energy sound speed $c_s^2 = 1 + 2M_2^4/\\bar{M}^2$, where $\\bar{M}$ is the effective Planck mass. The method leverages the fact that such interferometers can detect subtle changes in spacetime geometry on cosmological scales.
\n\n
作者提出利用月球激光干涉仪测量视界尺度的度规涨落。这些涨落对暗能量EFT的动能项敏感，特别是通过时间依赖的系数 $M_2^4(t)$ 及其关联的暗能量声速 $c_s^2 = 1 + 2M_2^4/\\bar{M}^2$（其中 $\\bar{M}$ 为有效普朗克质量）。该方法利用了此类干涉仪可探测宇宙学尺度上时空几何微小变化的能力。

Result: The analysis shows that a lunar laser interferometer can achieve direct sensitivity to the EFT kinetic coefficient $M_2^4$ and the sound speed $c_s^2$, thereby probing regions of EFT parameter space that are inaccessible to conventional probes like supernovae, BAO, or CMB, which mainly constrain the background expansion.
\n\n
分析表明，月球激光干涉仪可直接对EFT动能系数 $M_2^4$ 和声速 $c_s^2$ 产生灵敏度，从而探测传统手段（如超新星、BAO或CMB）无法触及的EFT参数空间区域——后者主要约束背景膨胀。

Conclusion: This work establishes lunar laser interferometry as a qualitatively new probe of the microphysical structure of dark energy, enabling direct tests of the kinetic sector in the EFT of cosmic acceleration and potentially ruling out or discovering classes of modified gravity models based on their perturbative consistency.
\n\n
本工作确立了月球激光干涉测量作为探测暗能量微观结构的一种全新手段，可直接检验宇宙加速EFT中的动能项，并可能基于扰动自洽性排除或发现某些修改引力模型类别。

Abstract: The effective field theory (EFT) of cosmic acceleration provides a model-independent framework for describing dark energy and modified gravity, yet many of its defining operators remain weakly constrained by existing observations. We show that measurements of horizon-scale metric fluctuations with a lunar laser interferometer can directly probe the kinetic sector of the EFT of dark energy, enabling constraints on operators governing scalar perturbation dynamics rather than only the background expansion history. In particular, we demonstrate sensitivity to the EFT kinetic coefficient $M_2^4$ and the associated sound speed of dark energy, $c_s^2$. This establishes a qualitatively new observational handle on the microphysical consistency conditions of late-time acceleration models, allowing broad regions of EFT parameter space to be probed, constrained, or potentially discovered.

### [42] [STOchastic LAttice Simulation of hybrid inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04850)
*Tomoaki Murata,Yuichiro Tada*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper studies the spatial profile of curvature perturbations in multi-waterfall hybrid inflation models using lattice simulations with the STOLAS code. It confirms consistency with the stochastic-$δN$ formalism, identifies a PDF upper bound in the Cubic potential case that suppresses PBH formation, and uses the Euler characteristic to reveal that topological defects (domain walls, cosmic strings, monopoles) are fragmented into sub-Hubble structures during inflation. Global features in the curvature perturbation for $n=1$ may offer new observational signatures of early-universe physics.
\n\n
本文利用基于随机暴胀形式的格点模拟代码STOLAS，研究了多瀑布场混合暴胀模型中曲率扰动的空间分布。结果证实其与stochastic-$δN$算法一致；在Cubic势情形下发现PDF存在上限，抑制原初黑洞（PBH）形成；并通过Euler characteristic揭示：拓扑缺陷（畴壁、宇宙弦、磁单极子）在暴胀期间被随机噪声碎裂为远小于Hubble尺度的精细结构。对于$n=1$的情形，曲率扰动中出现的全局结构可能为早期宇宙物理提供新探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how multi-field dynamics in hybrid inflation—specifically models with multiple waterfall fields—generate non-Gaussian curvature perturbations and topological defects, and how these features imprint on cosmological observables. Previous work indicated that certain inflaton potentials can suppress PBH formation via a cutoff in the PDF of curvature perturbations; this paper extends that analysis to multiple field configurations and employs topological diagnostics to probe defect evolution during inflation.
\n\n
动机在于理解混合暴胀中多场动力学（特别是含多个waterfall场的模型）如何产生非高斯曲率扰动和拓扑缺陷，以及这些特征如何印迹于宇宙学可观测量上。先前工作表明，某些inflaton势可通过曲率扰动PDF中的截断抑制原初黑洞（PBH）形成；本文将该分析推广至多种场构型，并引入拓扑诊断工具以探究暴胀期间缺陷的演化。

Method: The authors perform lattice simulations using the STOLAS code, which implements the stochastic inflation formalism to evolve coarse-grained fields beyond the Hubble scale. They consider six scenarios: combinations of $n = 1, 2, 3$ waterfall fields and two inflaton potentials (“Quadratic” and “Cubic”). They compute the probability distribution function (PDF) and power spectrum of the curvature perturbation $\\zeta$, compare them with predictions from the stochastic-$δN$ algorithm, and apply the Euler characteristic—a topological invariant—to characterize the geometry and connectivity of field configurations and $\\zeta$ maps.
\n\n
作者使用STOLAS格点模拟代码，该代码基于stochastic inflation形式对超Hubble尺度的粗粒化场进行演化。他们考察六种情形：$n = 1, 2, 3$个waterfall场分别与两种inflaton势（“Quadratic”和“Cubic”）组合。计算曲率扰动$\\zeta$的概率分布函数（PDF）和功率谱，与stochastic-$δN$算法的预言对比，并应用Euler characteristic（一种拓扑不变量）来刻画场构型和$\\zeta$分布的几何与连通性结构。

Result: The PDFs and power spectra align with the stochastic-$δN$ prediction across all cases. The Cubic potential exhibits a sharp upper bound in the PDF, consistent with prior findings, which reduces PBH abundance. The Euler characteristic analysis reveals that topological defects—domain walls ($n=1$), cosmic strings ($n=2$), and monopoles ($n=3$)—are broken into fine-scale structures during inflation due to stochastic noise, yielding correlation lengths much smaller than the Hubble radius at the critical transition point. Additionally, for $n=1$, the curvature perturbation shows global topological features absent in $n=2,3$, though their direct link to domain walls remains inconclusive.
\n\n
结果表明：所有情形下的PDF和功率谱均与stochastic-$δN$预言一致；Cubic势情形下PDF存在明显上限，与先前结果一致，可降低PBH丰度。Euler characteristic分析显示：拓扑缺陷——畴壁（$n=1$）、宇宙弦（$n=2$）和磁单极子（$n=3$）——在暴胀期间因随机噪声被碎裂为精细结构，其关联长度远小于临界相变点处的Hubble半径。此外，仅在$n=1$时，曲率扰动呈现出全局拓扑结构，而$n=2,3$则无此特征，但尚不能确定该结构是否直接源于畴壁。

Conclusion: Multi-waterfall hybrid inflation generates curvature perturbations consistent with stochastic-$δN$, but with model-dependent features like PDF cutoffs that impact PBH and halo formation. Crucially, topological defects do not persist as large-scale relics; instead, stochastic dynamics during inflation fragment them into sub-Hubble structures. The emergence of global features in $\\zeta$ for $n=1$ suggests a potential new signature of early-universe multi-field physics, accessible through topological statistics like the Euler characteristic.
\n\n
多瀑布场混合暴胀产生的曲率扰动与stochastic-$δN$一致，但具有依赖模型的特征（如PDF截断），影响PBH与晕形成。关键的是，拓扑缺陷并未作为大尺度遗迹留存；相反，暴胀期间的随机动力学会将其碎裂为亚Hubble结构。对于$n=1$，$\\zeta$中出现的全局特征暗示了早期宇宙多场物理的一种潜在新信号，可通过Euler characteristic等拓扑统计量加以探测。

Abstract: We investigate the spatial profile of the curvature perturbation generated in multi-waterfall hybrid inflation models, which are known to produce various topological defects. Using the lattice simulation code \acl{STOLAS}, based on the stochastic formalism of inflation, we analyse six cases by varying the number of waterfall fields $n$ and the functional form of the inflaton potential (``Quadratic'' and ``Cubic'' cases). Our statistical analysis shows that the \acp{PDF} and power spectra are broadly consistent with the so-called stochastic-$δN$ algorithm. The ``Cubic'' case also exhibits a characteristic upper bound in the \ac{PDF}, as discovered in our previous work, that suppresses \acl{PBH} formation while potentially affecting halo formation. Furthermore, we employ the Euler characteristic as a topological diagnostic tool to identify the structures of the waterfall fields as well as the curvature perturbation. We find that the topological defects, such as domain walls ($n=1$), cosmic strings ($n=2$), and monopoles ($n=3$), are reconnected during inflation into finer structures by the stochastic noise, making their correlation lengths much smaller than the Hubble scale at the critical point of the waterfall phase transition counterintuitively. The Euler characteristic also implies global structures of the curvature perturbation for $n=1$, though we do not conclude if they are due to the domain wall, because neither the strings ($n=2$) nor monopoles ($n=3$) leave such structures. The global structures of the curvature perturbation will provide a novel probe for the physics of the early universe.
