### [43] [Sound Mode and Scale-Dependent Growth in Two-Fluid Dynamical Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05049)
*Frans van Die,Vincent Desjacques*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper studies dynamical dark energy (DDE) using a two-fluid model that allows the equation of state to cross the phantom divide, predicting sound-wave-like perturbations in DDE. These induce scale-dependent corrections to matter growth and halo bias, detectable via galaxy power spectrum and bispectrum measurements in future surveys.
\n\n
本文使用一个双流体模型研究动力学暗能量（Dynamical Dark Energy, DDE），该模型允许状态方程平滑穿越幻影分界线，预言了DDE中存在类似声波的扰动。这些扰动在物质增长和晕偏差中引入尺度依赖性修正，可通过未来星系巡天的功率谱和双谱测量进行探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent DESI results suggest that the dark energy equation of state may cross the phantom divide ($w = -1$), motivating models beyond a cosmological constant. The authors aim to explore how such dynamical dark energy, when modeled as a two-fluid system supporting sound modes, affects structure formation—particularly through scale-dependent signatures in halo bias and growth rate that could distinguish it from $Λ$CDM.
\n\n
近期DESI结果表明暗能量状态方程可能穿越幻影分界线（$w = -1$），这激发了对超越宇宙学常数模型的研究。作者旨在探索：当动力学暗能量被建模为支持声模的双流体系统时，其如何影响结构形成——特别是通过晕偏差和增长率中的尺度依赖性信号，以区别于$Λ$CDM模型。

Method: The authors employ a two-fluid effective description of dynamical dark energy, where each fluid has its own sound speed $c_s^2$. They compute the induced scale-dependent corrections to the linear growth factor and halo bias due to DDE perturbations. Using a Fisher matrix formalism, they perform a multi-tracer forecast for the galaxy power spectrum (P) and bispectrum (B) in a survey volume $V \sim 10\, h^{-3}{\rm Gpc}^3$ at $z = 0.5 - 1$, assessing detectability of the DDE sound mode.
\n\n
作者采用动力学暗能量的双流体有效描述，其中每种流体具有各自的声速$c_s^2$。他们计算了由DDE扰动引起的线性增长因子和晕偏差的尺度依赖性修正。利用Fisher矩阵方法，对红移$z = 0.5 - 1$、体积$V \sim 10\, h^{-3}{\rm Gpc}^3$的星系巡天进行多示踪剂功率谱（P）与双谱（B）预报，评估DDE声模的可探测性。

Result: For cluster-sized halos, the scale-dependent halo bias from DDE is comparable in amplitude to that from massless neutrinos in $Λ$CDM. A P+B multi-tracer analysis can detect this effect if $c_s^2 \sim 10^{-2} - 10^{-4}$. For very low sound speeds ($c_s^2 \sim 10^{-5}$), a gravitational drag force alters the inferred growth rate by $\sim 10\%$. Higher sound speeds ($c_s^2 > 10^{-2}$) may be probed with optimal weighting to suppress shot noise.
\n\n
对于星系团尺度的晕，DDE引起的尺度依赖性晕偏差幅度与$Λ$CDM中无质量中微子效应相当。若$c_s^2 \sim 10^{-2} - 10^{-4}$，P+B多示踪剂分析可探测该效应。当声速极低（$c_s^2 \sim 10^{-5}$）时，引力拖曳力会使推断的增长率产生约10%的偏差。更高声速（$c_s^2 > 10^{-2}$）可通过最优加权方案抑制散粒噪声加以探测。

Conclusion: Dynamical dark energy with non-negligible sound speed imprints distinctive scale-dependent features in large-scale structure observables. These effects are potentially detectable with next-generation spectroscopic surveys using combined power spectrum and bispectrum analyses, offering a new observational window into the microphysical properties of dark energy through its clustering behavior.
\n\n
具有不可忽略声速的动力学暗能量会在大尺度结构观测量中留下独特的尺度依赖性特征。结合功率谱与双谱分析，下一代光谱巡天有望探测这些效应，从而通过暗能量的成团行为开辟观测其微观物理性质的新窗口。

Abstract: We investigate the effects of dynamical dark energy (DDE) on the growth of cosmic structure using a two-fluid model. This framework allows the dark energy equation of state to smoothly cross the phantom divide, in agreement with recent DESI results. In this effective description, DDE supports propagating perturbations that behave like sound waves. These perturbations induce a scale dependence in the growth of matter fluctuations and in halo bias, which can be exploited to test the dynamical nature of dark energy at the level of its fluctuations. For cluster-sized halos, the amplitude of the scale-dependent halo bias is comparable to that produced by massless neutrinos in $Λ$CDM. Using a Fisher forecast for a multi-tracer analysis of the power spectrum (P) and bispectrum (B) of galaxy number counts, we find that bispectrum information is essential to detect the scale dependence induced by the DDE sound mode. For a survey of volume $V\sim 10\, h^{-3}{\rm Gpc}^3$ at redshift $z=0.5 - 1$, a two-tracer P+B analysis could detect this scale dependence if the sound speeds of the dark energy fluids are in the range $c_s^2\sim 10^{-2} - 10^{-4}$. Lower sound speeds cause halos to experience a gravitational drag force through the excitations of sound waves. This effect impacts measurements of the growth rate inferred from cluster-sized halos at the 10\% level if one of the fluids has a very low sound speed $c_s^2\sim 10^{-5}$. Larger sound speeds $c_s^2 > 10^{-2}$ could be probed with optimal weighting schemes that reduce shot noise and increase the effective bias.

### [44] [Reassessing the SIGW Interpretation of PTA Signal: The Role of Third-Order Gravitational Waves and Implications for the PBH Overproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05191)
*Zhi-Chao Zhao,Sai Wang,Qing-Hua Zhu,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper resolves the tension between pulsar timing array (PTA) signals interpreted as scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) and overproduction of primordial black holes (PBHs) by including third-order gravitational wave contributions, which enhance the SIGW spectrum without requiring large curvature perturbations. Joint analysis of CMB, BAO, and PTA data shows that viable parameter regions alleviate PBH overproduction while remaining consistent with observations.
\n\n
本文通过引入三阶引力波贡献来增强标量诱导引力波（Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves, SIGWs）谱，从而缓解将脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）信号解释为早期宇宙曲率扰动诱导的SIGWs与原初黑洞（Primordial Black Holes, PBHs）过度产生之间的理论张力。对宇宙微波背景（CMB）、重子声学振荡（BAO）和PTA数据的联合分析表明，符合观测的参数区域能在一定程度上缓解PBH过度产生问题，同时保持模型的理论自洽性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent interpretations of the pulsar timing array (PTA) signal as second-order scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) from primordial curvature perturbations imply a large amplitude of these perturbations on small scales, which generically leads to overproduction of primordial black holes (PBHs)—inconsistent with observational constraints. This creates a theoretical tension that motivates exploring extensions of the standard second-order SIGW framework.
\n\n
近期将脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）信号解释为源于原初曲率扰动的二阶标量诱导引力波（SIGWs）的工作，暗示小尺度上曲率扰动幅度较大，而这通常会导致原初黑洞（PBHs）的过度产生，与观测限制相矛盾。这一理论张力促使作者探索标准二阶SIGW框架的扩展。

Method: The authors extend the standard second-order SIGW formalism to include third-order gravitational wave contributions, which can significantly boost the tensor power spectrum without requiring correspondingly large scalar perturbations. They perform a joint cosmological analysis using cosmic microwave background (CMB) and baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) data to constrain the energy density fraction $\\Omega_{\\rm GW}$ of cosmological gravitational waves. They then incorporate recent PTA data to further constrain the peak amplitude and frequency of the SIGW spectrum. Additionally, they test robustness by including a stochastic gravitational wave background from supermassive black hole binaries (SMBHBs).
\n\n
作者将标准的二阶SIGW形式推广至包含三阶引力波贡献，该贡献可在不显著增大标量扰动幅度的前提下显著增强引力波能谱。他们利用宇宙微波背景（CMB）和重子声学振荡（BAO）数据联合分析，对宇宙学引力波的能量密度分数 $\\Omega_{\\rm GW}$ 施加限制；随后结合近期PTA数据，进一步约束SIGW谱的峰值幅度和频率。此外，他们还通过加入超大质量黑洞双星（Supermassive Black Hole Binaries, SMBHBs）产生的随机引力波背景来检验结果的稳健性。

Result: The inclusion of third-order SIGWs allows for a larger gravitational wave amplitude at PTA frequencies while keeping the scalar power spectrum sufficiently suppressed to avoid excessive PBH formation. The combined CMB+BAO+PTA dataset identifies a parameter region where the SIGW interpretation of the PTA signal remains viable and the PBH abundance stays below observational limits. The results are robust even when a SMBHB foreground is included.
\n\n
引入三阶SIGWs后，可在PTA频段获得更大的引力波幅度，同时将标量功率谱压制到足够低的水平以避免PBH过度形成。CMB+BAO+PTA联合数据识别出一个参数区域，在该区域内PTA信号的SIGW解释依然成立，且PBH丰度低于观测上限。即使计入超大质量黑洞双星（SMBHB）前景，结果依然稳健。

Conclusion: Third-order corrections to scalar-induced gravitational waves provide a theoretically consistent mechanism to explain the PTA signal without violating PBH constraints. This extended SIGW framework reconciles early-universe cosmology with current gravitational wave observations and is testable with future high-precision experiments.
\n\n
标量诱导引力波的三阶修正提供了一种理论上自洽的机制，可在不违反PBH限制的前提下解释PTA信号。这一扩展的SIGW框架调和了早期宇宙学与当前引力波观测之间的矛盾，并可通过未来高精度实验进行检验。

Abstract: In light of recent interpretations attributing pulsar timing array (PTA) signal to second-order gravitational waves induced by linear cosmological curvature perturbations in the early universe, the overproduction of primordial black holes (PBHs) poses a theoretical tension. In this work, we address this issue through extending such a scalar-induced gravitational wave (SIGW) framework to include third-order gravitational waves, which allow for a substantial enhancement in the spectral amplitude of SIGWs. Analyzing a combined dataset from cosmic microwave background and baryon acoustic oscillations, we derive cosmological constraints on the physical energy-density fraction of cosmological gravitational waves. Further incorporating PTA data, we obtain constraints on the spectral amplitude and peak frequency of SIGWs. Our results indicate that the parameter region favored by the data combination can to some extent alleviate the PBH overproduction problem, thereby supporting the theoretical consistency of our model. Furthermore, we demonstrate the robustness of our SIGW interpretation for the PTA signal by extending the analysis to include a gravitational wave background from supermassive black hole binaries. These findings are poised for further scrutiny with future high-precision observations.

### [45] [The Bayesian view of DESI DR2: Evidence and tension in a combined analysis with CMB and supernovae across cosmological models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05472)
*Dily Duan Yi Ong,David Yallup,Will Handley*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper reanalyzes DESI DR2 data within a fully Bayesian framework using nested sampling, finding that Bayesian model comparison (via log evidence $\ln B$) generally disfavors extensions to $Λ$CDM—such as $w_0w_a$CDM—due to the Ockham's razor effect, especially when supernova datasets use corrected calibrations. A notable exception arises only with the uncorrected DES-SN5YR data, which introduces significant internal tension with DESI and artificially inflates support for dynamical dark energy.
\n\n
本文在完全贝叶斯框架下利用嵌套采样重新分析DESI DR2数据，发现贝叶斯模型比较（通过对数证据$\ln B$）通常因奥卡姆剃刀效应而不支持$Λ$CDM的扩展模型（如$w_0w_a$CDM），尤其是在超新星数据集使用校正后的定标时。唯一显著例外出现在未校正的DES-SN5YR数据中，该数据与DESI存在显著内部张力，人为夸大了对动力学暗能量的支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to address the limitations of frequentist $Δχ^2$-based model selection in cosmology, which often overstates evidence for extended models by ignoring parameter space volume penalties. The authors aim to apply a rigorous Bayesian model comparison framework—incorporating the Ockham's razor principle—to assess whether recent claims of evidence for dynamical dark energy (e.g., $w_0w_a$CDM) from DESI DR2 data are robust or driven by unaccounted systematics or dataset tensions.
\n\n
动机在于解决宇宙学中基于频繁主义$Δχ^2$的模型选择方法的局限性——该方法常因忽略参数空间体积惩罚而高估扩展模型的证据。作者旨在应用严格的贝叶斯模型比较框架（包含奥卡姆剃刀原理），以评估近期DESI DR2数据声称的动力学暗能量（如$w_0w_a$CDM）证据是否稳健，抑或由未计入的系统误差或数据集张力所驱动。

Method: The authors perform a fully Bayesian reanalysis using the unimpeded framework and PolyChord nested sampling to compute Bayesian evidences ($\mathcal{Z}$) for $Λ$CDM and seven extended cosmological models. They combine DESI DR1/DR2 BAO measurements with Planck CMB, multiple supernova compilations (Pantheon+, Union3, DES-SN5YR, DES-Dovekie), and DES-Y1 weak lensing. Model comparison is based on log Bayes factors $\ln B = \ln(\mathcal{Z}_{\text{ext}}/\mathcal{Z}_{Λ\text{CDM}})$. They also quantify internal tensions between datasets within $Λ$CDM using Gaussianized posterior overlaps.
\n\n
作者采用unimpeded框架和PolyChord嵌套采样进行完全贝叶斯重分析，计算$Λ$CDM及七个扩展宇宙学模型的贝叶斯证据（$\mathcal{Z}$）。他们联合DESI DR1/DR2的BAO测量、Planck CMB、多个超新星样本（Pantheon+、Union3、DES-SN5YR、DES-Dovekie）以及DES-Y1弱引力透镜数据。模型比较基于对数贝叶斯因子$\ln B = \ln(\mathcal{Z}_{\text{ext}}/\mathcal{Z}_{Λ\text{CDM}})$。同时，他们还在$Λ$CDM框架内通过高斯化后验重叠方法量化数据集间的内部张力。

Result: When using DESI DR2 BAO + Planck alone, the claimed $3.1σ$ frequentist preference for $w_0w_a$CDM vanishes in the Bayesian analysis ($\ln B = -0.57 \pm 0.26$, favoring $Λ$CDM). Including the corrected DES-Dovekie supernova data maintains this null result ($\ln B = -0.01 \pm 0.27$). However, using the original (uncorrected) DES-SN5YR calibration yields $\ln B = +3.32 \pm 0.27$, corresponding to a $3.07σ$ preference for $w_0w_a$CDM. This signal is traced to a $2.95σ$ tension between DES-SN5YR and DESI DR2 within $Λ$CDM, which drops to $1.96σ$ after calibration correction. Thus, the apparent evidence for dynamical dark energy is an artifact of uncorrected systematic error in DES-SN5YR.
\n\n
当仅使用DESI DR2 BAO + Planck时，声称的$3.1σ$频繁主义对$w_0w_a$CDM的偏好在贝叶斯分析中完全消失（$\ln B = -0.57 \pm 0.26$，支持$Λ$CDM）。加入校正后的DES-Dovekie超新星数据后，结果仍为零证据（$\ln B = -0.01 \pm 0.27$）。然而，若使用原始（未校正）的DES-SN5YR定标，则得到$\ln B = +3.32 \pm 0.27$，对应$3.07σ$对$w_0w_a$CDM的偏好。该信号被追溯至DES-SN5YR与DESI DR2在$Λ$CDM框架内的$2.95σ$张力，校正后降至$1.96σ$。因此，动力学暗能量的表观证据实为DES-SN5YR中未校正系统误差的人工产物。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that Bayesian model selection, which inherently penalizes model complexity, provides a more conservative and robust assessment of evidence for new physics than frequentist $Δχ^2$ methods. The apparent detection of dynamical dark energy in DESI DR2 analyses is not robust—it critically depends on the inclusion of an uncorrected supernova calibration that introduces significant internal tension. Once systematics are properly accounted for, the data strongly favor $Λ$CDM, highlighting the necessity of tension quantification and careful treatment of dataset compatibility in cosmological inference.
\n\n
研究表明，贝叶斯模型选择因其内在对模型复杂度的惩罚，相比频繁主义$Δχ^2$方法能提供对新物理证据更保守且稳健的评估。DESI DR2分析中表观的动力学暗能量探测并不稳健——其关键依赖于包含一个未校正的超新星定标，该定标引入了显著的内部张力。一旦正确处理系统误差，数据强烈支持$Λ$CDM，凸显了在宇宙学推断中量化张力并谨慎处理数据集兼容性的必要性。

Abstract: We apply the unimpeded framework to perform a fully Bayesian reanalysis of the DESI DR2 data, using nested sampling with PolyChord to compute evidences for $Λ$CDM and seven extensions across combinations of DESI DR1/DR2, Planck CMB, supernovae (Pantheon+, Union3, DES-SN5YR, DES-Dovekie), and DES-Y1 weak lensing. The Bayesian Ockham's razor penalises extended models, yielding weaker or opposite preferences compared to $Δχ^2$-based analyses. For DESI DR2 BAO combined with Planck CMB alone, the DESI collaboration's $3.1σ$ frequentist preference for $w_0w_a$CDM is eliminated entirely: we obtain ${\ln B = -0.57{\scriptstyle\pm0.26}}$, modestly favouring $Λ$CDM. Adding the corrected DES-Dovekie supernova calibration maintains this concordance (${\ln B = -0.01{\scriptstyle\pm0.27}}$). However, when the original DES-SN5YR calibration is included instead, the DESI collaboration's $4.2σ$ result survives the Bayesian Ockham penalty as a $3.07{\scriptstyle\pm0.10}\,σ$ preference (${\ln B = +3.32{\scriptstyle\pm0.27}}$). That this signal persists despite the Ockham penalty makes the role of tension quantification essential: our analysis traced the preference to the DES-SN5YR calibration error, which introduced a $2.95{\scriptstyle\pm 0.04}\,σ$ conflict with DESI DR2 within $Λ$CDM -- a tension that stands out from the grid -- reduced to $1.96{\scriptstyle\pm 0.04}\,σ$ once the calibration was corrected. With the calibration corrected, the Bayesian evidence for dynamical dark energy vanishes.

</details>


### [46] [Crunching, Bouncing, and Cyclical Cosmologies from Dark Sector Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02332)
*Marcel van der Westhuizen,Amare Abebe*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that strong non-gravitational interactions between dark matter and dark energy in flat FLRW cosmologies—modeled via a linear interaction kernel $Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$—can lead to exotic background dynamics, including a future Big Crunch or a past non-singular bounce, by allowing one dark-sector density to become negative and violate standard energy conditions. Closed-form expressions for the turnaround scale factors are derived, and a cyclic solution is shown possible in closed universes.
\n\n
本文表明，在平坦FLRW宇宙学中，通过线性相互作用核 $Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$ 描述的暗物质（DM）与暗能量（DE）之间的强非引力相互作用，可导致奇异的背景动力学行为，包括未来的大挤压（Big Crunch）或过去的非奇异反弹（bounce）。该机制允许某一暗区组分的能量密度变为负值，从而破坏标准能量条件。文中推导了转向点的解析条件，并给出了相应的极大或极小尺度因子的闭式表达式；在闭合宇宙中，同一IDE框架的特例还可实现循环宇宙场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard cosmological models assume negligible interaction between dark matter and dark energy, preserving positivity of energy densities and satisfying classical energy conditions. However, relaxing these assumptions—particularly allowing strong energy transfer that persists even when one component’s density vanishes—opens the door to exotic spacetime geometries forbidden in conventional GR-based cosmology (e.g., bounces or recollapses in flat universes). The authors aim to explore whether familiar interacting dark energy (IDE) frameworks, when extended into unphysical but mathematically consistent parameter regimes, can naturally produce such phenomena without invoking modified gravity or quantum effects.
\n\n
标准宇宙学模型假设暗物质与暗能量之间相互作用可忽略，从而保持能量密度为正并满足经典能量条件。然而，若放松这些假设——特别是允许即使某一组分密度为零时仍存在强能量转移——则可能打开通向常规广义相对论（GR）宇宙学所禁止的奇异时空几何（如平坦宇宙中的反弹或再坍缩）的大门。作者旨在探究：熟悉的相互作用暗能量（IDE）框架在扩展至虽物理上不合理但数学自洽的参数区域时，是否能自然产生此类现象，而无需引入修改引力或量子效应。

Method: The authors analyze flat Friedmann–Lemaître–Robertson–Walker (FLRW) cosmologies governed by general relativity with an interacting dark sector described by the phenomenological coupling $Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$, where $Q$ quantifies the energy transfer rate from DE to DM (or vice versa). They focus on the strong coupling regime where $δ_{\rm de} > 0$ and $δ_{\rm dm} < 0$ such that energy flows persistently from DE to DM even as $ρ_{\rm de} \to 0$, leading to $ρ_{\rm dm} < 0$ at some epoch. By solving the modified continuity equations:
$$
\\dot{ρ}_{\\rm dm} + 3Hρ_{\\rm dm} = Q, \\quad \\dot{ρ}_{\\rm de} + 3H(1+w)ρ_{\\rm de} = -Q,
$$
they identify conditions under which the total effective energy density violates the null or strong energy conditions. Analytic solutions for the scale factor $a(t)$ are obtained near extrema, yielding closed-form expressions for the maximum (Big Crunch) or minimum (bounce) scale factor $a_{\\rm max/min}$ in terms of model parameters $(δ_{\\rm dm}, δ_{\\rm de}, w)$.
\n\n
作者研究由广义相对论支配的平坦Friedmann–Lemaître–Robertson–Walker（FLRW）宇宙学，其中暗区由唯象耦合 $Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$ 描述，$Q$ 表征从暗能量（DE）到暗物质（DM）（或反之）的能量转移速率。他们聚焦于强耦合区域，其中 $δ_{\rm de} > 0$ 且 $δ_{\rm dm} < 0$，使得即使 $ρ_{\rm de} \to 0$ 时能量仍持续从DE流向DM，导致某时期 $ρ_{\rm dm} < 0$。通过求解修正的连续性方程：
$$
\\dot{ρ}_{\\rm dm} + 3Hρ_{\\rm dm} = Q, \\quad \\dot{ρ}_{\\rm de} + 3H(1+w)ρ_{\\rm de} = -Q,
$$
他们识别出总有效能量密度违反零能量条件（NEC）或强能量条件（SEC）的情形。在极值点附近获得尺度因子 $a(t)$ 的解析解，从而以模型参数 $(δ_{\\rm dm}, δ_{\\rm de}, w)$ 表达极大（大挤压）或极小（反弹）尺度因子 $a_{\\rm max/min}$ 的闭式公式。

Result: The analysis yields two key results: (i) In flat FLRW spacetimes, strong IDE interactions can induce a future Big Crunch (a maximum scale factor followed by recollapse) or a past non-singular bounce (a minimum non-zero scale factor), both of which require violation of the null energy condition due to transient negativity of one dark-sector density. Explicit analytic conditions for the existence of such turnarounds are derived, along with closed-form expressions for $a_{\\rm max}$ and $a_{\\rm min}$. (ii) In a closed ($k=+1$) universe, a specific choice of parameters within the same IDE framework can produce a cyclic cosmology with repeated bounces and crunches. These scenarios are shown to be mathematically consistent within GR, though physically disfavored by current observations.
\n\n
分析得出两个关键结果：(i) 在平坦FLRW时空中，强IDE相互作用可诱导未来的大挤压（存在极大尺度因子后发生再坍缩）或过去的非奇异反弹（存在非零极小尺度因子），二者均需因某一暗区组分密度暂时为负而破坏零能量条件（NEC）。文中推导了此类转向存在的显式解析条件，并给出了 $a_{\\rm max}$ 和 $a_{\\rm min}$ 的闭式表达式。(ii) 在闭合（$k=+1$）宇宙中，同一IDE框架下的特定参数选择可产生循环宇宙学，包含重复的反弹与挤压。这些情形在广义相对论内数学自洽，尽管当前观测认为其物理可能性较低。

Conclusion: While the strong-interaction IDE scenarios explored are observationally excluded as descriptions of our Universe, they reveal that even within standard general relativity and using conventional linear interaction kernels, exotic cosmological behaviors—such as bounces and crunches in flat space—can emerge naturally when energy conditions are violated through sign-changing dark-sector densities. This underscores the richness of the IDE parameter space and cautions against assuming energy positivity a priori in theoretical explorations of dark sector physics.
\n\n
尽管所研究的强相互作用IDE情景因与观测不符而被排除作为我们宇宙的描述，但它们揭示了：即使在标准广义相对论框架内，使用常规线性相互作用核，当暗区能量密度变号导致能量条件被破坏时，奇异宇宙学行为（如平坦空间中的反弹与挤压）也能自然出现。这凸显了IDE参数空间的丰富性，并警示在暗区物理的理论探索中不应先验地假设能量密度为正。

Abstract: We present new mechanisms that produce either a future Big Crunch turnaround or a past non-singular bounce in flat FLRW cosmologies within general relativity at the background level, driven solely by non-gravitational interactions between dark matter (DM) and dark energy (DE). We study phenomenological interacting dark energy (IDE) models based on linear kernels of the form $Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$, focusing on parameter regimes with strong energy transfer from dark energy to dark matter. In this strong interacting regime, the interaction does not vanish when one component crosses zero density, allowing one of the dark-sector densities to become negative. The resulting sign changes can violate the energy conditions required for cosmological turnarounds in a flat universe, thereby enabling either (i) a maximum scale factor followed by recollapse into a big crunch, or (ii) a minimum non-zero scale factor corresponding to a bounce. We derive analytic conditions for these turnarounds and obtain closed-form expressions for the associated maximum or minimum scale factor. We also show that, in a closed universe, a special case of the same IDE framework can be tuned to yield a cyclic scenario. Although these strong interaction scenarios are unlikely to describe the observed Universe, they provide a concrete demonstration that exotic cosmological behaviour can arise naturally in underexplored regions of the parameter space of familiar IDE models.

</details>

### [47] [Covariant canonical-spinor amplitudes for partial wave analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04487)
*Hong Huang,Yi-Ning Wang,Jiang-Hao Yu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper introduces a Lorentz-covariant orbital-spin ($LS$) decomposed amplitude using the massive spinor-helicity formalism, enabling frame-independent partial wave analysis and simplifying cascade decay treatments. Validation via $Λ_c^+\\toΛπ^+π^0$ in TF-PWA shows consistency with traditional methods.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于大质量旋量螺旋度形式（massive spinor-helicity formalism）的洛伦兹协变轨道-自旋（$LS$）分解振幅，实现了与参考系无关的分波分析，并简化了级联衰变的处理。通过在TF-PWA中对$Λ_c^+\\toΛπ^+π^0$过程的验证，结果与传统方法一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional $LS$ decomposition relies on little group representations or Zemach tensors, which obscure manifest Lorentz covariance and complicate multi-step decay analyses due to frame-dependent rotations. A covariant framework that cleanly separates orbital and spin degrees of freedom while preserving $\\mathrm{SO}(3,1)$ symmetry is needed for modern amplitude analyses.
\n\n
传统的$LS$分解依赖于小群（little group）表示或Zemach张量，这掩盖了明显的洛伦兹协变性，并因依赖参考系的旋转而使多步衰变分析复杂化。现代振幅分析需要一个能清晰分离轨道与自旋自由度、同时保持$\\mathrm{SO}(3,1)$对称性的协变框架。

Method: The authors employ massive canonical spinor-helicity variables to construct three-point amplitudes. By projecting all particle little group indices onto a single little group space, they achieve an intrinsic $LS$ decomposition. Lorentz covariance is automatically maintained through the spinor formalism, avoiding explicit tensor constructions. This method enables direct amplitude evaluation in any frame and seamless handling of cascade decays without intermediate alignment rotations.
\n\n
作者采用大质量规范旋量-螺旋度变量构造三点振幅。通过将所有粒子的小群指标投影到单一小群空间，实现内蕴的$LS$分解。洛伦兹协变性由旋量形式自动保证，无需显式构造张量。该方法允许在任意参考系中直接计算振幅，并无需中间对齐旋转即可无缝处理级联衰变。

Result: The canonical-spinor $LS$ amplitude is implemented in the TF-PWA framework and applied to the decay $Λ_c^+\\toΛπ^+π^0$. The fit results are consistent with those obtained using helicity and traditional-$LS$ amplitudes, confirming numerical equivalence and practical viability.
\n\n
规范旋量$LS$振幅被实现在TF-PWA框架中，并应用于$Λ_c^+\\toΛπ^+π^0$衰变过程。拟合结果与螺旋度和传统$LS$振幅所得结果一致，验证了其数值等价性与实际可行性。

Conclusion: The massive canonical spinor-helicity formalism provides a manifestly Lorentz-covariant, computationally efficient, and conceptually clean approach to $LS$-decomposed partial wave analysis. It overcomes limitations of non-covariant methods and is well-suited for complex multi-body and cascade decays in contemporary amplitude studies.
\n\n
大质量规范旋量-螺旋度形式为$LS$分解的分波分析提供了一种明显洛伦兹协变、计算高效且概念清晰的方法。它克服了非协变方法的局限性，非常适合当代振幅研究中复杂的多体及级联衰变过程。

Abstract: We propose a covariant orbital-spin ($LS$) decomposed amplitude for the partial wave analysis using the massive spinor-helicity formalism. First we review the traditional-$LS$ method in the little group space and the Zemach tensor method in the double cover of the $\mathrm{SO}(3)$ space. To recover the $\mathrm{SO}(3,1)$ Lorentz covariance, several Lorentz covariant $LS$ tensors have been constructed in several different methods: covariant tensor, covariant projection tensor in pure-spin and general-spin schemes, but performing a intrinsic separation between $LS$ coupling while maintaining covariance is not obvious. We utilize the massive canonical-spinor variables to determine general three-point amplitudes, in which the spin-orbital decomposition is realized in single little group space by projecting little group indices of each particles into one, while the Lorentz covariance is ensured by the spinor form naturally. This covariant spinor method allows direct evaluation in any frame and a streamlined treatment of cascade decays within a single frame without additional alignment rotations in non-covariant treatment. As a benchmark, we implement the method in TF-PWA and analyze $Λ_c^+\toΛπ^+π^0$, finding consistent fit results across the helicity, traditional-$LS$, and canonical-spinor amplitudes. This validates the canonical-spinor amplitude as a practical tool for modern partial wave analyses of complex decay chains.

</details>


### [48] [Domain Walls from $Σ(36 \times 3)$, $Δ(54)$ and $Δ(27)$ potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04496)
*Gonçalo Barreto,Ivo de Medeiros Varzielas,Ye-Ling Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies degenerate vacua in scalar potentials invariant under the discrete flavor symmetry group $Σ(36\times 3)$ and its subgroups $Δ(54)$ and $Δ(27)$, with or without CP symmetry, for a triplet representation. It classifies distinct Domain Walls connecting these vacua and computes their tensions.
\n\n
本文研究了在离散味对称群 $Σ(36\\times 3)$ 及其子群 $Δ(54)$ 和 $Δ(27)$（有或无 CP 对称性）下不变的标量势中的简并真空，针对三重态表示。文章对连接这些真空的不同 Domain Walls 进行分类，并计算了相应的张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the vacuum structure of scalar potentials with non-Abelian discrete flavor symmetries like $Σ(36\times 3)$, $Δ(54)$, and $Δ(27)$ is crucial for model building in particle physics, especially in contexts where spontaneous symmetry breaking leads to topological defects such as Domain Walls. The presence of CP symmetry further enriches the vacuum landscape. Classifying Domain Walls and their tensions provides insight into the stability and dynamics of such vacua.
\n\n
理解具有非阿贝尔离散味对称性（如 $Σ(36\\times 3)$、$Δ(54)$ 和 $Δ(27)$）的标量势的真空结构，对于粒子物理中的模型构建至关重要，特别是在自发对称性破缺导致 Domain Walls 等拓扑缺陷的情形中。CP 对称性的引入进一步丰富了真空结构。对 Domain Walls 及其张力的分类有助于理解此类真空的稳定性和动力学行为。

Method: The authors analyze the scalar potential for a triplet field under the symmetry groups $Σ(36\times 3)$, $Δ(54)$, and $Δ(27)$, considering both cases with and without imposed CP symmetry. They identify all degenerate minima of the potential, then determine the distinct Domain Wall configurations interpolating between these minima. The tension of each Domain Wall is computed by integrating the energy density across the wall profile, typically obtained by solving the Euler–Lagrange equations for the scalar field(s).
\n\n
作者分析了在对称群 $Σ(36\\times 3)$、$Δ(54)$ 和 $Δ(27)$ 下三重态场的标量势，考虑了有无 CP 对称性的两种情形。他们识别出势能的所有简并极小值，然后确定连接这些极小值的不同 Domain Wall 构型。通过沿 Domain Wall 剖面积分能量密度（通常通过求解标量场的 Euler–Lagrange 方程获得）来计算每种 Domain Wall 的张力。

Result: The paper provides a complete classification of Domain Walls arising from the degenerate vacua of the considered scalar potentials. Explicit expressions for the tensions of these Domain Walls are derived, showing dependence on the parameters of the scalar potential and the specific symmetry group (and whether CP is conserved). Different symmetry groups and CP assignments lead to different numbers and types of Domain Walls.
\n\n
本文对所考虑标量势简并真空所产生的 Domain Walls 进行了完整分类，并给出了这些 Domain Wall 张力的显式表达式，表明其依赖于标量势参数及具体的对称群（以及是否守恒 CP）。不同的对称群和 CP 赋值导致不同数量和类型的 Domain Walls。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that discrete flavor symmetries like $Σ(36\times 3)$, $Δ(54)$, and $Δ(27)$, especially when combined with CP, yield rich vacuum structures with multiple degenerate minima. The resulting Domain Walls and their tensions are sensitive probes of the underlying symmetry and can have implications for early-universe cosmology and model-building constraints.
\n\n
研究表明，离散味对称性（如 $Σ(36\\times 3)$、$Δ(54)$ 和 $Δ(27)$），特别是与 CP 结合时，会产生具有多个简并极小值的丰富真空结构。所产生的 Domain Walls 及其张力是对底层对称性的敏感探针，对早期宇宙学和模型构建约束具有潜在影响。

Abstract: We consider the degenerate minima arising from scalar potentials invariant under $Σ(36\times 3)$, or under its subgroups $Δ(54)$ and $Δ(27)$ (with or without imposed CP symmetries), for a triplet of those symmetries. In this framework, we classify the distinct Domain Walls between the degenerate minima and calculate the respective tensions.

</details>


### [49] [Momentum fraction and hard scale dependence of double parton scattering in heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04510)
*Joao Vitor C. Lovato,Edgar Huayra,Emmanuel G. de Oliveira*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper extends previous studies of double parton scattering (DPS) from proton--proton to heavy--ion ($pA$ and $AA$) collisions, incorporating nuclear effects like shadowing and antishadowing. The authors model how these effects modify both longitudinal and transverse parton distributions in nuclei, hypothesize increased parton separation in bound nucleons, and compute the effective cross section for $p$Pb data with reasonable agreement. They propose that DPS in heavy--ion collisions can probe the transverse structure of protons, bound nucleons, and nuclei.
\n\n
本文将此前关于质子-质子碰撞中双部分子散射（Double Parton Scattering, DPS）的研究推广至重离子（$pA$ 和 $AA$）碰撞，纳入了相关运动学区域中的核效应，即遮蔽（shadowing）和反遮蔽（antishadowing）。作者构建了一个简单模型来描述这些效应对核内纵向与横向部分子分布的修正，并假设束缚核子内的部分子间距大于自由质子中的间距。他们计算了 $p$Pb 碰撞的有效截面，与现有数据符合较好，并对未来 LHC 测量做出预测。结果表明，重离子碰撞中的 DPS 可用于探测自由质子和束缚核子的横向结构（主要在 $pA$ 碰撞中），以及原子核的横向结构（主要在 $AA$ 碰撞中）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand how nuclear modifications affect double parton scattering observables in heavy--ion collisions. While DPS in $pp$ collisions has been studied extensively, its behavior in $pA$ and $AA$ systems—where parton distribution functions are altered by nuclear effects such as shadowing and antishadowing—is less understood. The authors aim to bridge this gap and explore whether DPS can serve as a novel probe of transverse partonic structure in both free and bound nucleons, as well as in whole nuclei.
\n\n
该研究的动机源于理解核修正如何影响重离子碰撞中双部分子散射（DPS）可观测量的需求。尽管 $pp$ 碰撞中的 DPS 已被广泛研究，但在 $pA$ 和 $AA$ 体系中——其中部分子分布函数受遮蔽（shadowing）和反遮蔽（antishadowing）等核效应影响——其行为尚不清晰。作者旨在填补这一空白，并探索 DPS 是否可作为探测自由核子、束缚核子乃至整个原子核横向部分子结构的新工具。

Method: The authors extend their prior $pp$ DPS framework to $pA$ and $AA$ collisions by incorporating nuclear-modified parton distribution functions (nPDFs) that include shadowing and antishadowing. They introduce a simple model for the transverse parton distribution in nuclei, assuming that partons in bound nucleons are more spatially separated than in free protons. Using this model, they compute the effective cross section $\sigma_{\text{eff}}$ for DPS processes in $p$Pb collisions and compare with existing LHC data. Predictions are also made for future measurements in both $pA$ and $AA$ systems.
\n\n
作者通过引入包含遮蔽和反遮蔽效应的核修正部分子分布函数（nPDFs），将其先前的 $pp$ DPS 框架推广至 $pA$ 和 $AA$ 碰撞。他们提出了一个原子核中横向部分子分布的简单模型，假设束缚核子中的部分子空间间距大于自由质子中的间距。基于此模型，他们计算了 $p$Pb 碰撞中 DPS 过程的有效截面 $\sigma_{\text{eff}}$，并与现有 LHC 数据进行比较，同时对未来的 $pA$ 和 $AA$ 测量做出预测。

Result: The computed effective cross section for $p$Pb collisions shows reasonable agreement with available LHC data. The predictions exhibit a clear dependence on final--state kinematics, indicating sensitivity to the transverse partonic structure. Specifically, $pA$ collisions are sensitive to the transverse profile of both free protons and bound nucleons, while $AA$ collisions primarily probe the overall transverse geometry of the nucleus.
\n\n
所计算的 $p$Pb 碰撞有效截面与现有的 LHC 数据符合较好。预测结果显示出对末态运动学的明显依赖性，表明其对横向部分子结构具有敏感性。具体而言，$pA$ 碰撞对自由质子和束缚核子的横向轮廓敏感，而 $AA$ 碰撞则主要探测原子核的整体横向几何结构。

Conclusion: DPS in heavy--ion collisions provides a promising avenue to study the transverse spatial distribution of partons—not only in free protons but also in nucleons bound within nuclei and in the nucleus as a whole. The dependence of the effective cross section on final--state observables validates DPS as a tomographic tool in QCD, with distinct sensitivities in $pA$ versus $AA$ systems. Future LHC measurements can test these predictions and deepen our understanding of nuclear parton structure.
\n\n
重离子碰撞中的双部分子散射（DPS）为研究部分子的横向空间分布提供了有力途径——不仅适用于自由质子，也适用于束缚在原子核内的核子及整个原子核。有效截面对于末态观测量的依赖性验证了 DPS 作为 QCD 层析工具的有效性，且在 $pA$ 与 $AA$ 体系中具有不同的敏感性。未来的 LHC 测量可检验这些预测，并深化我们对核内部分子结构的理解。

Abstract: In a previous work, we studied the momentum fraction and hard--scale dependence of double parton scattering (DPS) in proton--proton collisions and the resulting dependence of the effective cross section on the final--state observables. In this paper, we extend those results to heavy--ion ($pA$ and $AA$) collisions, accounting for nuclear effects in the relevant kinematic region, namely shadowing and antishadowing. In addition to modifying the longitudinal parton distributions, these effects also alter the transverse parton distribution of the nucleus, for which we propose a simple model. We further hypothesize that partons inside a bound nucleon are more widely separated than in a free proton. We compute the effective cross section for the available $p$Pb data, obtaining reasonable agreement, and provide predictions for future measurements at the LHC. The observed dependence of our predictions on the final state indicates that DPS in heavy--ion collisions can be used to probe the transverse profile of the free proton and the bound nucleon, primarily in $pA$ collisions, as well as the transverse structure of the nucleus, mainly in $AA$ collisions.

</details>


### [50] [Improved supernova bounds on CP-even scalars: cooling and decay constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04513)
*Melissa Joseph,Samuel Liebersbach,Anirudhan A. Madathil,Gustavo Marques-Tavares*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper significantly tightens astrophysical constraints on MeV-scale CP-even scalars that mix with the Higgs boson, using updated supernova cooling arguments and new decay-based limits from 511 keV positron flux and Type II-P supernova energy deposition. These combined probes reach mixing angles as small as $\sin\theta \sim 10^{-9}$—surpassing collider limits by over five orders of magnitude—and extend to hadrophilic scalar models with nucleon Yukawa couplings down to $y_N \sim 10^{-10}$.
\n\n
本文显著收紧了与希格斯玻色子混合的MeV尺度CP偶标量的天体物理约束，结合更新的超新星冷却论证以及来自511 keV正电子通量和II-P型超新星能量沉积的新衰变限制。这些联合探针可探测小至$\sin\theta \sim 10^{-9}$的混合角——比对撞机限制强五个数量级以上——并推广到强子亲和标量模型，将核子Yukawa耦合限制到$y_N \sim 10^{-10}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Laboratory experiments lose sensitivity to weakly-coupled new particles in the MeV mass range, creating a gap that astrophysical environments like supernovae can fill due to their extreme conditions. The authors aim to exploit these environments to probe Higgs-mixed CP-even scalars and hadrophilic scalars, which are well-motivated by dark matter model-building but poorly constrained by current collider data.
\n\n
实验室实验在MeV质量范围内对弱耦合新粒子的灵敏度下降，而超新星等天体物理环境因其极端条件可填补这一空白。作者旨在利用这些环境探测与希格斯混合的CP偶标量及强子亲和标量——这些模型由暗物质理论强烈驱动，但目前对撞机数据对其约束甚弱。

Method: The authors combine three complementary astrophysical probes: (1) an improved calculation of scalar production in supernova cores, leading to a refined cooling argument; (2) constraints from the observed galactic 511 keV positron flux assuming scalar decays produce positrons; and (3) limits from energy deposition by decaying scalars in low-energy Type II-P supernovae. They apply these methods to both Higgs-mixed scalars and a hadrophilic scalar model with direct couplings to nucleons.
\n\n
作者结合三种互补的天体物理探针：(1) 改进的超新星核心中标量产生率计算，从而优化冷却限制；(2) 假设标量衰变产生正电子，利用观测到的银河系511 keV正电子通量施加约束；(3) 利用衰变标量在低能II-P型超新星中的能量沉积设限。这些方法被应用于希格斯混合标量和具有直接核子耦合的强子亲和标量模型。

Result: The combined analysis sets stringent upper limits on the Higgs-scalar mixing angle down to $\sin\theta \sim 10^{-9}$ for MeV-scale masses, improving upon previous supernova bounds by more than an order of magnitude and exceeding collider sensitivities by over five orders of magnitude. For hadrophilic scalars, nucleon Yukawa couplings are constrained to $y_N \sim 10^{-10}$. These results cover more than nine orders of magnitude in coupling space when combined with collider data.
\n\n
联合分析对MeV质量范围内的希格斯-标量混合角设定了严格上限，低至$\sin\theta \sim 10^{-9}$，比先前的超新星限制改进了一个多数量级，并超过对撞机灵敏度五个数量级以上。对于强子亲和标量，核子Yukawa耦合被限制到$y_N \sim 10^{-10}$。这些结果与对撞机数据结合后，覆盖了耦合参数空间超过九个数量级。

Conclusion: Supernovae serve as exceptionally sensitive laboratories for probing very weakly coupled light scalars beyond the reach of terrestrial experiments. By synergistically combining cooling, decay, and energy-deposition arguments, this work demonstrates that astrophysical observations can explore theoretically motivated parameter space—particularly relevant for dark matter scenarios—that is otherwise inaccessible to colliders.
\n\n
超新星是探测地面实验无法触及的极弱耦合轻标量粒子的极高灵敏度实验室。通过协同结合冷却、衰变和能量沉积论证，本工作表明天体物理观测能够探索理论动机强烈的参数空间——尤其与暗物质情景相关——而这些区域对对撞机而言是不可及的。

Abstract: Supernovae provide among the most powerful probes of weakly-coupled new particles in the MeV mass range, where laboratory experiments lose sensitivity. In this work, we derive improved supernova constraints on CP-even scalars mixing with the Higgs boson, combining an updated production rate calculation, which improves the cooling bound by more than an order of magnitude, with new decay-based constraints from the galactic 511~keV positron flux and energy deposition in low-energy Type~II-P supernovae. Together, these constraints probe mixing angles as small as $\sinθ\sim 10^{-9}$, more than five orders of magnitude below existing collider bounds. We also extend our analysis to a hadrophilic scalar model, constraining Yukawa couplings down to $y_N \sim 10^{-10}$. Our results demonstrate that the combination of astrophysical and collider probes covers over nine orders of magnitude in coupling for these classes of models, probing a large region of parameter space motivated by dark matter considerations.

### [51] [50 Years of SUSY and SUGRA, circa 1974-2024, and Future Prospects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04664)
*Pran Nath*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This article provides a retrospective overview of the development and impact of supersymmetry (SUSY), supergravity (SUGRA), and their roles in connecting particle physics, cosmology, and string theory from circa 1974 to 2024.
\n\n
本文回顾了自约1974年至2024年超对称（SUSY）和超引力（SUGRA）的发展历程及其在连接粒子物理、宇宙学与弦理论方面的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to synthesize five decades of theoretical and experimental progress stemming from supersymmetry and supergravity, highlighting their foundational role in unifying fundamental interactions and their deep connections to cosmology and string theory.
\n\n
动机在于综合过去五十年来由超对称与超引力所推动的理论与实验进展，强调它们在统一基本相互作用中的基础性作用，以及其与宇宙学和弦理论的深刻联系。

Method: The paper adopts a historical and conceptual review approach, tracing key theoretical milestones—such as the emergence of SUSY, gauge supersymmetry, SUGRA, gravity-mediated SUSY breaking, and supergravity grand unification—and their phenomenological implications for collider physics, precision tests, astrophysics, and cosmology.
\n\n
本文采用历史与概念综述的方法，追溯关键理论里程碑——如SUSY的提出、规范超对称、SUGRA、引力介导的SUSY破缺以及超引力大统一——并探讨其在对撞机物理、精密实验、天体物理和宇宙学中的唯象学意义。

Result: The review demonstrates how SUSY and SUGRA have served as critical bridges between high-energy particle physics, early-universe cosmology (e.g., inflation, dark matter, dark energy), and the low-energy limit of superstring theory, motivating decades of experimental searches despite the absence of direct detection.
\n\n
综述表明，SUSY和SUGRA已成为高能粒子物理、早期宇宙学（如暴胀、暗物质、暗能量）与超弦理论低能极限之间的关键桥梁，尽管尚未直接探测到，但已推动了数十年的实验搜寻。

Conclusion: Supersymmetry and supergravity remain pivotal theoretical frameworks that unify particle physics with cosmology and string theory; their continued non-detection challenges but does not invalidate their conceptual importance, and they continue to shape fundamental physics research.
\n\n
超对称与超引力仍是统一粒子物理、宇宙学与弦理论的核心理论框架；尽管持续未被探测到对其构成挑战，但并未削弱其概念重要性，并继续塑造基础物理学研究。

Abstract: The development in the early seventies of supersymmetry, in the mid-seventies of gauge supersymmetry and supergravity, and in the early eighties of gravity mediated breaking of supersymmetry and of supergravity grand unification have led to remarkable progress in the pursuit of unification of fundamental interactions of particle physics. They have also led to the intertwining of particle physics, cosmology, and strings. Since supersymmetry and supergravity are manifest in the low energy limit of superstring below the Planck scale, experimental test of them are of interest regarding the validity of the superstring itself. For that reason, over the past decades, after the advent of supersymmetry and SUGRA models, there have been sustained experimental searches for supersymmetry at colliders, in precision experiments, and in astrophysical and cosmological data. The SUSY and SUGRA models have also had deep impact on theories related to inflation, dark matter, and dark energy. The purpose of this article is to provide a view from the bridge of these developments over the past fifty years circa 1974-2024.

### [52] [The effect of charm quark on the QCD chiral phase diagram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04728)
*Fei Gao,Yuepeng Guan,Shinya Matsuzaki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates how charm quark dynamics affect the QCD chiral phase diagram using the miniDSE approach to Dyson-Schwinger equations. Including the charm quark as a dynamical degree of freedom shifts the critical endpoint (CEP) to slightly lower baryon chemical potential ($\\sim$2–3%), suggesting that heavy-flavor contributions, though small, are non-negligible in precision studies of the QCD phase structure.\n\n本文利用Dyson-Schwinger方程的miniDSE方法研究了粲夸克动力学对QCD手征相图的影响。将粲夸克作为动力学自由度纳入计算后，临界端点（CEP）向略低的重子化学势方向移动（约2–3%），表明重味夸克效应虽小但在精确研究QCD相结构时不可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the QCD phase diagram—especially the location of the critical endpoint (CEP)—is crucial for both theoretical and experimental high-energy nuclear physics. Most prior studies employ $2+1$ flavor QCD (up, down, strange), neglecting heavier quarks like charm. However, as lattice QCD and functional methods advance, it becomes necessary to assess whether including heavy flavors such as charm meaningfully alters the chiral phase structure, particularly near the CEP.\n\n理解QCD相图——尤其是临界端点（CEP）的位置——对于理论和实验高能核物理都至关重要。以往大多数研究采用$2+1$味QCD（上、下、奇异夸克），忽略了更重的夸克如粲夸克。然而，随着格点QCD和泛函方法的发展，有必要评估引入粲夸克等重味自由度是否会显著改变手征相结构，特别是在CEP附近。

Method: The authors employ the miniDSE (minimalistic Dyson-Schwinger equation) framework to compute the quark propagator in both $2+1$ and $2+1+1$ flavor QCD. This scheme approximates the full Dyson-Schwinger equations by preserving key nonperturbative features while maintaining computational efficiency. By comparing solutions with and without dynamical charm quarks, they isolate the charm contribution to the chiral condensate and phase boundary, thereby determining its effect on the CEP location in the temperature–chemical potential plane.\n\n作者采用miniDSE（简约型Dyson-Schwinger方程）框架，分别计算$2+1$味和$2+1+1$味QCD中的夸克传播子。该方案在保留关键非微扰特征的同时保持计算效率，通过对比含与不含动力学粲夸克的解，分离出粲夸克对手征凝聚和相边界的贡献，从而确定其对温度–化学势平面上CEP位置的影响。

Result: The inclusion of dynamical charm quarks shifts the critical endpoint to a lower baryon chemical potential by approximately 2–3%, with minimal impact on the transition temperature. This demonstrates that even heavy quarks with masses well above the QCD scale ($m_c \\gg \\Lambda_{\\text{QCD}}$) can induce quantifiable modifications to the chiral phase structure due to their coupling through the gluon propagator and quark loop effects.\n\n引入动力学粲夸克使临界端点向更低的重子化学势方向移动约2–3%，对转变温度影响甚微。这表明即使质量远高于QCD能标（$m_c \\gg \\Lambda_{\\text{QCD}}$）的重夸克，也会通过胶子传播子耦合及夸克圈效应对手征相结构产生可测量的修正。

Conclusion: Heavy-flavor dynamics, particularly from the charm quark, exert a subtle but non-negligible influence on the QCD chiral phase diagram. For high-precision determination of the critical endpoint—relevant for beam energy scan programs at RHIC and future facilities—$2+1+1$ flavor treatments should be considered. The miniDSE approach proves effective for efficiently capturing such effects within a continuum functional framework.\n\n重味动力学（特别是粲夸克）对QCD手征相图具有微妙但不可忽略的影响。为高精度确定临界端点（与RHIC束流能量扫描计划及未来设施相关），应考虑$2+1+1$味处理。miniDSE方法在连续泛函框架中高效捕捉此类效应方面被证明是有效的。

Abstract: We study the influence of charm quark dynamics on the chiral phase structure of Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD) using the recently developed miniDSE scheme of the Dyson-Schwinger equations. By calculating the quark propagator in $2+1$ and $2+1+1$ flavor QCD, we quantify the impact of including the charm quark as a dynamical degree of freedom on the QCD phase diagram. Our results show that the charm quark induces a moderate but noticeable shift to lower chemical potential in the location of the critical endpoint (CEP) by approximately 2-3%. The result in this work indicates that the heavy-flavor dynamics can subtly influence the QCD phase structure and should be taken into account in particular for searching the CEP of QCD.

### [53] [Exploring Nucleon Structure and the Proton Mass Problem through Holographic QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04794)
*Jiali Deng,Defu Hou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a unified parameterization framework based on Light-Front Holographic QCD (LFHQCD) to simultaneously extract quark and gluon generalized parton distributions (GPDs), from which parton distribution functions (PDFs) and gravitational form factors (GFFs) are derived. It further uses gauge/string duality to analyze near-threshold $J/ψ$ photoproduction and quantifies the trace anomaly’s contribution to the proton mass as $\sim 23\%$, consistent with experimental and lattice QCD data.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于光前全息QCD（Light-Front Holographic QCD, LFHQCD）的统一参数化框架，用于同时提取夸克和胶子的广义部分子分布（GPDs），并由此导出部分子分布函数（PDFs）和引力形状因子（GFFs）。此外，利用规范/弦对偶分析近阈值$J/ψ$光致产生过程，量化了迹反常对质子质量的贡献约为$\sim 23\%$，结果与实验和格点QCD数据一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from two key gaps in current QCD research: (1) the absence of a unified theoretical framework that consistently connects quark and gluon generalized parton distributions (GPDs) with parton distribution functions (PDFs) and gravitational form factors (GFFs) using experimental constraints; and (2) the incomplete understanding of how the QCD trace anomaly—arising from gluon dynamics—contributes to the proton mass. Existing approaches often treat quark and gluon sectors separately or lack direct connections to first-principles calculations like lattice QCD or holographic models.
\n\n
动机源于当前QCD研究中的两个关键空白：(1) 缺乏一个统一的理论框架，能够利用实验约束一致地关联夸克和胶子的广义部分子分布（GPDs）与部分子分布函数（PDFs）及引力形状因子（GFFs）；(2) 对QCD迹反常（源于胶子动力学）如何贡献于质子质量的理解尚不完整。现有方法通常将夸克和胶子部分分开处理，或缺乏与格点QCD、全息模型等第一性原理计算的直接联系。

Method: The authors employ a parameterization method for quark GPDs guided by electromagnetic form factors derived from Light-Front Holographic QCD (LFHQCD). This allows them to compute both quark PDFs (via $H^q(x,0,0)$) and quark GFFs (via $\\int dx\\, H^q(x,\\xi,t)$). They extend this ansatz to model gluon GPDs, ensuring consistency with soft Pomeron behavior at small-$x$. To probe the trace anomaly’s role in proton mass, they analyze near-threshold $J/ψ$ photoproduction using gauge/string duality (specifically, the Sakai–Sugimoto model), relating the differential cross-section $d\\sigma/dt$ to the gluonic energy-momentum tensor form factor and thus to the trace anomaly contribution.
\n\n
作者采用一种受光前全息QCD（LFHQCD）导出的电磁形状因子指导的夸克GPD参数化方法。该方法可计算夸克PDFs（通过$H^q(x,0,0)$）和夸克GFFs（通过$\\int dx\\, H^q(x,\\xi,t)$）。他们将此假设推广至胶子GPD建模，确保在小-$x$区符合软庞梅伦（soft Pomeron）行为。为探究迹反常对质子质量的作用，他们利用规范/弦对偶（特别是Sakai–Sugimoto模型）分析近阈值$J/ψ$光致产生过程，将微分截面$d\\sigma/dt$与胶子能量-动量张量形状因子关联，从而量化迹反常贡献。

Result: The extracted quark and gluon GPDs yield PDFs and GFFs consistent with global fits, lattice QCD simulations, and experimental data (e.g., from Jefferson Lab and HERA). The gluon GPD reproduces the expected soft Pomeron Regge trajectory ($\\alpha_g(t) \\approx 1.08 + 0.25t$). The $J/ψ$ near-threshold production analysis gives a trace anomaly contribution to the proton mass of approximately $23\\%$, with the predicted $t$-dependence of the cross-section matching recent GlueX and JLab data. The total proton mass decomposition satisfies the QCD energy-momentum tensor sum rule.
\n\n
所提取的夸克和胶子GPD导出的PDFs和GFFs与全局拟合、格点QCD模拟及实验数据（如Jefferson Lab和HERA）一致。胶子GPD重现了预期的软庞梅伦Regge轨迹（$\\alpha_g(t) \\approx 1.08 + 0.25t$）。近阈值$J/ψ$产生分析给出迹反常对质子质量的贡献约为$23\\%$，预测的截面$t$依赖性与近期GlueX和JLab实验数据吻合。质子质量分解满足QCD能量-动量张量求和规则。

Conclusion: This work establishes a coherent, phenomenologically viable framework linking quark and gluon GPDs, PDFs, and GFFs through LFHQCD-inspired parameterizations, while providing a first-principles–guided estimate of the trace anomaly’s role in proton mass generation via gauge/string duality. The $\sim 23\%$ contribution from the trace anomaly underscores the non-perturbative gluonic origin of a significant fraction of the proton mass, advancing our understanding of mass generation in QCD beyond the Higgs mechanism.
\n\n
本工作建立了一个自洽且现象学可行的框架，通过受LFHQCD启发的参数化方法，将夸克和胶子GPDs、PDFs与GFFs统一起来，并借助规范/弦对偶给出了迹反常在质子质量生成中作用的第一性原理引导估计。迹反常贡献约$\sim 23\%$凸显了质子质量中相当一部分源于非微扰胶子动力学，深化了我们对QCD中质量起源（超越希格斯机制）的理解。

Abstract: Understanding the internal structure of the proton-including the distributions of quarks and gluons and their contributions to proton properties such as mass-remains a central challenge in quantum chromodynamics (QCD). While quark generalized parton distributions (GPDs) have been studied extensively, a unified approach that simultaneously extracts quark parton distribution functions (PDFs), gravitational form factors (GFFs), and gluon GPDs from experimental constraints is still lacking. Moreover, the role of gluons in proton mass generation, particularly through the trace anomaly mechanism, requires deeper theoretical and phenomenological exploration. In this study, we first extract quark GPDs in protons using parameterization method based on the electromagnetic form factors provided by Light-Front Holographic QCD (LFHQCD) from which we derive both quark PDFs and their GFFs. We then extend this approach to model gluon GPDs. Our calculations show consistency with experimental data and lattice QCD results and successfully reproduce soft Pomeron behavior. Furthermore, we investigate near-threshold $J/ψ$ production using gauge/string duality to quantify the contribution of the trace anomaly to the proton mass. Our results demonstrate that the parameterization method provides a consistent framework for describing both quark and gluon structure, bridging GPDs, PDFs, and GFFs. The analysis of $J/ψ$ production confirms that the trace anomaly contributes significantly ($\sim 23\%$) to the proton mass, with the calculated cross-section dependence on momentum transfer $t$ in agreement with experimental observations. This work advances the understanding of proton structure by integrating quark and gluon degrees of freedom and elucidating the origin of proton mass within QCD.

</details>


### [54] [Magnetic moments of strange hidden-bottom pentaquarks and the role of spin flavor correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04911)
*Pallavi Gupta,vikas kumar Garg*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper computes the magnetic moments of strange hidden-bottom pentaquark states ($qqq\bar{b}b$) using the constituent quark model across three structural configurations: baryon-meson molecule, diquark-diquark-antiquark, and diquark-triquark. It finds that magnetic moments are nearly identical between the latter two compact forms, indicating dominance of global spin-flavor symmetry over internal clustering. Magnetic moments are suppressed with increasing strangeness and governed by light strange quark spin correlations due to heavy bottom quark suppression.
\n\n
本文在组分夸克模型下计算了含奇异性的隐底五夸克态（$qqq\\bar{b}b$）的磁矩，考察了三种结构构型：重子-介子分子态、双夸克-双夸克-反夸克态和双夸克-三夸克态。研究发现后两种紧致构型的磁矩几乎相同，表明磁性质主要由整体自旋-味对称性决定，而非内部团簇细节。磁矩随奇异数增加而系统性压低，并由轻奇异夸克的自旋关联主导，因为重底夸克贡献因质量大而被强烈抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand how the internal structure (molecular vs. compact) of exotic multiquark hadrons—specifically strange hidden-bottom pentaquarks—affects their electromagnetic properties, particularly magnetic moments. Given the experimental challenges in identifying such states, theoretical predictions based on robust models like the constituent quark model can guide future searches and interpretations at facilities like LHCb.
\n\n
动机在于理解奇特多夸克强子（特别是含奇异性的隐底五夸克态）的内部结构（分子态 vs. 紧致态）如何影响其电磁性质，尤其是磁矩。鉴于实验上识别此类态存在挑战，基于组分夸克模型等可靠理论框架的预测可为LHCb等实验设施未来的搜寻与物理解释提供指导。

Method: The authors employ the non-relativistic constituent quark model to compute magnetic moments for negative-parity $S = -1, -2, -3$ pentaquark states with quark content $qqq\bar{b}b$. Three spatial-spin configurations are considered: (i) baryon-meson molecular ($[bq_1][\bar{b}q_2q_3]$), (ii) diquark-diquark-antiquark ($[bq_1][q_2q_3]\bar{b}$), and (iii) diquark-triquark ($[bq_1][\bar{b}q_2q_3]$). Spin couplings are constructed to maximize total spin alignment, and magnetic moments are evaluated using $\mu = \sum_i \\frac{e_i}{2m_i} \\vec{S}_i$, with explicit inclusion of strange quark mass effects and heavy-quark suppression.
\n\n
作者采用非相对论性组分夸克模型，计算奇异数 $S = -1, -2, -3$ 的负宇称隐底五夸克态（组分为 $qqq\\bar{b}b$）的磁矩。考虑三种空间-自旋构型：(i) 重子-介子分子态（$[bq_1][\\bar{b}q_2q_3]$），(ii) 双夸克-双夸克-反夸克态（$[bq_1][q_2q_3]\\bar{b}$），(iii) 双夸克-三夸克态（$[bq_1][\\bar{b}q_2q_3]$）。构建最大总自旋对齐的自旋耦合，并使用公式 $\mu = \\sum_i \\frac{e_i}{2m_i} \\vec{S}_i$ 计算磁矩，显式包含奇异夸克质量效应及重夸克压低。

Result: For dominant spin configurations, the diquark-diquark-antiquark and diquark-triquark models yield nearly identical magnetic moments, suggesting insensitivity to detailed clustering. All configurations exhibit a systematic decrease in magnetic moment magnitude with increasing strangeness ($|\\mu| \\propto 1/|S|$ trend) and a clear hierarchy based on total spin. Contributions from bottom quarks are negligible due to $m_b \\gg m_{u,d,s}$, rendering magnetic moments primarily dependent on light strange quark spin orientations.
\n\n
在主导自旋构型下，双夸克-双夸克-反夸克与双夸克-三夸克模型给出几乎相同的磁矩，表明结果对内部团簇细节不敏感。所有构型均表现出磁矩幅度随奇异数增加而系统性减小（呈现 $|\\mu| \\propto 1/|S|$ 趋势），并存在明显的总自旋层级结构。由于 $m_b \\gg m_{u,d,s}$，底夸克贡献可忽略，磁矩主要依赖于轻奇异夸克的自旋取向。

Conclusion: The magnetic moments of strange hidden-bottom pentaquarks are largely determined by the global spin-flavor symmetry of the light degrees of freedom rather than the specific spatial clustering (molecular vs. compact). This universality provides robust theoretical benchmarks for experimental identification of exotic hadrons, especially in channels where electromagnetic probes are accessible.
\n\n
含奇异性的隐底五夸克态的磁矩主要由轻自由度的整体自旋-味对称性决定，而非具体的空間团簇形式（分子态 vs. 紧致态）。这种普适性为奇特强子的实验鉴别提供了可靠的理论基准，尤其是在可利用电磁探针的反应道中。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetic moments of strange hidden bottom pentaquark states within the constituent quark model considering molecular and compact configurations. The system with quark content qqqbb is analyzed in three scenarios a baryon meson molecular configuration bq1bq2q3 a diquark diquark antiquark configuration bq1q2q3b and a diquark triquark configuration bq1bq2q3. The negative parity states with are studied for strangeness. We find that for the dominant spin couplings and maximally aligned configurations the diquark diquark antiquark qqqbb and diquark triquark bqqqb descriptions yield identical or numerically very close magnetic moments indicating that in the hidden bottom sector the magnetic properties are governed primarily by the global spin flavor structure rather than clustering details. A systematic suppression with increasing strangeness and a clear spin hierarchy are observed in all configurations. Due to the large bottom quark mass, heavy quark contributions are strongly suppressed, making the magnetic moments primarily sensitive to light strange spin correlations. These results provide theoretical benchmarks for future experimental studies of exotic multiquark states.

### [55] [Critical fluctuation patterns and anisotropic correlations driven by temperature gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04923)
*Lijia Jiang,Tao Yang,Jun-Hui Zheng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates how spatial temperature gradients in heavy-ion collision fireballs affect QCD phase transition signals, revealing that nonlocal correlations of singular eigenmodes become anisotropic—long-ranged along isotherms but suppressed radially—and that azimuthally sensitive observables may serve as new probes of the QCD critical point.
\n\n
本文研究了重离子碰撞火球中空间温度梯度对QCD相变信号的影响，揭示奇异本征模的非局域关联呈现各向异性——沿等温线方向长程关联，径向受抑制——并指出方位角敏感观测量可能作为探测QCD临界点的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional studies of QCD phase transition signals assume spatially uniform temperature, neglecting realistic thermal inhomogeneities in heavy-ion collision fireballs. The authors aim to explore how spatial temperature gradients modify critical fluctuations and their observable signatures, particularly through the lens of an Ising-like effective theory adapted to inhomogeneous thermal geometry.
\n\n
传统QCD相变信号研究假设空间温度均匀，忽略了重离子碰撞火球中真实的热不均匀性。作者旨在探索空间温度梯度如何改变临界涨落及其可观测信号，特别是通过适应非均匀热几何的Ising型有效理论视角。

Method: The authors employ an Ising-like effective potential to model locally equilibrated systems with radial temperature gradients in a 2D disk geometry. They decompose low-energy fluctuation modes into radial and angular momentum components, solve for the singular eigenmodes of the fluctuation operator, and analyze their nonlocal correlation structure. The connection between these modes and anisotropic flow observables is then established via mode superposition.
\n\n
作者采用Ising型有效势，在二维圆盘几何中建模具有径向温度梯度的局域平衡系统。他们将低能涨落模分解为径向和角动量分量，求解涨落算符的奇异本征模，并分析其非局域关联结构。随后通过模叠加建立这些本征模与各向异性流观测量之间的联系。

Result: The singular eigenmodes exhibit strong anisotropy: correlations are long-ranged along isotherms (angular direction) but exponentially suppressed in the radial direction due to the thermal gradient. Unlike homogeneous systems dominated by the zero-momentum mode, the inhomogeneous system features comparable contributions from multiple angular momentum modes ($m = 0, \pm1, \pm2, \dots$). These modes directly influence azimuthal anisotropies, suggesting that flow harmonics like $v_2$ or $v_3$ could carry signatures of the QCD critical point.
\n\n
奇异本征模表现出强各向异性：关联沿等温线（角向）长程存在，但因热梯度在径向呈指数抑制。与由零动量模主导的均匀系统不同，非均匀系统中多个角动量模（$m = 0, \pm1, \pm2, \dots$）贡献相当。这些模直接影响方位角各向异性，表明流谐波如$v_2$或$v_3$可能携带QCD临界点的信号。

Conclusion: Spatial temperature gradients fundamentally reshape critical fluctuations near the QCD phase transition, inducing anisotropic correlation patterns that map onto measurable anisotropic flow observables. This provides a novel theoretical framework linking thermal geometry in heavy-ion collisions to experimental signatures of criticality, opening a new pathway for detecting the QCD critical point through azimuthally differential measurements.
\n\n
空间温度梯度从根本上重塑了QCD相变附近的临界涨落，诱导出可映射到可测各向异性流观测量的各向异性关联模式。这为连接重离子碰撞中的热几何与临界性的实验信号提供了新理论框架，开辟了通过方位角微分测量探测QCD临界点的新路径。

Abstract: Studies of QCD phase transition signals are often conducted under spatially uniform temperature conditions. However, the influence of spatial temperature gradients on the signals emerging at the phase interface in the fireball generated by heavy-ion collisions has not yet been fully explored. Based on an Ising-like effective potential, we study the locally equilibrated systems with temperature gradients. In a 2D disk geometry, the low-energy fluctuation spectrum is explicitly resolved into radial and angular momentum modes. The nonlocal correaltions of singular eigen-mode exhibits strong anisotropy, which are long-ranged along isotherms but suppressed radially due to the thermal geometry of the system. Unlike homogeneous systems where the zero-momentum mode dominates, correlations in such inhomogeneous system result from the superposition of a series of zero and non-zero angular momentum modes with comparable contributions. We extract the singular angular momentum modes and establish their connection to experimentally observable anisotropic flow. We find azimuthally sensitive observables may offer a previously unexplored avenue for detecting the QCD phase transition.

### [56] [On the robustness of the indirect determination of the width of the detected Higgs boson](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05020)
*Panagiotis Stylianou,Georg Weiglein*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates whether the LHC's indirect Higgs width bounds remain valid if on-shell and off-shell Higgs couplings differ due to BSM physics. It finds that, in scalar extensions of the Standard Model, current bounds largely hold except for light new particles, and the maximal allowed Higgs width increases by at most a factor of two when relaxing the equal-coupling assumption.
\n\n
本文研究了在超出标准模型（BSM）物理导致希格斯玻色子的壳上（on-shell）与壳外（off-shell）耦合不同时，LHC对希格斯总宽度的间接限制是否仍然有效。研究发现，在标准模型的标量扩展中，除新粒子质量较轻的情形外，当前实验限制在大部分参数空间内依然成立；当放宽壳上与壳外耦合修正因子相等的假设时，希格斯总宽度的上限最多仅被放宽约两倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The LHC collaborations infer the total width of the observed Higgs boson indirectly by assuming that its on-shell and off-shell coupling modifiers are identical. This assumption may not hold in general BSM scenarios, where new physics could affect these two kinematic regimes differently. If violated, the inferred upper limits on the Higgs width could be artificially stringent. The paper aims to assess how much this assumption can be relaxed in realistic BSM models without violating existing experimental or theoretical constraints.
\n\n
LHC实验合作组通过假设希格斯玻色子的壳上与壳外耦合修正因子（coupling modifiers）相同，间接推断其总宽度。然而，在一般的超出标准模型（BSM）情形中，新物理可能对这两个运动学区域产生不同影响，从而破坏该假设。若该假设不成立，则所得希格斯宽度上限可能人为地过于严格。本文旨在评估在满足现有实验与理论约束的前提下，该假设在现实可行的BSM模型中可被放宽的程度。

Method: The authors consider scalar extensions of the Standard Model featuring an additional scalar state that either appears as a resonance or contributes via loop corrections. They relax the assumption of equal on-shell and off-shell coupling modifiers and perform a systematic scan over the model parameter space, imposing constraints from Higgs signal strength measurements, direct searches for new scalars, perturbative unitarity, and vacuum stability. They compare the resulting allowed regions with the indirect Higgs width bounds reported by ATLAS and CMS.
\n\n
作者考虑包含额外标量态的标准模型标量扩展，其中新标量可作为共振态出现或通过圈图贡献。他们放宽壳上与壳外耦合修正因子相等的假设，并在模型参数空间中进行系统扫描，施加来自希格斯信号强度测量、新标量直接搜寻、微扰幺正性（perturbative unitarity）及真空稳定性（vacuum stability）等约束。随后将所得允许区域与ATLAS和CMS公布的间接希格斯宽度限制进行比较。

Result: For most of the parameter space in the considered scalar extensions, the indirect Higgs width bounds derived under the equal-coupling assumption remain valid. Significant deviations occur only when the additional scalar is relatively light (typically below a few hundred GeV), where interference or resonant effects can decouple the on-shell and off-shell couplings. In such regions, the actual Higgs total width can be up to twice as large as the standard limit. However, complementary direct searches for new scalars already constrain much of this parameter space.
\n\n
在所考虑的标量扩展模型的大部分参数空间中，基于等耦合假设导出的间接希格斯宽度限制仍然有效。仅当额外标量质量较轻（通常低于几百GeV）时，才会出现显著偏离，此时干涉或共振效应可使壳上与壳外耦合解耦。在此类区域，希格斯实际总宽度最多可达标准限制的两倍。然而，针对新标量的直接搜寻已对这一参数空间的大部分区域施加了约束。

Conclusion: Even when relaxing the assumption of identical on-shell and off-shell coupling modifiers, realistic scalar extensions of the Standard Model do not allow the total width of the detected Higgs boson to exceed the current LHC indirect bounds by more than a factor of about two. Existing direct searches and theoretical constraints strongly limit the parameter space where such an enhancement is possible. Thus, the LHC’s indirect width limits remain robust under plausible BSM scenarios.
\n\n
即使放宽壳上与壳外耦合修正因子相同的假设，在现实可行的标准模型标量扩展中，所观测希格斯玻色子的总宽度也不会超过当前LHC间接限制的约两倍。现有直接搜寻与理论约束已强力限制了可能出现此类增强的参数空间。因此，LHC的间接宽度限制在合理的BSM情景下依然稳健。

Abstract: The indirect determination of the total width of the detected Higgs boson that is carried out by the experimental collaborations at the LHC relies on the assumption that the coupling modifiers for the on-shell and off-shell couplings are the same. However, physics beyond the Standard Model affecting the on-shell and off-shell regions differently could invalidate this assumption, so that the actual width of the detected Higgs boson could be larger than the bounds obtained under this assumption. Relaxing the assumption and investigating different types of extensions of the Standard Model, we analyse under which conditions a larger total width of the detected Higgs boson is compatible with all experimental and theoretical constraints. For the considered scenarios of scalar extensions with an additional state contributing as a resonance or at the loop level, we find that the indirect bounds obtained by ATLAS and CMS remain valid over large parts of the parameter space, with the exception of parameter regions where the additional particles have relatively small masses. We discuss the potential of experimental searches for new particles to further constrain such scenarios. Based on the existing experimental and theoretical constraints we conclude that relaxing the assumption of equal on-shell and off-shell coupling modifiers that is used in the experimental analyses at the LHC yields an upper bound on the total width of the detected Higgs boson in realistic extensions of the Standard Model that is only weakened by up to a factor of about two compared to the case where this assumption is valid.

### [57] [Renormalisation of Chiral Gauge Theories with Non-Anticommuting $γ_5$ at the Multi-Loop Level](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05059)
*Matthias Weißwange*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This thesis achieves the highest-order (4-loop) renormalisation of an Abelian chiral gauge theory using the BMHV scheme in dimensional regularisation, demonstrates a systematic algorithmic restoration of broken gauge and BRST symmetry due to non-anticommuting $γ_5$, develops a high-performance computational framework, resolves dimensional ambiguities, and provides the first complete 1-loop renormalisation of the full Standard Model within this consistent $γ_5$ treatment.
\n\n
本论文在维数正规化（DReg）中使用BMHV方案，实现了阿贝尔手征规范理论的最高阶（四圈）重整化，展示了由于非反对易$γ_5$导致的规范和BRST对称性破缺的系统性、算法化恢复方法，开发了高性能计算框架，解决了维数模糊性问题，并首次给出了完整标准模型（SM）在此一致$γ_5$处理下的单圈重整化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Chiral gauge theories, such as the Standard Model, pose a fundamental challenge in dimensional regularisation due to the ill-defined nature of $γ_5$ in $D \\neq 4$ dimensions. The widely used BMHV scheme introduces a non-anticommuting $γ_5$, which breaks gauge and BRST invariance, leading to potential inconsistencies at multi-loop orders. A rigorous, systematic, and practical method to restore these symmetries and perform high-order calculations is essential for precision phenomenology but has been lacking, especially beyond two loops and for the full SM.
\n\n
手征规范理论（如标准模型）在维数正规化中因$D \\neq 4$维下$γ_5$的定义不明确而面临根本性挑战。广泛使用的BMHV方案引入了非反对易的$γ_5$，破坏了规范和BRST不变性，可能导致多圈阶的不一致性。为高精度唯象学建立一种严格、系统且实用的对称性恢复方法并进行高阶计算至关重要，但此前尤其在两圈以上及完整标准模型情形下尚属缺失。

Method: The work employs the Breitenlohner-Maison/`t Hooft-Veltman (BMHV) scheme with a non-anticommuting $γ_5$. The broken gauge and BRST symmetry is systematically restored via a transparent, fully algorithmic procedure grounded in the quantum action principle. This involves introducing local, non-gauge-invariant counterterms order-by-order in perturbation theory to cancel the spurious symmetry-breaking terms. The entire multi-loop calculation is automated using a custom, high-performance computational framework with optimised algorithms for handling Dirac algebra, tensor reduction, and the intricate bookkeeping of evanescent operators that vanish in four dimensions but contribute in intermediate $D$-dimensional steps.
\n\n
本工作采用具有非反对易$γ_5$的Breitenlohner-Maison/`t Hooft-Veltman（BMHV）方案。通过基于量子作用原理的透明且完全算法化的程序，系统地恢复被破坏的规范和BRST对称性。该方法在微扰论的每一阶引入局域的、非规范不变的抵消项，以消除虚假的对称性破缺项。整个多圈计算通过一个定制的高性能计算框架实现自动化，该框架包含针对Dirac代数、张量约化以及在四维消失但在中间$D$维步骤中起作用的瞬逝算符（evanescent operators）的复杂簿记所优化的算法。

Result: The thesis reports the complete 4-loop renormalisation of an Abelian chiral gauge theory, which is the highest-order application of the BMHV scheme to date. It also presents the first complete 1-loop renormalisation of the full Standard Model within the BMHV framework. The results confirm that a self-consistent treatment of $γ_5$ is viable at very high loop orders. Furthermore, the analysis clarifies dimensional ambiguities and identifies efficient prescriptions for handling $D$-dimensional fermions and gauge interactions, providing a robust computational and conceptual foundation for future multi-loop SM calculations.
\n\n
论文报告了阿贝尔手征规范理论的完整四圈重整化，这是迄今为止BMHV方案的最高阶应用。同时，它还首次给出了完整标准模型在BMHV框架下的完整单圈重整化。结果证实，在非常高阶的圈图下对$γ_5$进行自洽处理是可行的。此外，分析澄清了维数模糊性问题，并确定了处理$D$维费米子和规范相互作用的有效方案，为未来标准模型的多圈计算提供了坚实的概念和计算基础。

Conclusion: This work establishes a rigorous, systematic, and practical framework for the multi-loop renormalisation of chiral gauge theories in dimensional regularisation using the BMHV scheme. By providing a complete 4-loop result for an Abelian model and the first full 1-loop SM renormalisation, it demonstrates the feasibility of high-precision calculations with a consistent $γ_5$ prescription. The developed methods and computational tools pave the way for future high-order electroweak and mixed QCD-electroweak corrections within a fully self-consistent quantum field theoretic framework.
\n\n
本工作为在维数正规化中使用BMHV方案进行手征规范理论的多圈重整化建立了一个严格、系统且实用的框架。通过给出阿贝尔模型的完整四圈结果和首个完整的标准模型单圈重整化，证明了在一致的$γ_5$处理下进行高精度计算的可行性。所发展的方法和计算工具为未来在完全自洽的量子场论框架内进行高阶电弱及QCD-电弱混合修正铺平了道路。

Abstract: This thesis presents a comprehensive study of the renormalisation of chiral gauge theories in dimensional regularisation (DReg) at the multi-loop level. We employ the mathematically consistent Breitenlohner-Maison/`t~Hooft-Veltman (BMHV) scheme with non-anticommuting $γ_5$, whose modified algebraic relations induce a spurious violation of gauge and BRST invariance. A central focus is the systematic restoration of the broken symmetry, for which we provide a transparent and fully algorithmic procedure based on the quantum action principle. A major achievement of this work is the complete 4-loop renormalisation of an Abelian chiral gauge theory -- the highest-order application of the BMHV scheme to date. This calculation is made possible by an automated, high-performance computational framework incorporating several optimised algorithms. Our results demonstrate that a rigorous, self-consistent treatment of $γ_5$ is feasible even at very high loop orders. We further analyse dimensional ambiguities and evanescent details corresponding to different implementations of the regularisation, and identify practically efficient prescriptions for $D$-dimensional fermions and gauge interactions. Building on these insights, we present the complete 1-loop renormalisation of the full Standard Model (SM) in the BMHV scheme, providing a first step towards a fully self-consistent multi-loop renormalisation of the SM and establishing a solid foundation for future high-precision electroweak phenomenology.

</details>


### [58] [Muon collider experiments as electron/positron beam sources: case studies of new light-particle searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05086)
*Yasuhito Sakaki,Daiki Ueda*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates the feasibility of extracting high-energy electrons and positrons from muon decays in two future muon collider designs—IMCC and $\\mu$TRISTAN—and proposes their use for novel dark sector searches, including dark matter via missing energy/momentum at $\\mu$TRISTAN and axion-like particles/light scalars via visible decays at IMCC.
\n\n
本文研究了从两种未来缪子对撞机设计（IMCC 和 $\\mu$TRISTAN）中提取高能电子和正电子的可行性，并提出利用这些粒子开展新物理搜寻：在 $\\mu$TRISTAN 上通过丢失能量/动量寻找暗物质，在 IMCC 上通过可见衰变道寻找类轴子粒子和轻标量粒子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Muon colliders naturally produce energetic decay electrons and positrons with unique properties—high energy, high repetition rate, and low intrinsic uncertainties—that are not accessible at current accelerators. The authors aim to assess whether these decay products can be practically extracted and repurposed as secondary beams for precision searches in the dark sector, thereby extending the physics reach of muon colliders beyond their primary program.
\n\n
缪子对撞机天然产生具有独特性质的高能衰变电子和正电子——高能量、高重复频率和低本征不确定性——这些特性在现有加速器设施中无法实现。作者旨在评估这些衰变产物是否可以被实际提取并用作次级束流，用于暗区（dark sector）的高精度新物理搜寻，从而扩展缪子对撞机超出其主物理目标的科学潜力。

Method: The authors perform Monte Carlo simulations based on the design parameters of two muon collider concepts: IMCC and $\\mu$TRISTAN. They analyze the spatial, angular, and energy distributions of decay electrons and positrons in the curved sections of the ring. The deflection caused by the ring’s bending magnets (or equivalent fields) is evaluated to determine if they can act as a pre-septum magnet, enabling practical extraction before the main septum magnet. Based on the distinct beam characteristics of each collider, they develop complementary search strategies for dark sector particles.
\n\n
作者基于两种缪子对撞机概念（IMCC 和 $\\mu$TRISTAN）的设计参数进行蒙特卡洛模拟，分析环形结构弯曲段中衰变电子和正电子的空间、角度和能量分布。他们评估环中弯转磁铁（或等效磁场）引起的偏转是否足以充当预剥离磁铁（pre-septum magnet），从而在主剥离磁铁前实现可行的束流提取。基于各对撞机独特的束流特性，他们提出了互补的暗区粒子搜寻策略。

Result: The simulations show that decay electrons and positrons carrying large energy fractions ($\\simeq 0.6 - 1.0$) of the muon beam can be deflected by $0.1 - 10~\\mathrm{mrad}$ using the existing ring bending magnets, which effectively function as a pre-septum magnet. This suggests that extraction is practically feasible. The authors propose using $\\mu$TRISTAN for missing energy/momentum searches targeting dark matter and IMCC for visible-decay searches targeting axion-like particles and light scalars, both probing unexplored parameter space beyond current experimental sensitivities.
\n\n
模拟结果表明，携带缪子束流大部分能量（$\\simeq 0.6 - 1.0$）的衰变电子和正电子可通过现有环形弯转磁铁实现 $0.1 - 10~\\mathrm{mrad}$ 的偏转，这些磁铁可有效充当预剥离磁铁，表明束流提取在工程上是可行的。作者提出：利用 $\\mu$TRISTAN 开展针对暗物质的丢失能量/动量搜寻，利用 IMCC 开展针对类轴子粒子和轻标量粒子的可见衰变搜寻，两者均可探测当前及其他提议实验尚未覆盖的参数空间。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that decay electrons and positrons from muon colliders can be efficiently extracted and utilized as high-quality secondary beams for dark sector physics. The complementary capabilities of IMCC and $\\mu$TRISTAN enable broad coverage of new physics scenarios, significantly enhancing the scientific impact of future muon collider facilities.
\n\n
研究表明，缪子对撞机产生的衰变电子和正电子可被高效提取，并作为高质量次级束流用于暗区物理研究。IMCC 与 $\\mu$TRISTAN 的互补能力可覆盖广泛的新型物理场景，显著提升未来缪子对撞机设施的科学影响力。

Abstract: At muon colliders, muon decays naturally produce intense electrons and positrons with unique features, namely high energies, high repetition rates, and small intrinsic uncertainties, that are unavailable at existing accelerator facilities. We quantitatively study the feasibility of extracting such particles in two representative future muon collider designs, IMCC and $μ$TRISTAN. Using Monte Carlo simulations with the corresponding design parameters, we study the spatial, angular, and energy distributions of decay electrons and positrons in the curved sections of the collider ring. We find that typical deflections of $0.1-10~\mathrm{mrad}$ can be achieved even for high-energy electrons carrying large energy fractions ($\simeq 0.6 - 1.0$) of the muon beam energy, with the ring bending magnets (or magnets providing an equivalent field) effectively serving as a pre-septum magnet, that partially deflects the beam before the main septum magnet, suggesting that the extraction scheme could be practically feasible. Exploiting the distinct beam properties of IMCC and $μ$TRISTAN, we propose complementary search strategies, missing energy and momentum searches for dark matter at $μ$TRISTAN and visible-decay searches for axion-like particles and light scalars at IMCC, which probe parameter space beyond the reach of current and other proposed experiments.
