### [59] [Flavor Democracy Calls for Vector Like Leptons and Quarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05104)
*Burak Dagli,Saleh Sultansoy,Ismail Toy*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper argues that Flavor Democracy in the Standard Model is challenged by the large top quark mass, but can be restored by introducing Vector-Like Leptons (VLLs) and Vector-Like Quarks (VLQs). Current experimental searches for VLLs are limited to a Restricted Model with unrealistic assumptions, necessitating a broader analysis covering all viable decay channels.
\n\n
本文指出，标准模型中的Flavor Democracy假设因顶夸克质量过大而面临挑战，但可通过引入Vector-Like Leptons（VLLs）和Vector-Like Quarks（VLQs）予以恢复。当前ATLAS和CMS对VLLs的实验搜索局限于一个具有不现实假设的Restricted Model，因此亟需开展涵盖所有可行衰变道的更全面分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the tension between the Flavor Democracy hypothesis—which posits that all fermion generations are fundamentally equivalent at high energy—and the observed large hierarchy in fermion masses, particularly $m_t \gg m_b, m_\tau$. The exclusion of a fourth SM generation by Higgs data removes a previously plausible solution, prompting the exploration of extensions involving VLLs and VLQs that preserve the spirit of Flavor Democracy while fitting current data.
\n\n
动机源于Flavor Democracy假设（即在高能下所有费米子代本质上等价）与观测到的费米子质量层级（特别是$m_t \gg m_b, m_\tau$）之间的张力。由于希格斯数据已基本排除第四代标准模型，促使作者探索引入VLLs和VLQs的扩展方案，以在符合当前实验约束的同时保留Flavor Democracy的核心思想。

Method: The paper proposes a theoretical framework where Vector-Like Leptons and Vector-Like Quarks are added to the Standard Model. These vector-like fermions mix with the SM chiral fermions, generating realistic mass hierarchies through the democratic mass matrix mechanism. The authors critique the current experimental strategy—based on a Restricted Model assuming degenerate VLL doublet masses and no right-handed neutrinos—and advocate for a generalized phenomenological analysis that includes all kinematically allowed decay channels and non-degenerate mass spectra.
\n\n
本文提出一种理论框架，在标准模型中引入Vector-Like Leptons和Vector-Like Quarks。这些矢量型费米子与标准模型手征费米子混合，通过democratic mass matrix机制生成合理的质量层级。作者批评了当前基于Restricted Model的实验策略（该模型假设VLL双重态质量简并且不存在右手中微子），并主张开展更一般的唯象分析，涵盖所有运动学允许的衰变道及非简并质量谱。

Result: The introduction of VLLs and VLQs successfully reconciles the Flavor Democracy hypothesis with the observed fermion mass spectrum, including the heavy top quark. However, existing LHC constraints on VLLs are shown to be incomplete because they rely on overly restrictive assumptions. A general model allows for richer decay topologies and weaker current bounds, implying that significant regions of parameter space remain unexplored.
\n\n
引入VLLs和VLQs成功地将Flavor Democracy假设与包括重顶夸克在内的观测费米子质量谱相协调。然而，现有LHC对VLLs的限制被证明是不完整的，因其依赖于过度简化的假设。一般模型允许更丰富的衰变拓扑结构和更弱的当前限制，意味着大量参数空间尚未被探索。

Conclusion: To fully test the viability of Flavor Democracy in light of the top quark mass, future collider searches must move beyond the Restricted Model and adopt a comprehensive approach that accounts for non-degenerate VLL/VLQ masses, right-handed neutrinos, and all possible decay channels. This would ensure that experimental limits genuinely reflect the theoretical landscape of realistic Flavor Democracy scenarios.
\n\n
为充分检验Flavor Democracy在顶夸克质量背景下的可行性，未来对撞机搜索必须超越Restricted Model，采用涵盖非简并VLL/VLQ质量、右手中微子及所有可能衰变道的综合方法。这将确保实验限制真实反映Flavor Democracy现实场景的理论图景。

Abstract: There are strong arguments favoring the Flavor Democracy hypothesis (or the Democratic Mass Matrix approach) within the Standard Model framework. However, the large mass of the top quark ($m_t >> m_b, m_τ$) poses an obstacle to the functioning of Flavor Democracy in the three SM family scenario. While a fourth Standard Model generation could have provided a natural resolution, this possibility is now almost entirely excluded by precision data on Higgs boson production and decay rates. The Flavor Democracy hypothesis can be elegantly resurrected through the introduction of Vector-Like Leptons (VLLs) and Vector-Like Quarks (VLQs), which naturally accommodate the observed fermion mass hierarchies while remaining consistent with current experimental constraints. Currently, experimental searches for VLLs conducted by the ATLAS and CMS collaborations rely on a highly constrained Restricted Model. This model imposes a mass degeneracy between charged and neutral VLLs within a doublet and assumes the absence of right-handed neutrinos. Consequently, current results are valid only for the restricted model and do not cover a more realistic, general scenario. Therefore, to accurately reflect the physical reality, it is imperative to conduct a comprehensive re-evaluation that incorporates all viable decay channels.

### [60] [TeV-scale unification of light dark matter and neutrino mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05200)
*Cheng-Wei Chiang,Shu-Yu Ho,Van Que Tran*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: TeV-scale heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) in an inverse-seesaw framework simultaneously explain neutrino masses, generate sub-GeV dark matter (DM) via freeze-in, and mediate its decay into neutrinos. The DM is a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson from spontaneous lepton number breaking, with its mass from a small explicit breaking term. This leads to testable correlations between neutrino physics, DM relic density, and lifetime, with signals expected at Hyper-Kamiokande, DUNE, and JUNO.
\n\n
在逆跷跷板（inverse-seesaw）机制中，TeV 能标的重惰性轻子（heavy neutral leptons, HNLs）同时解释了中微子质量、通过 freeze-in 机制生成亚 GeV 暗物质（dark matter, DM），并介导其衰变为中微子。该暗物质是轻子数自发破缺产生的 pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone 玻色子，其质量来源于微小的显式破缺项。这一框架在中微子物理、暗物质遗迹密度和寿命之间建立了可观测的关联，相关信号有望在 Hyper-Kamiokande、DUNE 和 JUNO 等下一代探测器中被观测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to unify the origin of neutrino masses and dark matter within a minimal, testable theoretical framework. Standard mechanisms for neutrino mass generation (e.g., seesaw) often involve very high scales that decouple from observable DM phenomena. Here, the authors address this by employing TeV-scale HNLs in an inverse-seesaw setup, which allows both neutrino mass generation and DM dynamics to occur at experimentally accessible energies. Additionally, they seek to explain the stability and abundance of DM through the same particle content responsible for neutrino masses.
\n\n
本文旨在在一个极简且可检验的理论框架内统一中微子质量和暗物质的起源。传统的中微子质量生成机制（如跷跷板机制）通常涉及极高能标，导致与可观测的暗物质现象脱耦。作者通过引入 TeV 能标的重惰性轻子（HNLs）构建逆跷跷板模型，使得中微子质量生成与暗物质动力学均发生在实验可及的能量尺度上。此外，他们试图利用产生中微子质量的相同粒子内容来解释暗物质的稳定性与宇宙丰度。

Method: The authors construct a model where lepton number $U(1)_L$ is spontaneously broken, yielding a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson identified as the DM candidate. A small explicit breaking term gives the DM a non-zero mass. TeV-scale HNLs are introduced to realize the inverse-seesaw mechanism for neutrino mass generation. These same HNLs couple to the DM and the Standard Model neutrinos, enabling DM production via the freeze-in mechanism and mediating its decay into neutrinos. The relic abundance is computed using freeze-in thermodynamics, while the DM lifetime is derived from the effective decay operator induced by HNL exchange. Predictions for neutrino telescopes are obtained by linking the DM decay rate to observable neutrino fluxes.
\n\n
作者构建了一个轻子数 $U(1)_L$ 自发破缺的模型，由此产生的 pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone 玻色子被认定为暗物质候选者；微小的显式破缺项赋予其非零质量。引入 TeV 能标的重惰性轻子（HNLs）以实现逆跷跷板机制生成中微子质量。这些 HNLs 同时耦合到暗物质与标准模型中微子，使得暗物质可通过 freeze-in 机制产生，并通过 HNL 交换介导其衰变为中微子。遗迹丰度通过 freeze-in 热力学计算，而暗物质寿命则由 HNL 诱导的有效衰变算符导出。通过将暗物质衰变率与可观测的中微子通量关联，得到对中微子望远镜的预测。

Result: The model predicts a tight correlation among the light neutrino masses, the DM relic density, and the DM lifetime due to their common dependence on the HNL couplings and masses. For TeV-scale HNLs consistent with collider searches, the required relic abundance and observed lower bounds on DM lifetime constrain the DM mass to be sub-GeV. This parameter space yields DM decay-induced neutrino fluxes within reach of next-generation experiments like Hyper-Kamiokande, DUNE, and JUNO, offering a falsifiable link between neutrino mass generation and dark matter.
\n\n
该模型预言了轻中微子质量、暗物质遗迹密度与暗物质寿命之间的紧密关联，因为它们共同依赖于重惰性轻子（HNLs）的耦合与质量。对于与对撞机搜索相容的 TeV 能标 HNLs，所需的遗迹丰度与当前暗物质寿命下限将暗物质质量限制在亚 GeV 范围。此参数空间所产生的暗物质衰变诱导的中微子通量处于下一代实验（如 Hyper-Kamiokande、DUNE 和 JUNO）的探测灵敏度范围内，从而为中微子质量生成与暗物质之间提供了可证伪的联系。

Conclusion: This work presents a predictive and testable framework connecting neutrino mass generation via TeV-scale inverse-seesaw HNLs to sub-GeV pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone dark matter. The same HNLs responsible for neutrino masses also govern DM production and decay, leading to correlated observables in neutrino experiments. Upcoming detectors will critically test this scenario, potentially revealing a unified origin of neutrino mass and dark matter.
\n\n
本工作提出了一个具有预言能力且可检验的框架，将 TeV 能标逆跷跷板 HNLs 产生的中微子质量与亚 GeV 的 pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone 暗物质联系起来。产生中微子质量的同一组 HNLs 也主导了暗物质的产生与衰变，从而在中微子实验中产生关联的可观测量。即将运行的探测器将对该机制进行关键检验，有望揭示中微子质量与暗物质的统一起源。

Abstract: We demonstrate that TeV-scale heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) responsible for inverse-seesaw neutrino mass generation can simultaneously fix the cosmological abundance and decay properties of dark matter (DM). The spontaneous breaking of lepton number gives rise to a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson that serves as a light DM candidate, whose mass originates from a small explicit breaking term. The same HNLs that generate neutrino masses produce the DM via freeze-in and mediate its decay into neutrinos, leading to a tight correlation among neutrino masses, DM relic abundance, and DM lifetime. For collider-accessible TeV-scale HNLs, the observed relic density and lifetime constraints point to sub-GeV DM, yielding observable neutrino signals at next-generation detectors such as Hyper-Kamiokande, DUNE, and JUNO. This framework establishes a predictive and experimentally testable link between neutrino mass generation and dark matter.

### [61] [Effective vertexes in magnetized quark-gluon plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05248)
*V. Skalozub*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates one-loop quark contributions to the effective potential in high-temperature quark-gluon plasma (QGP), focusing on effective vertices coupling magnetic fields ($b^3, b^8, b$) and the $A_0$ condensate. These vertices yield novel experimental signatures of QGP formation in heavy-ion collisions.
\n\n
本文研究了高温夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）中单圈夸克对有效势的贡献，重点关注磁場（$b^3, b^8, b$）与 $A_0$ 凝聚之间的有效顶点。这些顶点产生了重离子碰撞实验中QGP形成的新型可观测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous work established a two-loop effective potential in SU(2) gluodynamics and full QCD that accounts for spontaneous generation of color and electromagnetic magnetic fields ($b^3, b^8, b \\neq 0$) and the $A_0(T)$ condensate at high temperature $T$. However, quark contributions—especially at one-loop level—and their induced interactions between magnetic backgrounds and $A_0$ were not fully explored. The authors aim to fill this gap to uncover new phenomenological signatures in QGP.
\n\n
先前的工作已在SU(2)胶子动力学和完整量子色动力学（QCD）中建立了包含自发产生的色磁場（$b^3, b^8$）和普通磁場（$b \\neq 0$）以及 $A_0(T)$ 凝聚的双圈有效势。然而，夸克贡献——尤其是单圈级别的贡献——及其诱导的磁背景与 $A_0$ 之间的相互作用尚未被充分研究。作者旨在填补这一空白，以揭示QGP中的新现象学信号。

Method: The authors compute one-loop quark contributions to the finite-temperature effective potential $W(T, b^3, b^8, b, A_0)$ in the presence of both Abelian magnetic fields and the $A_0$ condensate. They derive effective vertices describing couplings between quarks, magnetic fields, and the temporal gauge field $A_0$, using thermal quantum field theory techniques and the background field method. The calculation leverages the known generalization of Bernoulli polynomial integral representations adapted to magnetic backgrounds.
\n\n
作者在阿贝尔磁場和 $A_0$ 凝聚共存的情况下，计算有限温度有效势 $W(T, b^3, b^8, b, A_0)$ 中的单圈夸克贡献。他们利用热量子场论技术和背景场方法，推导出描述夸克、磁場与时间分量规范场 $A_0$ 之间耦合的有效顶点。该计算基于适用于磁背景的伯努利多项式积分表示的已知推广形式。

Result: The paper derives explicit one-loop effective vertices coupling the magnetic fields ($b^3, b^8, b$) and the $A_0$ condensate. These vertices generate new interaction terms in the effective action, leading to specific, potentially observable effects in heavy-ion collision experiments that signal the formation of QGP. The results complement earlier two-loop gluonic calculations and complete the leading-order fermionic sector of the effective potential.
\n\n
本文推导出了磁場（$b^3, b^8, b$）与 $A_0$ 凝聚之间明确的单圈有效顶点。这些顶点在有效作用量中产生新的相互作用项，导致重离子碰撞实验中可探测的特定效应，用以标志QGP的形成。该结果补充了早期的双圈胶子计算，并完成了有效势中领头阶费米子部分。

Conclusion: Including one-loop quark contributions reveals new effective couplings between magnetic fields and the $A_0$ condensate in high-temperature QGP. These couplings provide distinctive experimental signatures for QGP creation, enhancing our understanding of non-perturbative dynamics in hot QCD and the role of spontaneous magnetization and $A_0$ stabilization mechanisms.
\n\n
包含单圈夸克贡献揭示了高温QGP中磁場与 $A_0$ 凝聚之间的新有效耦合。这些耦合为QGP的产生提供了独特的实验信号，深化了我们对高温QCD中非微扰动力学、自发磁化以及 $A_0$ 稳定机制的理解。

Abstract: In quark-gluon plasma (QGP), at high temperatures $T$ the spontaneous generation of color magnetic fields, $b^3(T), b^8(T) \not = 0$ (3, 8 are color indexes), and usual magnetic field $b(T) \not = 0$ happens. Also, the Polyakov loop and related to it the $A_0(T)$ condensate, which is solution to Yang-Mills imaginary time equations, create.
  Recently, with the new type two-loop effective potential, which generalizes the known integral representation for the Bernoulli polynomials and takes into consideration the magnetic background, these effects were derived.
  The corresponding effective potential $W(T, b^3, b^8, b, A_0 )$ was calculated either in SU(2) gluodynamics or full quantum chromodynamics (QCD). The values of magnetic field strengths at different temperatures were calculated and the mechanism for stabilizing the background due to $A_0(T)$ was also discovered.
  In present paper, we concentrate on the one-loop quark contributions. In particular, we derive the effective vertexes, which couple magnetic fields and $A_0$. The vertexes result in new specific effects signalling the creation of QGP in heavy ion collision experiments.
  Key words: spontaneous magnetization, high temperature, asymptotic freedom, effective potential, $A_0$ condensate, effective vertexes.

### [62] [Axial-vector neutral-current measurements in coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05281)

TL;DR: This paper investigates the feasibility of measuring axial-current contributions to coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CE$ν$NS), identifying fluorine-based targets—especially $\text{C}_3\text{F}_8$—as optimal due to their non-zero nuclear spin and experimental relevance. It shows that with current neutrino sources (pion decay-at-rest and reactor fluxes), the axial coupling can be constrained at the $\sim 10\%$ level, enabling probes of spin-dependent new physics.
\n\n
本文研究了在相干弹性中微子-原子核散射（CE$ν$NS）中测量轴矢流贡献的可行性，指出含氟靶材（尤其是$\text{C}_3\text{F}_8$）因其非零核自旋和实验相关性而最为理想。研究表明，利用现有中微子源（静止π介子衰变和反应堆中微子），可在$\sim 10\%$精度上约束轴矢耦合，从而探测自旋依赖的新物理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While CE$ν$NS is dominated by vector neutral-current interactions, the axial-current component—though subleading—is crucial for probing spin-dependent couplings and potential new physics beyond the Standard Model. However, this contribution has been largely neglected experimentally due to its small size and measurement challenges. The authors aim to quantify its observability and identify optimal target materials to access it.
\n\n
尽管CE$ν$NS主要由矢量中性流相互作用主导，但轴矢流分量（尽管是次领头阶）对于探测自旋依赖耦合及标准模型之外的新物理至关重要。然而，由于其信号微弱且测量困难，该贡献在实验上长期被忽视。作者旨在量化其可观测性并识别最优靶材以提取该信号。

Method: The authors compare the relative magnitudes of vector and axial contributions to the CE$ν$NS cross section across various target nuclei used in neutrino and dark matter experiments. They focus on nuclei with non-zero ground-state spin, particularly fluorine-containing compounds. Using known nuclear structure factors and standard weak interaction theory, they compute event rates for both pion decay-at-rest and reactor neutrino spectra, incorporating realistic detector thresholds and flux uncertainties to assess sensitivity to the axial coupling $g_A$.
\n\n
作者比较了在各类中微子与暗物质实验所用靶核中，CE$ν$NS截面中矢量与轴矢贡献的相对大小，重点关注具有非零基态自旋的原子核，特别是含氟化合物。他们基于已知的核结构因子和标准弱相互作用理论，计算了静止π介子衰变和反应堆中微子谱下的事例率，并结合实际探测器阈值和通量不确定性，评估对轴矢耦合$g_A$的灵敏度。

Result: Fluorine-based targets, especially octafluoropropane ($\text{C}_3\text{F}_8$), exhibit the largest axial-to-vector event rate ratio among commonly used materials. With current experimental setups and neutrino sources, the axial coupling can be indirectly measured at the $\sim 10\%$ precision level. This sensitivity enables constraints on spin-dependent new physics scenarios via CE$ν$NS.
\n\n
含氟靶材（尤其是八氟丙烷$\text{C}_3\text{F}_8$）在常用材料中展现出最大的轴矢/矢量事例率比。利用当前实验装置和中微子源，可间接以$\sim 10\%$的精度测量轴矢耦合。该灵敏度使得通过CE$ν$NS对自旋依赖的新物理场景施加限制成为可能。

Conclusion: Axial-current effects in CE$ν$NS, though small, are measurable with appropriate target selection and existing neutrino sources. Fluorine-rich compounds like $\text{C}_3\text{F}_8$ offer a viable pathway to probe the axial coupling and, by extension, spin-dependent beyond-Standard-Model physics. This work motivates dedicated analyses in ongoing and future CE$ν$NS experiments to extract axial contributions.
\n\n
CE$ν$NS中的轴矢流效应虽小，但通过合理选择靶材和利用现有中微子源即可测量。富含氟的化合物（如$\text{C}_3\text{F}_8$）为探测轴矢耦合、进而探索自旋依赖的标准模型之外新物理提供了可行路径。本研究激励在当前及未来的CE$ν$NS实验中开展专门分析以提取轴矢贡献。

Abstract: Coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CE$ν$NS) is predominantly governed by vector neutral-current interactions, with subleading contributions arising from the axial current in nuclei with non-zero ground-state spin. Experimentally, the extraction of axial-current contributions has been so far of little interest, mainly because of the challenges its measurement entail. In this work, we investigate the relative size of the vector and axial components for target materials currently employed by the neutrino and dark matter experimental communities. We identify fluorine-based compounds as the most promising targets for probing the axial-current event rate. Among them, octafluoropropane ($\text{C}_3\text{F}_8$) emerges as a particularly suitable candidate, given its widespread use in spin-dependent dark matter searches and its relevance for upcoming dedicated CE$ν$NS experiments. Considering both pion decay-at-rest and reactor neutrino fluxes, we show that such measurements can allow an indirect determination of the axial coupling at the $\sim 10\%$ level, depending on flux uncertainties and detector thresholds. We further emphasize that measurements of the axial current will allow to probe spin-dependent new physics scenarios through CE$ν$NS.

</details>


### [63] [The eV-Scale Sterile Neutrino and Neutrinoless Double Beta Decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05304)
*Priya,Simran Arora,B. C. Chauhan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates eV-scale sterile neutrino models (3+1, 1+3, 2+2) to explain the LSND/MiniBooNE anomalies using updated neutrinoless double beta decay ($0\nu\beta\beta$) data and global fits. The 3+1 model is favored, with sterile neutrino mass constrained to ~4.75 eV (NH) and ~4.72 eV (IH) at $3\sigma$, and total neutrino mass sum limited to ~4.8 eV.
\n\n
本文利用更新的无中微子双贝塔衰变（$0\\nu\\beta\\beta$）数据和全局拟合结果，研究了eV能标的惰性中微子模型（3+1、1+3、2+2）以解释LSND/MiniBooNE反常。其中3+1模型最受支持，在$3\\sigma$置信度下，惰性中微子质量相对于最轻中微子质量被限制为~4.75 eV（正序）和~4.72 eV（倒序），四中微子总质量上限约为4.8 eV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the persistent short-baseline anomalies observed in LSND and MiniBooNE experiments, which show an excess of electron neutrinos inconsistent with standard three-neutrino oscillations. Introducing sterile neutrinos at the eV scale offers a potential explanation, and this work aims to test such scenarios against constraints from neutrinoless double beta decay and global oscillation data.
\n\n
动机源于LSND和MiniBooNE实验中持续存在的短基线反常现象——观测到的电子中微子超出无法用标准三中微子振荡解释。引入eV能标的sterile neutrino（惰性中微子）可提供潜在解释，本文旨在结合无中微子双贝塔衰变约束与全局振荡数据检验此类模型。

Method: The authors analyze three sterile neutrino mixing schemes—3+1, 1+3, and 2+2—within both normal hierarchy (NH) and inverted hierarchy (IH) frameworks for the active neutrino masses. They incorporate updated experimental limits on the effective Majorana mass $|m_{\beta\beta}|$ from neutrinoless double beta decay searches and use global fit data on neutrino oscillation parameters to constrain the sterile neutrino mass $m_s$ and the lightest active neutrino mass $m_{\text{lightest}}$.
\n\n
作者在活性中微子质量的正序（NH）和倒序（IH）框架下，分析了三种惰性中微子混合方案——3+1、1+3和2+2。他们结合来自无中微子双贝塔衰变实验对有效马约拉纳质量$|m_{\\beta\\beta}|$的最新限制，并利用中微子振荡参数的全局拟合数据，对惰性中微子质量$m_s$和最轻活性中微子质量$m_{\\text{lightest}}$进行约束。

Result: The 3+1 scheme is statistically preferred. At $3\sigma$ confidence level, the sterile neutrino mass is constrained to $m_s \approx 4.75~\text{eV}$ for NH and $4.72~\text{eV}$ for IH relative to $m_{\text{lightest}}$. The total sum of the four neutrino masses is limited to $\Sigma m_\nu < 4.81~\text{eV}$ (NH) and $< 4.78~\text{eV}$ (IH). Other schemes (1+3, 2+2) are less viable under current $0\nu\beta\beta$ constraints.
\n\n
3+1方案在统计上更受青睐。在$3\\sigma$置信度下，相对于$m_{\\text{lightest}}$，惰性中微子质量被限制为：正序时$m_s \\approx 4.75~\\text{eV}$，倒序时为$4.72~\\text{eV}$。四中微子总质量上限为：正序$\Sigma m_\\nu < 4.81~\\text{eV}$，倒序$< 4.78~\\text{eV}$。其他方案（1+3、2+2）在当前$0\\nu\\beta\\beta$约束下可行性较低。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the 3+1 sterile neutrino model remains compatible with current neutrinoless double beta decay limits and can accommodate the LSND/MiniBooNE anomalies while predicting specific mass ranges for sterile and active neutrinos. Future $0\nu\beta\beta$ experiments will further test these scenarios by probing the allowed parameter space more stringently.
\n\n
研究表明，3+1惰性中微子模型仍与当前无中微子双贝塔衰变限制兼容，可在解释LSND/MiniBooNE反常的同时预言惰性与活性中微子的具体质量范围。未来的$0\\nu\\beta\\beta$实验将通过更严格地探测允许参数空间，进一步检验这些模型。

Abstract: In short-baseline experiments such as LSND and MiniBooNE, an excess of electron neutrinos has been observed, originating from a muon neutrino beam. To address this anomaly, in the line of many works, we investigate various neutrino mixing schemes involving eV-scale sterile neutrinos alongside three active neutrinos. Using updated experimental and global fit data, we studied neutrinoless double beta decay for three different schemes such as 3+1, 1 + 3, and 2 + 2, which involve one sterile neutrino and three active neutrinos. We have done analysis of these schemes for normal hierarchy (NH) as well as for inverted hierarchy (IH) frameworks, and constrained the sterile neutrino mass in light of current and future neutrinoless double beta decay experiments. The 3+1 scheme is found to be the most viable and at the level of $3σ$ the mass of sterile neutrino with respect to the lightest neutrino mass ($m_{\text{lightest}}$) is restricted to $4.75~eV$ for the NH and $4.72~eV$ for the IH. Additionally, the limits on the sum of four neutrino masses are determined to be $4.81~eV$ for the normal hierarchy and $4.78~eV$ for the inverted hierarchy. The updated analysis of all these schemes would help us in understanding physics governing neutrinoless double beta decay and limit on the mass of sterile neutrinos.

### [64] [Exploring $T_{ΥΥ}$ tetraquark candidates in a coupled-channels formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05311)
*P. G. Ortega,D. R. Entem,F. Fernandez,J. Segovia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study $T_{ΥΥ}$ tetraquark candidates using a coupled-channels approach, identifying numerous resonant and virtual states between the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ and $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ thresholds. These states form approximate heavy-quark spin symmetry multiplets, with widths from tens to hundreds of MeV. Many couple preferentially to channels with excited bottomonia, offering guidance for experimental searches in the $bb\bar b\bar b$ sector.
\n\n
我们采用耦合道方法研究 $T_{ΥΥ}$ 四夸克候选态，在 $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ 与 $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ 阈值之间识别出大量共振态和虚态。这些态近似构成重夸克自旋对称性多重态，宽度从几十到几百 MeV 不等。许多态优先耦合到包含激发底偶素的末态，为 $bb\bar b\bar b$ 体系中的实验搜寻提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to explore the existence and properties of fully-heavy $bb\bar b\bar b$ tetraquarks—specifically $T_{ΥΥ}$ candidates—motivated by recent experimental interest in exotic hadrons and the theoretical expectation that such systems may exhibit stable or narrow structures due to heavy-quark dynamics. Understanding their spectrum tests fundamental aspects like coupled-channel effects and heavy-quark spin symmetry (HQSS) in a regime where perturbative QCD is less reliable.
\n\n
本文旨在探索全重 $bb\bar b\bar b$ 四夸克态（特别是 $T_{ΥΥ}$ 候选者）的存在性与性质，其动机源于近期对奇特强子的实验兴趣，以及理论预期：由于重夸克动力学，此类系统可能呈现稳定或窄宽结构。理解其谱结构可检验耦合道效应和重夸克自旋对称性（HQSS）等基本性质，而该区域微扰 QCD 并不适用。

Method: The authors employ a coupled-channels framework based on the resonating group method (RGM) derived from a constituent quark model. They consider all meson-meson combinations of $Υ(1S)$, $Υ(2S)$, $η_b(1S)$, and $η_b(2S)$ with orbital angular momentum $L \leq 2$ across $J^P = 0^\pm, 1^\pm, 2^\pm$ quantum numbers. The interaction kernel is computed microscopically, and physical states are identified as poles of the scattering matrix ($S$-matrix) in the complex energy plane, distinguishing between resonances (poles on unphysical Riemann sheets) and virtual states (poles on the physical sheet below threshold).
\n\n
作者采用基于组分夸克模型并通过共振群方法（RGM）导出的耦合道框架。他们考虑了 $Υ(1S)$、$Υ(2S)$、$η_b(1S)$ 和 $η_b(2S)$ 的所有介子-介子组合，轨道角动量 $L \leq 2$，涵盖 $J^P = 0^\pm, 1^\pm, 2^\pm$ 量子数。相互作用核由微观计算得出，物理态通过散射矩阵（$S$-矩阵）在复能量平面上的极点来识别，区分共振态（非物理黎曼面上的极点）与虚态（物理面上阈值以下的极点）。

Result: The analysis reveals a rich spectrum of poles: multiple resonant and virtual states appear between the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ and $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ thresholds. These poles organize into approximate heavy-quark spin symmetry (HQSS) multiplets. Low-mass states are often dominated by a single channel and correspond to threshold enhancements, while higher-mass states exhibit significant mixing among channels involving radially excited bottomonia. Predicted widths range from $\sim$10 MeV to several hundred MeV. Branching ratios show that many states decay predominantly into final states containing at least one excited bottomonium ($Υ(2S)$ or $η_b(2S)$), implying limited visibility in ground-state-only channels like $Υ(1S)Υ(1S)$.
\n\n
分析揭示了丰富的极点谱：在 $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ 与 $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ 阈值之间出现多个共振态和虚态。这些极点近似构成重夸克自旋对称性（HQSS）多重态。低质量态通常由单一通道主导，对应于阈值增强结构；而高质量态则在包含径向激发底偶素的通道间表现出显著混合。预测宽度范围从约 10 MeV 到几百 MeV。分支比表明，许多态主要衰变到至少包含一个激发底偶素（$Υ(2S)$ 或 $η_b(2S)$）的末态，意味着它们在仅含基态的通道（如 $Υ(1S)Υ(1S)$）中难以观测。

Conclusion: The study provides a comprehensive prediction of the $bb\bar b\bar b$ tetraquark spectrum within a microscopic coupled-channels approach, demonstrating that HQSS is approximately realized and that threshold effects and channel mixing play crucial roles. The results offer concrete benchmarks for future experiments at facilities like LHCb and Belle II, emphasizing the need to search in channels with excited bottomonia to uncover the full spectrum of fully-heavy tetraquarks.
\n\n
本研究通过微观耦合道方法对 $bb\bar b\bar b$ 四夸克谱给出了全面预测，表明重夸克自旋对称性近似成立，且阈值效应与通道混合起关键作用。结果为 LHCb 和 Belle II 等未来实验提供了具体基准，强调需在包含激发底偶素的通道中进行搜寻，以揭示全重四夸克态的完整谱结构。

Abstract: We investigate the spectrum of $T_{ΥΥ}$ tetraquark candidates within a coupled-channels framework. The analysis includes all $L\leq2$ combinations of $Υ(1S)$, $Υ(2S)$, $η_b(1S)$, and $η_b(2S)$ in the $J^P = 0^\pm, 1^\pm, 2^\pm$ sectors. The meson-meson interaction is derived from an underlying constituent quark model through the resonating group method, and the properties of the states are obtained from poles of the scattering matrix. We find a rich spectrum of resonant, and virtual, states distributed between the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ and $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ thresholds. The pattern of poles exhibits approximate heavy-quark spin symmetry multiplets. Several states are dominated by a single channel and can be associated with threshold-driven structures, while higher-mass resonances show sizable mixing among channels involving radially excited bottomonia. The predicted widths range from tens to several hundred MeV. Branching ratios indicate that many states couple predominantly to final states with at least one excited bottomonium, whereas only a subset of the spectrum is expected to be visible in the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$, $η_b(1S)Υ(1S)$ and $Υ(1S)Υ(1S)$ channels. These results provide quantitative guidance for experimental searches of fully heavy tetraquarks and offer a test of coupled-channel dynamics and heavy-quark spin symmetry in the $bb\bar b\bar b$ sector.

</details>


### [65] [Renormalization and Factorization Scale-Invariant Predictions for the Higgs Rare Decay $H\to J/ψ+γ$ via the Principle of Maximum Conformality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05329)
*Qi-Sha Ran,Xing-Gang Wu,Jiang Yan,Xu-Chang Zheng,Chang-Xin Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper computes the decay width of the rare Higgs decay $H \to J/\psi + \gamma$ using nonrelativistic QCD (NRQCD) at next-to-next-to-leading order (N$^2$LO), employing the Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC) to eliminate renormalization and factorization scale ambiguities. The result is a precise, scale-invariant prediction: $\Gamma(H\to J/\psi+\gamma) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) \times 10^{-11}$ GeV, offering a clean probe of the charm-quark Yukawa coupling.
\n\n
本文在非相对论性量子色动力学（NRQCD）框架下，计算了稀有希格斯衰变过程 $H \to J/\psi + \gamma$ 的衰变宽度，达到了次次领头阶（N$^2$LO）。通过应用最大共形原理（Principle of Maximum Conformality, PMC），消除了重整化标度和因子化标度的模糊性，得到了一个精确且标度不变的预言：$\Gamma(H\to J/\psi+\gamma) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) \times 10^{-11}$ GeV，为提取粲夸克Yukawa耦合提供了一个干净的探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to precisely determine the charm-quark Yukawa coupling via the rare exclusive Higgs decay $H \to J/\psi + \gamma$, which is theoretically clean in NRQCD. Traditional fixed-order predictions suffer from large renormalization- and factorization-scale uncertainties, undermining reliability. The authors aim to overcome these limitations by applying the Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC), which systematically eliminates scheme and scale ambiguities in perturbative QCD.
\n\n
动机在于通过稀有专属希格斯衰变 $H \to J/\psi + \gamma$ 精确测定粲夸克Yukawa耦合，该过程在非相对论性量子色动力学（NRQCD）中具有理论上的清洁性。传统固定阶微扰计算受制于显著的重整化标度和因子化标度不确定性，影响结果可靠性。作者旨在通过应用最大共形原理（Principle of Maximum Conformality, PMC）系统性地消除微扰QCD中的方案与标度模糊性，从而克服这些局限。

Method: The calculation uses NRQCD factorization at N$^2$LO in QCD. The short-distance coefficient is computed perturbatively, while the long-distance matrix element (LDME) is extracted from the measured leptonic decay width $\Gamma_{J/\psi \to e^+e^-}$. Large logarithms from Yukawa coupling renormalization are resummed. Crucially, the Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC) is applied to fix the renormalization scale order-by-order, removing conventional scale dependence. The factorization-scale dependence in the LDME and short-distance coefficient cancels exactly, yielding a scale-invariant total decay width.
\n\n
计算方法基于NRQCD因子化，在QCD微扰展开中达到N$^2$LO阶。短程系数通过微扰论计算，而长程矩阵元（LDME）则从实验测量的 $J/\psi$ 轻子衰变宽度 $\Gamma_{J/\psi \to e^+e^-}$ 中提取。对来自Yukawa耦合重整化的大对数项进行了重求和。关键创新在于应用最大共形原理（PMC），逐阶确定重整化标度，从而消除传统标度依赖性。LDME与短程系数中的因子化标度依赖性精确抵消，最终得到标度不变的总衰变宽度。

Result: The authors obtain a factorization- and renormalization-scale-invariant prediction for the decay width: $\Gamma(H\to J/\psi+\gamma) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) \times 10^{-11}$ GeV. The uncertainty combines errors from $\Delta\alpha_s(m_Z)$, $\Delta\Gamma_{J/\psi\to e^+e^-}$, $\Delta\overline{m}_c(\overline{m}_c)$, and an estimate of N$^3$LO contributions via Bayesian analysis. The perturbative series shows good convergence and no artificial scale dependence.
\n\n
作者得到了一个同时消除因子化标度和重整化标度依赖性的衰变宽度预言：$\Gamma(H\to J/\psi+\gamma) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) \times 10^{-11}$ GeV。不确定性来源于 $\Delta\alpha_s(m_Z)$、$\Delta\Gamma_{J/\psi\to e^+e^-}$、$\Delta\overline{m}_c(\overline{m}_c)$ 以及通过贝叶斯分析对N$^3$LO贡献的估计。微扰级数表现出良好的收敛性，且无任何人为标度依赖。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates for the first time that the Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC) can be successfully applied to exclusive Higgs decay processes involving heavy quarkonia, yielding fixed-order predictions that are invariant under both renormalization and factorization scale variations. This provides a robust, precise theoretical framework for extracting the charm-quark Yukawa coupling from future high-luminosity LHC data.
\n\n
本工作首次证明，最大共形原理（PMC）可成功应用于涉及重夸克偶素的专属希格斯衰变过程，得到在重整化标度和因子化标度变化下均保持不变的固定阶微扰预言。这为未来高亮度LHC实验中精确提取粲夸克Yukawa耦合提供了稳健可靠的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the \(J/ψ\) direct production mechanism in the rare exclusive Higgs decay \(H\to J/ψ+γ\) within nonrelativistic QCD (NRQCD), which provides a clean probe for extracting the charm-quark Yukawa coupling to the Higgs boson. The Principle of Maximum Conformality (PMC) is used to remove conventional renormalization-scheme and scale ambiguities in the next-to-next-to-leading-order (N\(^2\)LO) perturbative QCD series. Large logarithmic contributions arising from Yukawa coupling renormalization are resummed, providing a reliable foundation for subsequent analyses. Using the experimentally measured leptonic decay width of \(J/ψ\) and the N\(^2\)LO perturbative result, we extract the factorization-scale-dependent long-distance matrix element \(\langle J/ψ({\bm ε})|ψ^{\dagger}{\bm σ}\cdot{\bm ε}χ(μ_Λ) |0\rangle\). Combining this with the factorization-scale-dependent short-distance coefficient, we obtain a factorization-scale-invariant decay width for the channel. Compared with earlier predictions in the literature, our fixed-order result for \(Γ(H\to J/ψ+γ)\) is more robust and precise, with good convergence and no renormalization- or factorization-scale dependence. We find \(Γ(H\to J/ψ+γ) = (6.4574^{+0.3995}_{-0.3995}) \times 10^{-11}\) GeV, where the uncertainty is the quadratic sum of contributions from \(Δα_s(m_Z) = \pm 0.0009\), \(ΔΓ_{J/ψ\to e^+e^-} = \pm 0.10\ \text{GeV}\), \(Δ\overline{m}_c(\overline{m}_c) = \pm 0.0046\ \text{GeV}\), and the estimated magnitude of N\(^3\)LO contributions from Bayesian analysis. This work demonstrates for the first time how the PMC can be applied to obtain fixed-order perturbative predictions that are invariant under both renormalization and factorization scale variations.

</details>


### [66] [Evaluation of Feynman integrals via numerical integration of differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05336)
*Pau Petit Rosàs*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper presents a new numerical integrator for Feynman integrals based on solving their differential equations, featuring an improved treatment of branch cuts. It achieves fast evaluation (ms to hundreds of ms) of one- and two-loop master integrals in double/quad precision, enabling on-the-fly use in Monte Carlo event generators and efficient grid generation for complex topologies.
\n\n
本文提出了一种基于求解微分方程的新数值积分器用于Feynman积分，其对branch cuts的处理方式有所改进。该方法能以毫秒至数百毫秒的速度在双精度/四精度下计算单圈和双圈master integrals，从而支持在Monte Carlo事件生成器中实时调用，并高效生成复杂拓扑结构的数值网格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing numerical methods for evaluating Feynman integrals—especially those involving multiple scales or higher loops—are often computationally expensive, difficult to parallelize, or suffer from instabilities near branch cuts. The authors aim to overcome these limitations by revisiting the differential equation approach with robust handling of analytic structure, enabling faster and more reliable evaluations suitable for high-energy physics phenomenology.
\n\n
现有的Feynman积分数值计算方法——尤其是涉及多尺度或高圈图的情形——通常计算代价高昂、难以并行化，或在branch cuts附近出现数值不稳定。作者旨在通过重新审视微分方程方法，并稳健处理解析结构（特别是branch cuts），以克服这些限制，从而实现更快、更可靠的积分评估，适用于高能物理唯象学。

Method: The authors numerically integrate the differential equations satisfied by a basis of master integrals. A key innovation is a novel treatment of branch cuts in the complex plane, ensuring correct analytic continuation during integration. The integrator supports both double and quadruple floating-point precision and is designed for efficiency and parallelizability. It avoids precomputed grids for simple topologies and instead evaluates integrals on demand.
\n\n
作者对master integrals基底所满足的微分方程进行数值积分。其关键创新在于对复平面上branch cuts的新颖处理，确保积分过程中解析延拓的正确性。该积分器支持双精度和四精度浮点运算，注重效率与可并行性。对于较简单拓扑，它避免使用预计算网格，而是按需实时计算积分。

Result: The method successfully evaluates one-loop integrals in ~1 ms and two-loop integrals in ~100 ms in double precision. It demonstrates stability across phase space and handles nontrivial analytic structures correctly. The approach drastically reduces computational time compared to existing tools, making it feasible to compute higher-complexity integrals during Monte Carlo integration.
\n\n
该方法成功在约1毫秒内计算单圈积分，在约100毫秒内计算双圈积分（双精度）。它在相空间中表现出良好的数值稳定性，并能正确处理非平凡的解析结构。相比现有工具，该方法显著缩短了计算时间，使得在Monte Carlo积分过程中实时计算更高复杂度的积分成为可能。

Conclusion: The proposed integrator represents a practical advance in the numerical evaluation of Feynman integrals. Its speed, precision, and robustness open new possibilities for automated amplitude computations in collider physics. Future work includes extending the method to more complex multi-scale topologies and integrating it into full Monte Carlo event generators.
\n\n
所提出的积分器在Feynman积分的数值计算方面实现了实用性的进步。其速度、精度和鲁棒性为对撞机物理中的自动化振幅计算开辟了新可能。未来工作包括将该方法推广到更复杂的多尺度拓扑结构，并将其集成到完整的Monte Carlo事件生成器中。

Abstract: We revisit the idea of numerically integrating the differential form of Feynman integrals. With a novel approach for the treatment of branch cuts, we develop an integrator capable of evaluating a basis of master integrals in double and quadruple precision, with significantly smaller run times than other tools. This opens the door to evaluating higher complexity Feynman integrals on the fly in Monte Carlo generators, and enables a cheaper and easy to parallelise generation of grids for the topologies with prohibitive computational times. To show its performance, we test one- and two-loop integral families, achieving evaluation times in double precision of milliseconds and hundreds of milliseconds, respectively. We comment on the results and suggest room for improvement.

</details>


### [67] [Constraints on millicharged particles from thunderstorms on the Solar system planets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05338)
*Ekaterina Dmitrieva,Petr Satunin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores the production of millicharged particles (mCPs) via the Schwinger mechanism in planetary thunderstorms across the Solar System, using observational data to derive stringent constraints on mCP charge and mass. The strongest limits arise from Saturn’s thunderstorms: $q > 10^{-11}$ for fermionic mCPs and $q > 10^{-24}$ for bosonic mCPs—currently the best in the literature.
\n\n
本文研究了太阳系内行星雷暴中通过Schwinger机制产生millicharged particles (mCPs) 的过程，利用卫星任务获得的行星大气观测数据对mCP的电荷和质量施加了严格限制。最强的限制来自土星大气中的雷暴：费米型mCP要求 $q > 10^{-11}$，玻色型mCP要求 $q > 10^{-24}$——据作者所知，这是目前文献中最优的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to probe the existence of millicharged particles (mCPs)—hypothetical particles with tiny electric charges—by leveraging strong electric fields in extraterrestrial thunderstorms, where the Schwinger mechanism can become efficient. Planetary atmospheres, especially those of gas giants like Saturn, offer extreme electromagnetic environments not replicable on Earth, enabling novel astrophysical constraints on mCP properties.
\n\n
动机在于利用地外雷暴中的强电场探测millicharged particles (mCPs)——即具有微小电荷的假想粒子——的存在，因为在这些环境中Schwinger机制可能变得高效。行星大气（尤其是土星等气态巨行星）提供了地球上无法复现的极端电磁环境，从而可对mCP性质施加新的天体物理限制。

Method: The authors compute the Schwinger pair production rate for both fermionic and scalar millicharged particles in the presence of strong electric fields typical of planetary thunderstorms. For scalar mCPs, they include Bose enhancement effects in the production rate. They then use empirical data on electric field strengths and durations from satellite missions (e.g., Cassini for Saturn) to estimate the expected mCP flux and compare it with observational non-detection, thereby deriving lower bounds on the particle charge $q$ as a function of mass.
\n\n
作者计算了在典型行星雷暴强电场下，费米型和标量millicharged particles的Schwinger对产生率；对于标量mCP，他们在产生率中计入了Bose enhancement效应。随后，他们利用卫星任务（如卡西尼号对土星的观测）获得的电场强度和持续时间经验数据，估算预期的mCP通量，并与观测未探测到的结果进行比较，从而导出粒子电荷 $q$ 对质量的下限约束。

Result: The analysis yields the strongest current constraints on millicharged particles: from Saturn’s thunderstorms, they obtain $q > 10^{-11} e$ for fermionic mCPs and an extraordinarily stringent $q > 10^{-24} e$ for bosonic mCPs (where $e$ is the electron charge). These bounds surpass previous laboratory and astrophysical limits by many orders of magnitude for certain mass ranges.
\n\n
分析得出了目前对millicharged particles最强的限制：从土星雷暴中得到费米型mCP的 $q > 10^{-11} e$，以及对玻色型mCP极其严格的 $q > 10^{-24} e$（其中 $e$ 为电子电荷）。在某些质量范围内，这些限制比以往的实验室和天体物理限制高出多个数量级。

Conclusion: Planetary thunderstorms, particularly on Saturn, serve as powerful natural laboratories for probing exotic particle physics via non-perturbative quantum electrodynamics effects like the Schwinger mechanism. The derived constraints significantly advance the search for millicharged particles and demonstrate the potential of multi-messenger planetary science in fundamental physics.
\n\n
行星雷暴（尤其是土星上的）可作为强大的天然实验室，通过Schwinger机制等非微扰量子电动力学效应探测量子新物理。所导出的限制显著推进了对millicharged particles的搜寻，并展示了多信使行星科学在基础物理研究中的潜力。

Abstract: We investigate the production of millicharged particles (mCPs) by the Schwinger mechanism in thunderstorms in the atmospheres of different planets in the Solar system. We study both fermion and scalar mCPs; for scalar mCPs, we take into account the effect of Bose enhancement. We use the observational data of planetary atmospheres obtained by satellite missions to establish constraints on the charge and mass of mCP particles. The best constraints came from the observation of thunderstorms in Saturn's atmosphere: $q > 10^{-11}$ for fermionic mCP and $q > 10^{-24}$ for bosonic mCPs. These constraints are, to the best of our knowledge, the best in the literature.

### [68] [Lepton mixing and charged lepton flavour violation from inverse seesaw with non-degenerate heavy states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05360)
*F. P. Di Meglio,C. Hagedorn*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study an inverse seesaw model with 3+3 gauge singlets, where the flavour structure is governed by Delta(3n^2) or Delta(6n^2) flavour symmetries and CP. The sterile neutrinos form three pseudo-Dirac pairs with distinct masses. Current constraints from charged lepton flavour violation (cLFV) are weak, but future experiments like Mu3E, COMET, and Mu2e will significantly probe the parameter space.
\n\n
我们研究了一个具有3+3规范单态的逆跷跷板模型，其味结构由Delta(3n^2)或Delta(6n^2)味对称性和CP决定。惰性中微子形成三个具有不同质量的准狄拉克对。当前带电轻子味破坏（cLFV）过程的限制较弱，但未来实验如Mu3E、COMET和Mu2e将显著探测该参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to construct a predictive inverse seesaw framework that explains neutrino masses and mixing while being testable via charged lepton flavour violating (cLFV) processes. By imposing discrete flavour symmetries Delta(3n^2) or Delta(6n^2) together with CP, the model reduces arbitrariness in the Yukawa sector and links low-energy observables to high-scale symmetry breaking patterns.
\n\n
本文旨在构建一个可预测的逆跷跷板框架，既能解释中微子质量和混合，又能通过带电轻子味破坏（cLFV）过程进行检验。通过引入离散味对称性Delta(3n^2)或Delta(6n^2)以及CP，该模型减少了Yukawa耦合中的任意性，并将低能观测量与高能对称性破缺模式联系起来。

Method: The authors employ a 3+3 inverse seesaw extension of the Standard Model, where three right-handed neutrinos and three additional gauge singlets are introduced. The Dirac mass matrix of the singlets carries all non-trivial flavour structure dictated by residual symmetries from Delta(3n^2) or Delta(6n^2) and CP. Lepton mixing is derived from the mismatch between residual symmetries in the charged lepton and neutrino sectors. cLFV amplitudes are computed at one-loop level, primarily through dipole and box diagrams involving heavy sterile states, and compared with current and projected experimental sensitivities.
\n\n
作者采用标准模型的3+3逆跷跷板扩展，引入三个右手手中微子和三个额外的规范单态。单态的狄拉克质量矩阵承载了由Delta(3n^2)或Delta(6n^2)及CP的剩余对称性所决定的全部非平凡味结构。轻子混合源于带电轻子与中微子扇区中剩余对称性的不匹配。带电轻子味破坏振幅在单圈水平上计算，主要通过涉及重惰性态的偶极子和盒子图，并与当前及预期的实验灵敏度进行比较。

Result: The model successfully accommodates the observed lepton mixing angles within 3 sigma. The sterile neutrinos form three pseudo-Dirac pairs with generally non-degenerate masses. Current experimental bounds on cLFV processes such as $\\mu \\to e\\gamma$, $\\mu \\to 3e$, $\\tau \\to \\ell\\gamma$, $\\tau \\to 3\\ell$ ($\\ell = e, \\mu$), and $\\mu-e$ conversion in nuclei do not strongly constrain the viable parameter space. However, upcoming experiments—Mu3E, COMET, and Mu2e—are expected to probe significant portions of the model’s predictions.
\n\n
该模型成功在3 sigma范围内拟合了观测到的轻子混合角。惰性中微子形成三个通常质量非简并的准狄拉克对。当前对$\\mu \\to e\\gamma$、$\\mu \\to 3e$、$\\tau \\to \\ell\\gamma$、$\\tau \\to 3\\ell$（$\\ell = e, \\mu$）以及原子核中$\\mu-e$转换等cLFV过程的实验限制并未对可行参数空间构成强约束。然而，即将开展的Mu3E、COMET和Mu2e实验有望探测该模型预测的大部分参数区域。

Conclusion: The inverse seesaw model based on Delta(3n^2) or Delta(6n^2) flavour symmetries and CP provides a viable and predictive framework for neutrino physics. While current cLFV limits are insufficient to rule out the model, next-generation experiments will critically test its parameter space, offering a clear pathway for experimental validation or exclusion.
\n\n
基于Delta(3n^2)或Delta(6n^2)味对称性及CP的逆跷跷板模型为中微子物理提供了一个可行且可预测的框架。尽管当前cLFV限制不足以排除该模型，但下一代实验将对其参数空间进行关键检验，为实验验证或排除提供明确路径。

Abstract: We analyse an inverse seesaw scenario with 3+3 gauge singlets. The flavour structure is determined by a flavour symmetry, Delta (3 n^2) or Delta (6 n^2), n integer, and CP and their residual groups among charged leptons and the neutral states. For the latter, the Dirac mass matrix of the gauge singlets carries all non-trivial flavour structure. Consequently, the heavy sterile states form three pseudo-Dirac pairs which have in general distinct masses. We discuss the signal strength of different charged lepton flavour violating processes. Ensuring that the lepton mixing angles can be accommodated at the 3 sigma level or better, we find that the current bounds on the branching ratios of mu -> e gamma, mu -> 3 e, tau -> l gamma and tau -> 3 l, l=e, mu, as well as the rate of mu-e conversion in nuclei do not strongly constrain the considered parameter space, while the limits expected from the upcoming experiments Mu3E, COMET and Mu2e will have a relevant impact.

### [69] [Connecting Flavor and Baryon Asymmetry via Leptogenesis in Effective Froggatt-Nielsen Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05372)
*Cheshta Batra,Rusa Mandal,Kunal Rawat,Tom Tong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a unified Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) framework that simultaneously explains Standard Model flavor hierarchies, neutrino masses via Type-I seesaw, CP violation in meson decays, dark matter (as the lightest right-handed neutrino), and baryogenesis via leptogenesis. The FN symmetry-breaking scale $v_\\phi$ governs both RHN masses and flavon couplings, enabling successful thermal leptogenesis in both freeze-in and freeze-out dark matter production regimes—requiring resonant enhancement in the latter due to lighter RHNs.
\n\n
本文提出一个统一的Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) 框架，同时解释Standard Model味层次结构、通过Type-I seesaw机制产生的中微子质量、介子衰变中的CP破坏、暗物质（作为最轻的右手中微子）以及通过leptogenesis产生的重子不对称性。FN对称性破缺标度 $v_\\phi$ 同时控制RHN质量和flavon耦合强度，使得在freeze-in和freeze-out两种暗物质产生机制下均能实现成功的热leptogenesis——后者因RHN较轻而需要共振增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Standard Model exhibits unexplained hierarchical patterns in fermion masses and mixing angles across quark and lepton sectors. The Froggatt-Nielsen mechanism offers an elegant origin for these hierarchies via a spontaneously broken $U(1)_{\\rm FN}$ symmetry. However, a complete theory should also address neutrino masses, dark matter, and the baryon asymmetry of the Universe. This work aims to embed all these phenomena—flavor structure, neutrino oscillations, CP violation, DM, and baryogenesis—into a single, predictive FN-based effective field theory, building on prior results where the lightest right-handed neutrino (RHN) serves as a viable DM candidate.
\n\n
Standard Model中费米子质量和混合角在夸克与轻子扇区呈现出无法解释的层级结构。Froggatt-Nielsen机制通过自发破缺的 $U(1)_{\\rm FN}$ 对称性为这些层级提供了优雅的起源。然而，一个完整的理论还应解释中微子质量、暗物质和宇宙重子不对称性。本工作旨在将所有这些现象——味结构、中微子振荡、CP破坏、暗物质和重子生成——嵌入到一个基于FN的、具有预测能力的有效场论中，该工作建立在先前研究基础上，其中最轻的右手中微子（RHN）可作为可行的暗物质候选者。

Method: The authors extend the Froggatt-Nielsen framework by introducing three right-handed neutrinos (RHNs) and a complex flavon field $\\phi$ whose vacuum expectation value $v_\\phi$ breaks $U(1)_{\\rm FN}$. Fermion Yukawa couplings arise from higher-dimensional operators suppressed by powers of $\\langle \\phi \\rangle / \\Lambda$, generating hierarchical masses and mixing. Light neutrino masses are produced via the Type-I seesaw mechanism. CP-violating phases emerge from complex FN charges (or coefficients). The lightest RHN is stable and acts as dark matter, produced via freeze-in or freeze-out depending on $v_\\phi$. Baryogenesis is achieved through thermal leptogenesis: heavier RHNs decay out-of-equilibrium into SM particles and flavons, generating a lepton asymmetry. The authors compute one-loop CP asymmetries $\\epsilon_i$ including flavon-mediated diagrams and solve the full Boltzmann equations incorporating both standard and flavon-induced decay channels.
\n\n
作者通过引入三个右手中微子（RHNs）和一个复标量flavon场 $\\phi$ 来扩展Froggatt-Nielsen框架，其真空期望值 $v_\\phi$ 破缺 $U(1)_{\\rm FN}$ 对称性。费米子Yukawa耦合由高维算符产生，这些算符被 $\\langle \\phi \\rangle / \\Lambda$ 的幂次压低，从而生成层级化的质量和混合。轻中微子质量通过Type-I seesaw机制产生。CP破坏相位来源于复的FN荷（或系数）。最轻的RHN是稳定的，并作为暗物质，其产生机制（freeze-in或freeze-out）取决于 $v_\\phi$。重子生成通过热leptogenesis实现：较重的RHNs在非平衡条件下衰变到SM粒子和flavon，产生轻子不对称性。作者计算了包含flavon介导图的一圈CP不对称参数 $\\epsilon_i$，并求解包含标准衰变道和flavon诱导衰变道的完整Boltzmann方程。

Result: The model successfully accommodates observed quark and lepton flavor structures, including CKM and PMNS mixing matrices with physical CP-violating phases. It predicts viable dark matter in the form of the lightest RHN, with two distinct production regimes: freeze-in at high $v_\\phi$ and freeze-out at lower $v_\\phi$. Crucially, thermal leptogenesis can generate the observed baryon asymmetry in both regimes. In the high-$v_\\phi$ limit, the scenario reduces to standard hierarchical leptogenesis. In the low-$v_\\phi$ (freeze-out) regime, RHN masses are lower ($\\sim$ TeV scale), necessitating resonant leptogenesis via nearly degenerate heavy neutrinos to achieve sufficient CP asymmetry. The flavon-induced decay channels contribute non-negligibly to the total lepton asymmetry.
\n\n
该模型成功容纳了观测到的夸克和轻子味结构，包括具有物理CP破坏相位的CKM和PMNS混合矩阵。它预言最轻RHN作为可行的暗物质，并存在两种不同的产生机制：高 $v_\\phi$ 下的freeze-in和低 $v_\\phi$ 下的freeze-out。关键的是，热leptogenesis在这两种机制下均能产生观测到的重子不对称性。在高 $v_\\phi$ 极限下，该场景退化为标准的层级leptogenesis。在低 $v_\\phi$（freeze-out）区域，RHN质量较低（$\\sim$ TeV量级），需要通过近简并的重中微子实现共振leptogenesis以获得足够的CP不对称性。flavon诱导的衰变道对总轻子不对称性的贡献不可忽略。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that a minimal Froggatt-Nielsen extension of the Standard Model—featuring three RHNs and a flavon—can provide a unified and predictive explanation for flavor hierarchies, neutrino masses, CP violation, dark matter, and the baryon asymmetry of the Universe. The FN symmetry-breaking scale $v_\\phi$ acts as a master parameter linking RHN masses, flavon couplings, DM phenomenology, and leptogenesis efficiency. The framework remains testable: low-scale resonant leptogenesis and TeV-scale RHNs in the freeze-out regime could be probed at colliders and intensity-frontier experiments, while CP-violating observables in meson decays offer complementary constraints.
\n\n
本工作表明，一个包含三个RHNs和一个flavon的Minimal Froggatt-Nielsen扩展模型能够为味层次结构、中微子质量、CP破坏、暗物质和宇宙重子不对称性提供统一且具有预测能力的解释。FN对称性破缺标度 $v_\\phi$ 作为一个主参数，关联了RHN质量、flavon耦合、暗物质现象学和leptogenesis效率。该框架具有可检验性：freeze-out机制下的低能标共振leptogenesis和TeV量级RHNs可在对撞机和强度前沿实验中被探测，而介子衰变中的CP破坏观测量则提供了互补的约束。

Abstract: We investigate the hierarchical flavor structure of the Standard Model in a Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) framework, where the spontaneous breaking of a $U(1)_{\rm FN}$ symmetry by a complex flavon field generates fermion masses and mixing patterns through higher-dimensional operators. Extending the setup with three right-handed neutrinos (RHNs), light neutrino masses arise via the Type-I seesaw mechanism. Allowing complex FN coefficients enables a consistent description of the CKM and PMNS matrices while inducing CP-violating signatures in meson decays. Building on our previous work, where the lightest RHN acts as a viable dark matter (DM) candidate produced through freeze-in or freeze-out mechanisms, we investigate the origin of the baryon asymmetry of the Universe. The heavier RHNs generate a lepton asymmetry through out-of-equilibrium decays, including both Standard Model channels and additional flavon-induced processes in which the flavon appears as an intermediate or final-state particle. We compute the corresponding one-loop CP asymmetries and incorporate these effects in the Boltzmann equations. We show that although freeze-in and freeze-out DM production occur in two qualitatively distinct regions of the FN symmetry-breaking scale $v_φ$, successful thermal leptogenesis can be achieved in both regimes. In the large-$v_φ$ (freeze-in-compatible) region the results approach the standard leptogenesis limit, while in the freeze-out-compatible region the lower value of $v_φ$ implies lighter RHNs, requiring resonant enhancement. This tightly constrained framework, in which $v_φ$ simultaneously controls RHN masses and the interaction strengths of the flavon and DM sectors, provides a predictive and unified description of flavor hierarchies, neutrino masses, CP violation, dark matter, and baryogenesis within a single effective theory.

### [70] [Accelerating Feynman Integral Evaluation by Avoiding Contour Deformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05444)
*Stephen P. Jones,Anton Olsson,Thomas Stone*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper presents a novel method to rewrite dimensionally regulated Feynman parameter integrals in the Minkowski regime as sums of real, positive integrands with complex prefactors, bypassing the need for contour deformation and achieving speedups of up to several orders of magnitude over pySecDec. The approach is generalized to arbitrary Feynman integrals—including those with massive propagators—via an improved resolution procedure using Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition.
\n\n
本文提出了一种新方法，将Minkowski区域中维度正规化的Feynman参数积分重写为实正被积函数与复数前因子的和，从而避免了轮廓变形（contour deformation）的需求，并在性能上比pySecDec实现快达几个数量级。该方法通过使用Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition算法改进的resolution procedure，推广到任意Feynman积分，包括含质量传播子的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Contour deformation in numerical integration of Feynman integrals in the Minkowski regime is computationally expensive and constitutes a major bottleneck. The authors aim to eliminate this step by reformulating the integrals into a form that retains real, positive integration domains while encoding all complex structure in analytic prefactors.
\n\n
在Minkowski区域中对Feynman积分进行数值积分时，轮廓变形（contour deformation）计算代价高昂，是主要瓶颈。作者旨在通过将积分重构为实正积分域的形式，同时将所有复结构编码到解析前因子中，从而消除这一计算步骤。

Method: The method rewrites dimensionally regulated Feynman parameter integrals as a sum over sectors, each consisting of a real, positive integrand multiplied by a complex prefactor derived from the analytic structure of the original integral. This avoids the need for complex contour deformation during numerical integration. The sector decomposition is enhanced using the Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition (GCAD) algorithm, which systematically resolves singularities and generalizes the approach to integrals with massive propagators and arbitrary kinematics.
\n\n
该方法将维度正规化的Feynman参数积分重写为多个sector的和，每个sector由一个实正被积函数与一个源自原积分解析结构的复数前因子相乘构成。这避免了数值积分过程中复杂的轮廓变形。通过Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition（GCAD）算法增强sector decomposition，系统地解析奇点，使该方法可推广至含质量传播子及任意运动学构型的积分。

Result: The authors demonstrate the method on two explicit examples, showing agreement with known results while achieving performance improvements of up to several orders of magnitude compared to contour deformation as implemented in pySecDec. The use of GCAD enables the treatment of previously inaccessible configurations, including those with massive internal lines.
\n\n
作者在两个具体例子上演示了该方法，在结果与已知值一致的同时，相比pySecDec中实现的轮廓变形方法，性能提升高达几个数量级。GCAD的引入使得此前难以处理的构型（如含质量内线的情形）得以计算。

Conclusion: The proposed representation offers a robust, efficient alternative to contour deformation for numerical evaluation of Feynman integrals in the physical Minkowski regime. By leveraging algebraic decomposition techniques like GCAD, the method is universally applicable and significantly accelerates computations critical for high-precision collider physics predictions.
\n\n
所提出的表示法为物理Minkowski区域中Feynman积分的数值计算提供了一种稳健高效的替代方案，无需轮廓变形。通过利用GCAD等代数分解技术，该方法具有普适性，可显著加速高精度对撞机物理预测中的关键计算。

Abstract: We describe our method for rewriting dimensionally regulated Feynman parameter integrals in the Minkowski regime as a sum of real, positive integrands multiplied by complex prefactors. This representation eliminates the need for a contour deformation, which is one of the main computational bottlenecks in numerical integration. We demonstrate clearly how the method works on two examples, and benchmark the performance against contour deformation as implemented in pySecDec, where we observe performance gains of up to several orders of magnitude. We describe an improvement in the resolution procedure using the Generic Cylindrical Algebraic Decomposition algorithm, which generalises our method to any Feynman integral, including those with massive propagators.

</details>
